// ===== app.js =====
require('dotenv').config();

const path = require('path');
const express = require('express');
const session = require('express-session');
const flash = require('connect-flash');
const helmet = require('helmet');
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const methodOverride = require('method-override');
const SQLiteStore = require('./src/middleware/sessionStore');

const db = require('./src/db');
global.categories = db.categories;
const { attachLocals } = require('./src/middleware/locals');
const { createLayoutEngine } = require('./src/views/layoutEngine');
const { csrfProtection } = require('./src/middleware/csrf');
const { requestContext } = require('./src/middleware/requestContext');
const pageRoutes = require('./src/routes/pageRoutes');
const authRoutes = require('./src/routes/authRoutes');
const jobRoutes = require('./src/routes/jobRoutes');
const workerRoutes = require('./src/routes/workerRoutes');
const dashboardRoutes = require('./src/routes/dashboardRoutes');
const adminRoutes = require('./src/routes/adminRoutes');
const reportRoutes = require('./src/routes/reportRoutes');
const messageRoutes = require('./src/routes/messageRoutes');
const businessRoutes = require('./src/routes/businessRoutes');
const promotionRoutes = require('./src/routes/promotionRoutes');
const reviewRoutes = require('./src/routes/reviewRoutes');
const paymentRoutes = require('./src/routes/paymentRoutes');
const disputeRoutes = require('./src/routes/disputeRoutes');
const alertRoutes = require('./src/routes/alertRoutes');
const posterRoutes = require('./src/routes/posterRoutes');
const apiRoutes = require('./src/routes/apiRoutes');
const notificationRoutes = require('./src/routes/notificationRoutes');
const draftRoutes = require('./src/domains/drafts/draftRoutes');
const privateFileRoutes = require('./src/routes/privateFileRoutes');

const app = express();
const port = process.env.PORT || 3000;
const isProduction = process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production';
const sessionSecret = process.env.SESSION_SECRET;
const configuredBaseUrl = String(process.env.BASE_URL || '').trim();

if (isProduction && (!sessionSecret || sessionSecret.length < 32)) {
  throw new Error('SESSION_SECRET must be configured with at least 32 characters in production.');
}
if (isProduction) {
  let parsedBaseUrl;
  try { parsedBaseUrl = new URL(configuredBaseUrl); } catch (_error) { /* handled below */ }
  if (!parsedBaseUrl || parsedBaseUrl.protocol !== 'https:') {
    throw new Error('BASE_URL must be configured as an HTTPS origin in production.');
  }
}
if (process.env.TRUST_PROXY) app.set('trust proxy', process.env.TRUST_PROXY === 'true' ? 1 : process.env.TRUST_PROXY);

db.ensureDb();
app.disable('x-powered-by');
app.set('views', path.join(__dirname, 'views'));
app.engine('ejs', createLayoutEngine({ viewsRoot: app.get('views') }));
app.set('view engine', 'ejs');

const cspDirectives = {
  defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
  scriptSrc: ["'self'", (_req, res) => `'nonce-${res.locals.cspNonce}'`, 'https://cdn.jsdelivr.net'],
  scriptSrcAttr: ["'none'"],
  styleSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'", 'https://cdn.jsdelivr.net', 'https://fonts.googleapis.com'],
  fontSrc: ["'self'", 'data:', 'https://fonts.gstatic.com', 'https://cdn.jsdelivr.net'],
  imgSrc: ["'self'", 'data:', 'blob:'],
  connectSrc: ["'self'", 'https://cdn.jsdelivr.net'],
  objectSrc: ["'none'"],
  baseUri: ["'self'"],
  formAction: ["'self'"],
  frameAncestors: ["'none'"],
};
if (isProduction) cspDirectives.upgradeInsecureRequests = [];

app.use(requestContext);

app.use(helmet({
  contentSecurityPolicy: { directives: cspDirectives },
  crossOriginEmbedderPolicy: false,
}));

app.use(express.static(path.join(__dirname, 'public'), {
  maxAge: isProduction ? '1d' : 0,
  setHeaders: (res, filePath) => {
    if (filePath.endsWith('service-worker.js')) res.setHeader('Cache-Control', 'no-cache, no-store, must-revalidate');
  },
}));

app.use(rateLimit({
  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000,
  limit: 300,
  standardHeaders: true,
  legacyHeaders: false,
  skip: (req) => req.path === '/api/health',
}));

app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true, limit: '1mb' }));
app.use(express.json({ limit: '1mb' }));
app.use(methodOverride('_method'));

app.use(session({
  store: new SQLiteStore(),
  secret: sessionSecret || 'development-only-neighbourtask-session-secret',
  name: 'neighbourtask.sid',
  resave: false,
  saveUninitialized: false,
  rolling: true,
  cookie: {
    httpOnly: true,
    sameSite: 'lax',
    secure: isProduction,
    maxAge: 1000 * 60 * 60 * 24 * 7,
  },
}));

app.use(flash());
app.use(attachLocals);
app.use(csrfProtection);

app.use('/', pageRoutes);
app.use('/auth', authRoutes);
app.use('/jobs', jobRoutes);
app.use('/workers', workerRoutes);
app.use('/dashboard', dashboardRoutes);
app.use('/admin', adminRoutes);
app.use('/reports', reportRoutes);
app.use('/messages', messageRoutes);
app.use('/business', businessRoutes);
app.use('/promotions', promotionRoutes);
app.use('/reviews', reviewRoutes);
app.use('/payments', paymentRoutes);
app.use('/disputes', disputeRoutes);
app.use('/alerts', alertRoutes);
app.use('/notifications', notificationRoutes);
app.use('/posters', posterRoutes);
app.use('/files', privateFileRoutes);
app.use('/drafts', draftRoutes);
app.use('/api', apiRoutes);

app.use((req, res) => {
  if (req.path.startsWith('/api/')) return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Not found.' });
  return res.status(404).render('pages/404', { title: 'Page not found' });
});

app.use((err, req, res, _next) => {
  if (res.headersSent) return req.socket.destroy();
  const conflict = err && err.code === 'DB_CONFLICT';
  const status = conflict ? 409 : 500;
  console.error('[request-error]', {
    requestId: req.requestId,
    method: req.method,
    path: req.path,
    name: err.name,
    code: err.code,
    message: err.message,
  });
  if (req.path.startsWith('/api/')) {
    return res.status(status).json({
      error: conflict ? 'The record changed while you were editing it. Reload and try again.' : 'Internal server error.',
      requestId: req.requestId,
    });
  }
  req.flash('error', conflict
    ? 'That information changed in another request. Reload the page and try again.'
    : 'Something went wrong. Please try again.');
  const isDev = app.get('env') === 'development';
  return res.status(status).render('pages/error', {
    title: conflict ? 'Update conflict' : 'Server error',
    error: isDev ? err : null,
    requestId: req.requestId,
  });
});

let server = null;
let shuttingDown = false;

function startServer() {
  if (server) return server;
  server = app.listen(port, () => {
    console.log(`NeighbourTask running on port ${port}`);
  });
  server.on('error', (err) => {
    if (err.code === 'EADDRINUSE') {
      console.error(`Error: Port ${port} is already in use.`);
      process.exitCode = 1;
      return;
    }
    throw err;
  });
  return server;
}

function shutdown(signal) {
  if (shuttingDown) return;
  shuttingDown = true;
  console.log(`[shutdown] ${signal || 'requested'}`);
  const forceTimer = setTimeout(() => process.exit(1), 10_000);
  forceTimer.unref();

  const finish = () => {
    try { db.checkpoint(); } catch (error) { console.error('[shutdown-checkpoint]', error.message); }
    try { db.getDb().close(); } catch (_error) { /* already closed */ }
    clearTimeout(forceTimer);
    process.exit(0);
  };

  if (!server) return finish();
  server.close(finish);
}

if (require.main === module) {
  startServer();
  process.once('SIGTERM', () => shutdown('SIGTERM'));
  process.once('SIGINT', () => shutdown('SIGINT'));
}

module.exports = app;
module.exports.startServer = startServer;
module.exports.shutdown = shutdown;

  table[data-responsive-table] td::before { content: attr(data-label); color: var(--nt-muted); font-weight: 650; }
}

@media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce) {
  *, *::before, *::after { scroll-behavior: auto !important; transition-duration: .01ms !important; animation-duration: .01ms !important; animation-iteration-count: 1 !important; }
}

// ===== public/js/app.js =====
// Load the shared UX layer even when legacy templates only reference app.js.
(function () {
  if (!document.querySelector('link[data-neighbourtask-design-system]')) {
    const link = document.createElement('link');
    link.rel = 'stylesheet';
    link.href = '/css/design-system.css';
    link.dataset.neighbourtaskDesignSystem = 'true';
    document.head.appendChild(link);
  }
  if (!document.querySelector('script[data-neighbourtask-ux]')) {
    const script = document.createElement('script');
    script.src = '/js/ux.js';
    script.defer = true;
    script.dataset.neighbourtaskUx = 'true';
    document.head.appendChild(script);
  }
})();

(function () {
  const description = document.querySelector('textarea[name="description"]');
  const title = document.querySelector('input[name="title"]');
  const warningBox = document.createElement('div');
  warningBox.className = 'alert alert-warning mt-3 d-none';

  function scanText() {
    if (!description && !title) return;
    const form = (description || title).closest('form');
    if (!form) return;
    if (!warningBox.parentNode) form.appendChild(warningBox);

    const text = `${title ? title.value : ''} ${description ? description.value : ''}`.toLowerCase();
    const terms = ['electrical', 'gas', 'hvac', 'refrigerant', 'roof', 'ladder', 'plumbing', 'asbestos', 'mould', 'concrete drilling', 'under the table'];
    const matches = terms.filter((term) => text.includes(term));

    if (matches.length) {
      warningBox.classList.remove('d-none');
      warningBox.innerHTML = `<strong>Heads up:</strong> this post mentions ${matches.join(', ')}. The server will run a full risk scan and may require admin review.`;
    } else {
      warningBox.classList.add('d-none');
    }
  }

  if (description) description.addEventListener('input', scanText);
  if (title) title.addEventListener('input', scanText);
})();

// Client-side quote form validation
(function () {
  document.addEventListener('submit', function (e) {
    var form = e.target;
    if (!form.classList.contains('quote-form')) return;

    var valid = true;
    var firstInvalid = null;

    var email = form.querySelector('input[name="email"]');
    var phone = form.querySelector('input[name="phone"]');
    if (email || phone) {
      if ((!email || !email.value.trim()) && (!phone || !phone.value.trim())) {
        if (email) email.classList.add('is-invalid');
        if (phone) phone.classList.add('is-invalid');
        valid = false;
        firstInvalid = firstInvalid || email || phone;
      }
    }

    var amount = form.querySelector('input[name="amount"]');
    if (amount) {
      var val = parseFloat(amount.value);
      if (!amount.value.trim() || isNaN(val) || val <= 0) {
        amount.classList.add('is-invalid');
        valid = false;
        firstInvalid = firstInvalid || amount;
      }
    }

    var estHours = form.querySelector('input[name="estimatedHours"]');
    var quoteType = form.querySelector('select[name="quoteType"]');
    if (quoteType && quoteType.value === 'hourly' && estHours) {
      var hv = parseFloat(estHours.value);
      if (!estHours.value.trim() || isNaN(hv) || hv <= 0) {
        estHours.classList.add('is-invalid');
        valid = false;
        firstInvalid = firstInvalid || estHours;
      }
    }

    var compliance = form.querySelector('#workerCompliance');
    if (compliance && !compliance.checked) {
      compliance.classList.add('is-invalid');
      valid = false;
      firstInvalid = firstInvalid || compliance;
    }

    if (!valid) {
      e.preventDefault();
      if (firstInvalid) firstInvalid.focus();
    }
  });

  document.addEventListener('input', function (e) {
    if (e.target.closest('.quote-form')) {
      e.target.classList.remove('is-invalid');
    }
  });

  document.addEventListener('change', function (e) {
    if (e.target.closest('.quote-form')) {
      e.target.classList.remove('is-invalid');
    }
  });
})();

// Client-side file size validation
(function () {
  document.addEventListener('submit', function (e) {
    const form = e.target;
    const fileInputs = form.querySelectorAll('input[type="file"][data-max-size]');
    let tooLarge = [];

    fileInputs.forEach(function (input) {
      const maxMb = parseFloat(input.getAttribute('data-max-size'));
      if (!maxMb) return;
      const maxBytes = maxMb * 1024 * 1024;
      for (let i = 0; i < input.files.length; i++) {
        if (input.files[i].size > maxBytes) {
          tooLarge.push(input.files[i].name + ' (' + (input.files[i].size / 1024 / 1024).toFixed(1) + ' MB)');
        }
      }
    });

    if (tooLarge.length) {
      e.preventDefault();
      alert('The following files exceed the ' + fileInputs[0].getAttribute('data-max-size') + ' MB limit:\n\n' + tooLarge.join('\n'));
    }
  });
})();


// Ensure every browser form submits the session CSRF token, including multipart forms.
(function () {
  function readCookie(name) {
    const prefix = `${encodeURIComponent(name)}=`;
    const part = document.cookie.split('; ').find((item) => item.startsWith(prefix));
    return part ? decodeURIComponent(part.slice(prefix.length)) : '';
  }

  function attachToken(form) {
    if (!form || String(form.method || 'get').toLowerCase() === 'get') return;
    if (form.querySelector('input[name="_csrf"]')) return;
    const token = readCookie('XSRF-TOKEN');
    if (!token) return;
    const input = document.createElement('input');
    input.type = 'hidden';
    input.name = '_csrf';
    input.value = token;
    form.appendChild(input);
  }

  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
    document.querySelectorAll('form').forEach(attachToken);
  });
  document.addEventListener('submit', function (event) {
    attachToken(event.target);
  }, true);
})();

// ===== public/js/paste-upload.js =====
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
  const fileInput = document.querySelector('input[name="photos"]');
  if (!fileInput) return;

  const MAX_FILE_SIZE = 5 * 1024 * 1024;
  const MAX_FILES = 6;
  const ALLOWED_TYPES = new Set(['image/jpeg', 'image/png', 'image/webp', 'image/gif', 'application/pdf']);
  const parent = fileInput.parentNode;
  let selectedFiles = [];

  const errorContainer = document.createElement('div');
  errorContainer.id = 'file-error-container';
  errorContainer.className = 'alert alert-danger d-none mt-2 mb-0 py-2 small';
  errorContainer.setAttribute('role', 'alert');
  errorContainer.setAttribute('aria-live', 'polite');
  parent.appendChild(errorContainer);

  const pasteHint = document.createElement('div');
  pasteHint.className = 'small text-muted mt-2 d-flex align-items-center gap-1';
  pasteHint.innerHTML = '<i class="bi bi-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"></i> <span>Tip: paste images with <strong>Ctrl+V</strong>, or drag files here. Maximum 6 files and 5 MB per file.</span>';
  parent.appendChild(pasteHint);

  const previewContainer = document.createElement('div');
  previewContainer.id = 'photo-preview-container';
  previewContainer.className = 'row g-2 mt-3';
  previewContainer.setAttribute('aria-live', 'polite');
  parent.appendChild(previewContainer);

  function showError(message) {
    errorContainer.textContent = message;
    errorContainer.classList.remove('d-none');
  }

  function clearError() {
    errorContainer.classList.add('d-none');
    errorContainer.textContent = '';
  }

  function fileKey(file) {
    return [file.name, file.size, file.type, file.lastModified || 0].join(':');
  }

  function synchronizeInput() {
    if (typeof DataTransfer === 'undefined') {
      showError('This browser cannot combine pasted or dropped files. Use the file picker instead.');
      return false;
    }
    const transfer = new DataTransfer();
    selectedFiles.forEach((file) => transfer.items.add(file));
    try {
      fileInput.files = transfer.files;
      return true;
    } catch (_error) {
      showError('This browser cannot update the selected file list. Use the file picker instead.');
      return false;
    }
  }

  function renderPreviews() {
    previewContainer.replaceChildren();

    selectedFiles.forEach((file, index) => {
      const col = document.createElement('div');
      col.className = 'col-6 col-sm-4 col-md-3';

      const card = document.createElement('div');
      card.className = 'card border h-100 position-relative p-2 bg-light shadow-sm';
      card.style.minHeight = '120px';
      card.style.display = 'flex';
      card.style.flexDirection = 'column';
      card.style.alignItems = 'center';
      card.style.justifyContent = 'center';

      const deleteButton = document.createElement('button');
      deleteButton.type = 'button';
      deleteButton.className = 'btn btn-danger btn-sm position-absolute top-0 end-0 m-1 p-0 d-flex align-items-center justify-content-center rounded-circle';
      deleteButton.style.width = '24px';
      deleteButton.style.height = '24px';
      deleteButton.style.zIndex = '10';
      deleteButton.setAttribute('aria-label', `Remove ${file.name}`);
      deleteButton.innerHTML = '<i class="bi bi-x fs-6" aria-hidden="true" style="line-height:1;"></i>';
      deleteButton.addEventListener('click', function () {
        selectedFiles.splice(index, 1);
        clearError();
        synchronizeInput();
        renderPreviews();
      });
      card.appendChild(deleteButton);

      if (file.type.startsWith('image/')) {
        const image = document.createElement('img');
        const objectUrl = URL.createObjectURL(file);
        image.src = objectUrl;
        image.alt = `Preview of ${file.name}`;
        image.className = 'img-thumbnail rounded-3 w-100';
        image.style.height = '100px';
        image.style.objectFit = 'cover';
        image.addEventListener('load', () => URL.revokeObjectURL(objectUrl), { once: true });
        image.addEventListener('error', () => URL.revokeObjectURL(objectUrl), { once: true });
        card.appendChild(image);
      } else {
        const icon = document.createElement('div');
        icon.className = 'text-center my-2 text-primary';
        icon.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
        icon.innerHTML = file.type === 'application/pdf'
          ? '<i class="bi bi-file-earmark-pdf fs-1 text-danger"></i>'
          : '<i class="bi bi-file-earmark fs-1 text-secondary"></i>';
        card.appendChild(icon);
      }

      const label = document.createElement('div');
      label.className = 'text-truncate w-100 text-center small mt-1 text-muted';
      label.style.fontSize = '0.75rem';
      label.textContent = file.name;
      label.title = file.name;
      card.appendChild(label);

      col.appendChild(card);
      previewContainer.appendChild(col);
    });
  }

  function addFiles(fileList) {
    clearError();
    const errors = [];
    const existingKeys = new Set(selectedFiles.map(fileKey));

    for (const file of Array.from(fileList || [])) {
      if (selectedFiles.length >= MAX_FILES) {
        errors.push(`Only ${MAX_FILES} files can be uploaded.`);
        break;
      }
      if (!ALLOWED_TYPES.has(file.type)) {
        errors.push(`${file.name} is not an allowed image or PDF.`);
        continue;
      }
      if (file.size > MAX_FILE_SIZE) {
        errors.push(`${file.name} exceeds 5 MB.`);
        continue;
      }
      const key = fileKey(file);
      if (existingKeys.has(key)) continue;
      existingKeys.add(key);
      selectedFiles.push(file);
    }

    synchronizeInput();
    renderPreviews();
    if (errors.length) showError([...new Set(errors)].join(' '));
  }

  fileInput.addEventListener('change', function () {
    const pickedFiles = Array.from(fileInput.files || []);
    addFiles(pickedFiles);
  });

  window.addEventListener('paste', function (event) {
    const clipboard = event.clipboardData;
    if (!clipboard) return;
    const pastedFiles = Array.from(clipboard.items || [])
      .filter((item) => item.kind === 'file' && item.type.startsWith('image/'))
      .map((item, index) => {
        const blob = item.getAsFile();
        if (!blob) return null;
        const extension = (blob.type.split('/')[1] || 'png').replace(/[^a-z0-9]/gi, '');
        const timestamp = new Date().toISOString().replace(/T/, '_').replace(/\..+/, '').replace(/:/g, '-');
        return new File([blob], `pasted-image-${timestamp}-${index}.${extension}`, {
          type: blob.type,
          lastModified: Date.now(),
        });
      })
      .filter(Boolean);

    if (!pastedFiles.length) return;
    event.preventDefault();
    addFiles(pastedFiles);
    previewContainer.animate(
      [{ backgroundColor: 'rgba(80, 70, 229, 0.15)' }, { backgroundColor: 'transparent' }],
      { duration: 500 },
    );
  });

  const dropZone = fileInput.closest('.mb-3') || fileInput.closest('.col-12');
  if (dropZone) {
    dropZone.style.border = '2px dashed transparent';
    dropZone.style.borderRadius = 'var(--radius-md)';
    dropZone.style.padding = '10px';
    dropZone.style.transition = 'all 0.3s';

    dropZone.addEventListener('dragover', function (event) {
      event.preventDefault();
      dropZone.style.borderColor = 'var(--brand)';
      dropZone.style.backgroundColor = 'rgba(80, 70, 229, 0.05)';
    });

    dropZone.addEventListener('dragleave', function () {
      dropZone.style.borderColor = 'transparent';
      dropZone.style.backgroundColor = 'transparent';
    });

    dropZone.addEventListener('drop', function (event) {
      event.preventDefault();
      dropZone.style.borderColor = 'transparent';
      dropZone.style.backgroundColor = 'transparent';
      addFiles(event.dataTransfer ? event.dataTransfer.files : []);
    });
  }
});

// ===== public/js/pwa.js =====
let deferredInstallPrompt = null;
let serviceWorkerRegistration = null;
let refreshingForUpdate = false;

function showUpdatePrompt(registration) {
  if (!registration || !registration.waiting || document.getElementById('appUpdatePrompt')) return;

  const prompt = document.createElement('div');
  prompt.id = 'appUpdatePrompt';
  prompt.className = 'position-fixed bottom-0 start-50 translate-middle-x mb-3 alert alert-dark shadow d-flex align-items-center gap-3';
  prompt.style.zIndex = '1080';
  prompt.setAttribute('role', 'status');
  prompt.innerHTML = [
    '<span>A new version of NeighbourTask is available.</span>',
    '<button type="button" class="btn btn-light btn-sm" data-action="update-app">Update</button>',
    '<button type="button" class="btn-close btn-close-white" aria-label="Dismiss update"></button>',
  ].join('');

  prompt.querySelector('[data-action="update-app"]').addEventListener('click', () => {
    registration.waiting.postMessage('SKIP_WAITING');
  });
  prompt.querySelector('.btn-close').addEventListener('click', () => prompt.remove());
  document.body.appendChild(prompt);
}

if ('serviceWorker' in navigator) {
  window.addEventListener('load', async () => {
    try {
      serviceWorkerRegistration = await navigator.serviceWorker.register('/service-worker.js');
      if (serviceWorkerRegistration.waiting) showUpdatePrompt(serviceWorkerRegistration);

      serviceWorkerRegistration.addEventListener('updatefound', () => {
        const installing = serviceWorkerRegistration.installing;
        if (!installing) return;
        installing.addEventListener('statechange', () => {
          if (installing.state === 'installed' && navigator.serviceWorker.controller) {
            showUpdatePrompt(serviceWorkerRegistration);
          }
        });
      });
    } catch (error) {
      console.warn('Service worker registration failed', error);
    }
  });

  navigator.serviceWorker.addEventListener('controllerchange', () => {
    if (refreshingForUpdate) return;
    refreshingForUpdate = true;
    window.location.reload();
  });
}

window.addEventListener('beforeinstallprompt', (event) => {
  event.preventDefault();
  deferredInstallPrompt = event;
  const installButton = document.getElementById('installAppBtn');
  if (installButton) installButton.classList.remove('d-none');
});

window.addEventListener('appinstalled', () => {
  deferredInstallPrompt = null;
  const installButton = document.getElementById('installAppBtn');
  if (installButton) installButton.classList.add('d-none');
});

document.addEventListener('click', async (event) => {
  const installButton = event.target.closest('#installAppBtn');
  if (!installButton) return;
  if (!deferredInstallPrompt) {
    installButton.textContent = 'Use your browser menu to install';
    return;
  }
  deferredInstallPrompt.prompt();
  await deferredInstallPrompt.userChoice;
  deferredInstallPrompt = null;
});

// ===== public/js/ux.js =====
(function () {
  const SENSITIVE_NAMES = /password|token|secret|csrf|card|account|routing|sin|ssn/i;
  const DRAFT_MAX_AGE = 1000 * 60 * 60 * 24 * 14;
  const authenticated = document.documentElement.dataset.authenticated === 'true';

  function readCookie(name) {
    const prefix = `${encodeURIComponent(name)}=`;
    const part = document.cookie.split('; ').find((item) => item.startsWith(prefix));
    return part ? decodeURIComponent(part.slice(prefix.length)) : '';
  }

  function localKey(form, kind) {
    return `neighbourtask:draft:${kind}:${form.id || form.getAttribute('name') || 'form'}`;
  }

  function draftKind(form) {
    const explicit = String(form.dataset.draftKind || '').trim().toLowerCase();
    const raw = explicit || `${location.pathname}:${form.id || form.getAttribute('name') || 'form'}`;
    return raw.replace(/[^a-z0-9:_-]+/gi, '-').replace(/^-+|-+$/g, '').slice(0, 80) || 'form';
  }

  function autosaveEligible(form) {
    if (form.dataset.autosave === 'false' || String(form.method || 'get').toLowerCase() === 'get') return false;
    if (form.dataset.autosave === 'true') return true;
    return /^\/(jobs\/(new|quick)|workers\/profile|posters\/profile|disputes|business)/.test(location.pathname);
  }

  function serializeForm(form) {
    const values = {};
    for (const element of form.elements) {
      if (!element.name || element.disabled || SENSITIVE_NAMES.test(element.name) || ['file', 'submit', 'button', 'reset'].includes(element.type)) continue;
      if ((element.type === 'checkbox' || element.type === 'radio') && !element.checked) continue;
      if (element.type === 'select-multiple') values[element.name] = [...element.selectedOptions].map((option) => option.value);
      else values[element.name] = element.value;
    }
    return { savedAt: new Date().toISOString(), values };
  }

  function restoreForm(form, draft) {
    for (const [name, value] of Object.entries(draft.values || {})) {
      const fields = form.querySelectorAll(`[name="${CSS.escape(name)}"]`);
      fields.forEach((field) => {
        if (field.type === 'checkbox' || field.type === 'radio') {
          field.checked = Array.isArray(value) ? value.includes(field.value) : String(field.value) === String(value);
        } else if (field.type === 'select-multiple' && Array.isArray(value)) {
          [...field.options].forEach((option) => { option.selected = value.includes(option.value); });
        } else {
          field.value = value;
        }
        field.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', { bubbles: true }));
        field.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', { bubbles: true }));
      });
    }
  }

  function button(label, tone, attribute) {
    const element = document.createElement('button');
    element.type = 'button';
    element.className = `nt-button nt-button--${tone}`;
    element.textContent = label;
    element.dataset[attribute] = 'true';
    return element;
  }

  function showDraftBanner(form, draft, onRestore, onDiscard) {
    if (!draft || !Object.keys(draft.values || {}).length || document.querySelector('[data-draft-banner]')) return;
    const banner = document.createElement('aside');
    banner.className = 'nt-draft-banner';
    banner.dataset.draftBanner = 'true';
    banner.setAttribute('role', 'status');

    const heading = document.createElement('strong');
    heading.textContent = 'Restore your saved draft?';
    const copy = document.createElement('p');
    const savedDate = draft.savedAt ? new Date(draft.savedAt) : null;
    copy.textContent = savedDate && !Number.isNaN(savedDate.getTime())
      ? `Unfinished changes were saved ${savedDate.toLocaleString()}.`
      : 'Unfinished changes were saved.';
    const actions = document.createElement('div');
    actions.className = 'nt-cluster';
    const restore = button('Restore', 'primary', 'restore');
    const discard = button('Discard', 'secondary', 'discard');
    actions.append(restore, discard);
    banner.append(heading, copy, actions);
    restore.addEventListener('click', () => { restoreForm(form, draft); banner.remove(); onRestore(); });
    discard.addEventListener('click', () => { banner.remove(); onDiscard(); });
    document.body.appendChild(banner);
  }

  function localDraft(key) {
    try {
      const saved = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(key) || 'null');
      if (!saved) return null;
      const age = Date.now() - new Date(saved.savedAt || 0).getTime();
      if (age >= 0 && age < DRAFT_MAX_AGE) return saved;
      localStorage.removeItem(key);
    } catch (_error) {
      localStorage.removeItem(key);
    }
    return null;
  }

  async function serverDraft(kind) {
    if (!authenticated) return null;
    try {
      const response = await fetch(`/drafts/${encodeURIComponent(kind)}`, { headers: { Accept: 'application/json' }, credentials: 'same-origin' });
      if (!response.ok) return null;
      const result = await response.json();
      return result.draft ? { savedAt: result.draft.savedAt, values: result.draft.values || {} } : null;
    } catch (_error) {
      return null;
    }
  }

  async function saveServerDraft(kind, draft) {
    if (!authenticated) return false;
    try {
      const response = await fetch(`/drafts/${encodeURIComponent(kind)}`, {
        method: 'PUT',
        credentials: 'same-origin',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', Accept: 'application/json', 'X-CSRF-Token': readCookie('XSRF-TOKEN') },
        body: JSON.stringify({ route: location.pathname, values: draft.values }),
      });
      return response.ok;
    } catch (_error) {
      return false;
    }
  }

  async function deleteServerDraft(kind) {
    if (!authenticated) return;
    try {
      await fetch(`/drafts/${encodeURIComponent(kind)}`, {
        method: 'DELETE', credentials: 'same-origin', headers: { Accept: 'application/json', 'X-CSRF-Token': readCookie('XSRF-TOKEN') },
      });
    } catch (_error) { /* local cleanup still succeeds */ }
  }

  function draftState(form) {
    let state = form.querySelector('[data-draft-state]');
    if (!state) {
      state = document.createElement('span');
      state.className = 'nt-draft-state';
      state.dataset.draftState = 'true';
      state.setAttribute('role', 'status');
      const submit = form.querySelector('[type="submit"]');
      if (submit && submit.parentNode) submit.parentNode.insertBefore(state, submit.nextSibling);
      else form.appendChild(state);
    }
    return state;
  }

  async function enhanceAutosave(form) {
    if (!autosaveEligible(form)) return;
    const kind = draftKind(form);
    const key = localKey(form, kind);
    const indicator = draftState(form);
    let dirty = false;
    let timer;
    let saveSequence = 0;

    const remote = await serverDraft(kind);
    const local = localDraft(key);
    const remoteTime = remote ? new Date(remote.savedAt || 0).getTime() : 0;
    const localTime = local ? new Date(local.savedAt || 0).getTime() : 0;
    const saved = remoteTime >= localTime ? remote : local;
    if (saved) {
      showDraftBanner(form, saved, () => { dirty = true; }, async () => {
        localStorage.removeItem(key);
        await deleteServerDraft(kind);
      });
    }

    async function persist() {
      const sequence = ++saveSequence;
      const draft = serializeForm(form);
      indicator.textContent = 'Saving draft…';
      const savedRemotely = await saveServerDraft(kind, draft);
      if (!savedRemotely) {
        try { localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(draft)); } catch (_error) { /* storage may be disabled */ }
      } else {
        localStorage.removeItem(key);
      }
      if (sequence === saveSequence) indicator.textContent = savedRemotely ? 'Draft saved' : 'Draft saved on this device';
    }

    form.addEventListener('input', () => {
      dirty = true;
      clearTimeout(timer);
      timer = setTimeout(persist, 700);
    });
    form.addEventListener('submit', () => {
      dirty = false;
      clearTimeout(timer);
      localStorage.removeItem(key);
      deleteServerDraft(kind);
    });
    window.addEventListener('beforeunload', (event) => {
      if (!dirty) return;
      event.preventDefault();
      event.returnValue = '';
    });
  }

  function enhanceForm(form) {
    enhanceAutosave(form);
    form.addEventListener('submit', (event) => {
      if (!form.checkValidity()) {
        event.preventDefault();
        form.classList.add('was-validated');
        const first = form.querySelector(':invalid');
        if (first) first.focus();
        return;
      }
      const submitters = form.querySelectorAll('[type="submit"]');
      submitters.forEach((submitter) => {
        submitter.disabled = true;
        submitter.dataset.submitting = 'true';
        const label = submitter.querySelector('[data-button-label]');
        const replacement = submitter.dataset.loadingLabel || 'Working…';
        if (label) label.textContent = replacement;
        else submitter.textContent = replacement;
      });
      form.setAttribute('aria-busy', 'true');
    });
  }

  function enhanceTables() {
    document.querySelectorAll('table').forEach((table) => {
      table.dataset.responsiveTable = 'true';
      const headers = [...table.querySelectorAll('thead th')].map((header) => header.textContent.trim());
      table.querySelectorAll('tbody tr').forEach((row) => {
        [...row.children].forEach((cell, index) => { if (!cell.dataset.label) cell.dataset.label = headers[index] || ''; });
      });
      if (!table.parentElement.classList.contains('table-responsive')) {
        const wrapper = document.createElement('div');
        wrapper.className = 'table-responsive';
        table.parentNode.insertBefore(wrapper, table);
        wrapper.appendChild(table);
      }
    });
  }

  function enhanceStatusBadges() {
    document.querySelectorAll('[data-status], .badge').forEach((element) => {
      const status = String(element.dataset.status || element.textContent || '').trim().toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, '-');
      if (!status) return;
      element.classList.add('nt-status');
      if (/(complete|accept|verified|active|released|resolved|paid)/.test(status)) element.classList.add('nt-status--success');
      else if (/(review|pending|request|shortlist|invoice)/.test(status)) element.classList.add('nt-status--warning');
      else if (/(remove|reject|suspend|cancel|decline|expire)/.test(status)) element.classList.add('nt-status--danger');
      else if (/(open|submitted|hired)/.test(status)) element.classList.add('nt-status--info');
      else element.classList.add('nt-status--neutral');
    });
  }

  function enhanceNavigation() {
    const toggle = document.querySelector('[data-nav-toggle]');
    const nav = document.querySelector('[data-navigation]');
    if (!toggle || !nav) return;
    toggle.addEventListener('click', () => {
      const open = toggle.getAttribute('aria-expanded') !== 'true';
      toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', String(open));
      nav.classList.toggle('is-open', open);
    });
    document.addEventListener('keydown', (event) => {
      if (event.key === 'Escape' && nav.classList.contains('is-open')) {
        nav.classList.remove('is-open');
        toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
        toggle.focus();
      }
    });
  }

  function enhanceAlerts() {
    document.querySelectorAll('[data-dismiss-alert]').forEach((button) => button.addEventListener('click', () => button.closest('.nt-alert')?.remove()));
    const errorSummary = document.querySelector('[data-error-summary]');
    if (errorSummary) errorSummary.focus();
  }

  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    document.querySelectorAll('form').forEach(enhanceForm);
    enhanceTables();
    enhanceStatusBadges();
    enhanceNavigation();
    enhanceAlerts();
  });
})();

    { "src": "/icons/icon-192.png", "sizes": "192x192", "type": "image/png", "purpose": "any maskable" },
    { "src": "/icons/icon-512.png", "sizes": "512x512", "type": "image/png", "purpose": "any maskable" }
  ],

    { "name": "Post with camera", "short_name": "Post", "url": "/mobile/post", "description": "Create a photo-first task listing" },
    { "name": "Browse jobs", "short_name": "Jobs", "url": "/jobs", "description": "Find open odd jobs" },
    { "name": "Messages", "short_name": "Messages", "url": "/messages", "description": "Open message threads" },
    { "name": "Job alerts", "short_name": "Alerts", "url": "/alerts", "description": "Manage saved job alerts" }
  ]
}

// ===== public/service-worker.js =====
const CACHE_NAME = 'neighbourtask-static-v8';
const STATIC_ASSETS = [
  '/css/styles.css',
  '/css/design-system.css',
  '/js/app.js',
  '/js/ux.js',
  '/js/pwa.js',
  '/js/paste-upload.js',
  '/manifest.json',
  '/icons/icon-192.png',
];

self.addEventListener('install', (event) => {
  event.waitUntil(
    caches.open(CACHE_NAME).then((cache) => Promise.all(
      STATIC_ASSETS.map((asset) => cache.add(asset).catch(() => undefined)),
    )),
  );
  self.skipWaiting();
});

self.addEventListener('activate', (event) => {
  event.waitUntil(
    caches.keys().then((keys) => Promise.all(
      keys.filter((key) => key !== CACHE_NAME).map((key) => caches.delete(key)),
    )),
  );
  self.clients.claim();
});

function offlineJson() {
  return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: 'You appear to be offline.' }), {
    status: 503,
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Cache-Control': 'no-store' },
  });
}

function offlinePage() {
  return new Response(
    '<!doctype html><html><head><meta charset="utf-8"><meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width"><title>Offline</title></head><body><main><h1>You are offline</h1><p>Reconnect and reload to continue using NeighbourTask.</p></main></body></html>',
    { status: 503, headers: { 'Content-Type': 'text/html; charset=utf-8', 'Cache-Control': 'no-store' } },
  );
}

self.addEventListener('fetch', (event) => {
  const request = event.request;
  if (request.method !== 'GET') return;
  const url = new URL(request.url);
  if (url.origin !== self.location.origin) return;

  if (url.pathname.startsWith('/api/')) {
    event.respondWith(fetch(request).catch(offlineJson));
    return;
  }

  if (request.mode === 'navigate') {
    event.respondWith(fetch(request).catch(offlinePage));
    return;
  }

  const isStatic = url.pathname.startsWith('/css/')
    || url.pathname.startsWith('/js/')
    || url.pathname.startsWith('/icons/')
    || url.pathname === '/manifest.json';
  if (!isStatic) return;

  event.respondWith(
    caches.match(request).then((cached) => cached || fetch(request).then((response) => {
      if (response.ok && response.type === 'basic') {
        const copy = response.clone();
        caches.open(CACHE_NAME).then((cache) => cache.put(request, copy));
      }
      return response;
    })),
  );
});

self.addEventListener('push', (event) => {
  let payload = { title: 'NeighbourTask', body: 'You have a new update.', url: '/notifications' };
  try {
    if (event.data) payload = { ...payload, ...event.data.json() };
  } catch (_error) {
    if (event.data) payload.body = event.data.text();
  }
  event.waitUntil(self.registration.showNotification(payload.title || 'NeighbourTask', {
    body: payload.body || 'You have a new update.',
    icon: '/icons/icon-192.png',
    badge: '/icons/icon-192.png',
    data: { url: payload.url || '/notifications' },
  }));
});

self.addEventListener('notificationclick', (event) => {
  event.notification.close();
  const candidate = new URL(event.notification.data?.url || '/notifications', self.location.origin);
  const targetUrl = candidate.origin === self.location.origin
    ? candidate.href
    : new URL('/notifications', self.location.origin).href;
  event.waitUntil(self.clients.matchAll({ type: 'window', includeUncontrolled: true }).then(async (clients) => {
    const existing = clients.find((client) => new URL(client.url).origin === self.location.origin);
    if (existing) {
      await existing.navigate(targetUrl);
      return existing.focus();
    }
    return self.clients.openWindow(targetUrl);
  }));
});

self.addEventListener('message', (event) => {
  if (event.data === 'SKIP_WAITING') self.skipWaiting();
});

// ===== scripts/backup-db.js =====
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');
const db = require('../src/db');

function timestamp() {
  return new Date().toISOString().replace(/[:.]/g, '-');
}

async function run() {
  db.ensureDb();
  const backupDir = path.resolve(process.env.BACKUP_DIR || path.join(path.dirname(db.dbPath), 'backups'));
  const keep = Math.max(1, Math.min(Number(process.env.BACKUP_RETENTION || 14), 365));
  fs.mkdirSync(backupDir, { recursive: true, mode: 0o700 });
  const destination = path.join(backupDir, `neighbourtask-${timestamp()}.sqlite`);

  db.checkpoint();
  await db.getDb().backup(destination);
  fs.chmodSync(destination, 0o600);

  const backups = fs.readdirSync(backupDir)
    .filter((name) => /^neighbourtask-.*\.sqlite$/.test(name))
    .map((name) => ({ name, path: path.join(backupDir, name), mtime: fs.statSync(path.join(backupDir, name)).mtimeMs }))
    .sort((a, b) => b.mtime - a.mtime);
  for (const old of backups.slice(keep)) fs.unlinkSync(old.path);

  console.log(`Backup created: ${destination}`);
  console.log(`Retention: newest ${keep} backup(s).`);
}

run().catch((error) => {
  console.error('Backup failed:', error.message);
  process.exit(1);
});

// ===== scripts/clean.js =====
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');
const db = require('../src/db');
const { TABLES } = require('../src/db/relational');

if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production') {
  console.error('Refusing to clean data in production.');
  process.exit(1);
}
if (!process.argv.includes('--confirm')) {
  console.error('Usage: node scripts/clean.js --confirm');
  process.exit(1);
}

if (fs.existsSync(db.dbPath)) {
  const backupDir = path.join(path.dirname(db.dbPath), 'backups');
  fs.mkdirSync(backupDir, { recursive: true });
  const backupPath = path.join(backupDir, `db-before-clean-${new Date().toISOString().replace(/[:.]/g, '-')}.sqlite`);
  fs.copyFileSync(db.dbPath, backupPath);
  console.log(`Backup created: ${backupPath}`);
}

db.ensureDb();
db.checkpoint();
const sqlite = db.getDb();

const keepEmails = ['admin@neighbourtask.local', 'poster@example.com', 'worker@example.com'];
const keptUsers = sqlite.prepare(`SELECT id FROM core_users WHERE email IN (${keepEmails.map(() => '?').join(',')})`).all(...keepEmails);
const keptUserIds = new Set(keptUsers.map((row) => row.id));

const transaction = sqlite.transaction(() => {
  for (const [name, tableName] of Object.entries(TABLES)) {
    if (name === 'users') {
      const idsToDelete = sqlite.prepare(`SELECT id FROM ${tableName} WHERE id NOT IN (${keptUsers.map(() => '?').join(',')})`).all(...keptUsers.map((u) => u.id));
      for (const row of idsToDelete) {
        sqlite.prepare(`DELETE FROM ${tableName} WHERE id = ?`).run(row.id);
      }
    } else if (name === 'workerProfiles' || name === 'posterProfiles') {
      sqlite.prepare(`DELETE FROM ${tableName}`).run();
    } else {
      sqlite.prepare(`DELETE FROM ${tableName}`).run();
    }
  }
});
transaction.immediate();

console.log('Cleared sample data. Kept users:', [...keptUserIds].join(', '));

// ===== scripts/migrate-db.js =====
try { require('dotenv').config(); } catch (_error) { /* Environment variables may already be supplied. */ }
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');
const db = require('../src/db');
const { applyMigrations, inspectPendingMigrations, pendingMigrations, migrations } = require('../src/db/migrations');

function option(name) {
  return process.argv.includes(name);
}

function backupDatabase(sqlite, existedAtStart) {
  if (!existedAtStart || !fs.existsSync(db.dbPath)) return null;
  const backupDir = path.join(path.dirname(db.dbPath), 'backups');
  fs.mkdirSync(backupDir, { recursive: true });
  const destination = path.join(backupDir, `db-before-migration-${new Date().toISOString().replace(/[:.]/g, '-')}.sqlite`);
  sqlite.pragma('wal_checkpoint(TRUNCATE)');
  fs.copyFileSync(db.dbPath, destination);
  return destination;
}

function verify(sqlite) {
  const integrity = sqlite.pragma('integrity_check');
  const integrityOk = integrity.length === 1 && Object.values(integrity[0])[0] === 'ok';
  const foreignKeys = sqlite.pragma('foreign_key_check');
  const applied = new Map(sqlite.prepare('SELECT version, checksum FROM schema_migrations').all().map((row) => [row.version, row.checksum]));
  const missing = migrations.filter((migration) => applied.get(migration.version) !== migration.checksum);
  if (!integrityOk || foreignKeys.length || missing.length) {
    console.error('Migration verification failed.', {
      integrity,
      foreignKeyErrors: foreignKeys,
      missingOrMismatched: missing.map((item) => item.version),
    });
    process.exitCode = 1;
    return false;
  }
  console.log('Migration verification passed.');
  return true;
}

const modes = ['--status', '--dry-run', '--apply', '--verify'].filter(option);
if (modes.length !== 1) {
  console.error('Usage: node scripts/migrate-db.js --status|--dry-run|--apply|--verify');
  process.exit(1);
}

const existedAtStart = fs.existsSync(db.dbPath);
if (!existedAtStart && (option('--status') || option('--dry-run'))) {
  const summary = migrations.map((item) => option('--dry-run') ? `${item.version} (${item.checksum})` : item.version).join(', ');
  console.log(option('--dry-run') ? `Would apply: ${summary}` : `Pending migrations: ${summary}`);
  process.exit(0);
}
const sqlite = db.getDb();
let backup = null;
if (option('--apply')) {
  backup = backupDatabase(sqlite, existedAtStart);
  if (backup) console.log(`Backup created: ${backup}`);
}

const pending = (option('--status') || option('--dry-run'))
  ? inspectPendingMigrations(sqlite)
  : pendingMigrations(sqlite);

if (option('--status')) {
  console.log(pending.length
    ? `Pending migrations: ${pending.map((item) => item.version).join(', ')}`
    : 'Database schema is current.');
  process.exit(0);
}

if (option('--dry-run')) {
  console.log(pending.length
    ? `Would apply: ${pending.map((item) => `${item.version} (${item.checksum})`).join(', ')}`
    : 'No migrations would be applied.');
  process.exit(0);
}

if (option('--verify')) {
  verify(sqlite);
  process.exit(process.exitCode || 0);
}

if (!pending.length) {
  console.log('Database schema is current.');
  verify(sqlite);
  process.exit(process.exitCode || 0);
}

console.log('Applying migrations:', pending.map((item) => item.version).join(', '));
const applied = applyMigrations(sqlite);
console.log('Applied:', applied.join(', '));
verify(sqlite);

// ===== scripts/migrate-private-uploads.js =====
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');
const db = require('../src/db');
const { privateRoot, ensurePrivateRoot } = require('../src/services/privateFiles');

if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production' && !process.argv.includes('--confirm')) {
  console.error('Production migration requires --confirm.');
  process.exit(1);
}

const publicRoot = path.join(__dirname, '..', 'public', 'uploads');
ensurePrivateRoot();

if (fs.existsSync(db.dbPath)) {
  const backupDir = path.join(path.dirname(db.dbPath), 'backups');
  fs.mkdirSync(backupDir, { recursive: true });
  const backupPath = path.join(backupDir, `db-before-private-files-${new Date().toISOString().replace(/[:.]/g, '-')}.sqlite`);
  fs.copyFileSync(db.dbPath, backupPath);
  console.log(`Database backup created: ${backupPath}`);
}

const data = db.readDb();
let migrated = 0;
let missing = 0;
const copiedSources = [];

function migrateUrl(url, { ownerId, contextType, contextId, originalName, mimeType }) {
  if (!url || !url.startsWith('/uploads/')) return null;
  const sourceName = path.basename(url);
  const sourcePath = path.join(publicRoot, sourceName);
  if (!fs.existsSync(sourcePath)) {
    console.warn(`Missing source file: ${sourcePath}`);
    missing += 1;
    return null;
  }

  const extension = path.extname(sourceName).toLowerCase().replace(/[^.a-z0-9]/g, '');
  const storageName = `${uuidv4()}${extension}`;
  const destinationPath = path.join(privateRoot, storageName);
  fs.copyFileSync(sourcePath, destinationPath);
  copiedSources.push(sourcePath);
  fs.chmodSync(destinationPath, 0o600);

  const record = {
    id: uuidv4(), ownerId, contextType, contextId, storageName,
    originalName: originalName || sourceName,
    mimeType: mimeType || 'application/octet-stream',
    size: fs.statSync(destinationPath).size,
    createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
  };
  data.privateFiles.push(record);
  migrated += 1;
  return record;
}

for (const document of data.documents) {
  if (document.fileId) continue;
  const file = migrateUrl(document.fileUrl, {
    ownerId: document.workerId,
    contextType: 'workerDocument',
    contextId: document.id,
    originalName: document.originalName,
  });
  if (file) {
    document.fileId = file.id;
    document.fileUrl = `/files/${file.id}`;
  }
}

for (const evidence of data.paymentEvidence) {
  if (evidence.fileId) continue;
  const file = migrateUrl(evidence.fileUrl, {
    ownerId: evidence.uploadedById,
    contextType: 'paymentEvidence',
    contextId: evidence.id,
    originalName: evidence.originalName,
  });
  if (file) {
    evidence.fileId = file.id;
    evidence.fileUrl = `/files/${file.id}`;
  }
}

for (const evidence of data.disputeEvidence) {
  if (evidence.fileId) continue;
  const file = migrateUrl(evidence.fileUrl, {
    ownerId: evidence.uploadedById,
    contextType: 'disputeEvidence',
    contextId: evidence.id,
    originalName: evidence.originalName,
  });
  if (file) {
    evidence.fileId = file.id;
    evidence.fileUrl = `/files/${file.id}`;
  }
}

for (const message of data.messages) {
  message.attachments = (message.attachments || []).map((attachment) => {
    if (attachment.fileId) return attachment;
    const file = migrateUrl(attachment.url, {
      ownerId: message.senderId,
      contextType: 'message',
      contextId: message.id,
      originalName: attachment.originalName,
      mimeType: attachment.mimeType,
    });
    return file ? { ...attachment, fileId: file.id, url: `/files/${file.id}` } : attachment;
  });
}

db.writeDb(data);
if (!process.argv.includes('--keep-public')) {
  for (const sourcePath of copiedSources) {
    try { fs.unlinkSync(sourcePath); } catch (error) { console.warn(`Could not remove ${sourcePath}: ${error.message}`); }
  }
}
console.log(`Private-file migration complete. Migrated: ${migrated}; missing: ${missing}.`);
console.log(process.argv.includes('--keep-public') ? 'Original public files were retained.' : 'Migrated sensitive files were removed from public/uploads.');

// ===== scripts/migrate-projected-schema.js =====
const db = require('../src/db');
const { definitions, projectedColumns } = require('../src/db/schema');
const { isRelational, TABLES } = require('../src/db/relational');
const { pendingMigrations } = require('../src/db/migrations');

try {
  db.ensureDb();
  db.checkpoint();
  const sqlite = db.getDb();
  let projected = 0;
  let indexes = 0;
  let relational = 0;

  const pending = pendingMigrations(sqlite);
  if (pending.length) {
    console.log(`Pending migrations: ${pending.map((m) => m.version).join(', ')}`);
  }

  for (const [name, def] of Object.entries(definitions)) {
    if (isRelational(name)) {
      relational++;
      continue;
    }
    const columns = new Set(sqlite.prepare(`PRAGMA table_info("${name}")`).all().map((row) => row.name));
    const expected = projectedColumns(name).map((item) => item.column);
    const missing = expected.filter((column) => !columns.has(column));
    if (missing.length) throw new Error(`${name} is missing projected columns: ${missing.join(', ')}`);
    projected += expected.length;
    indexes += def.indexes.length;
  }

  console.log(`Projected schema ready: ${Object.keys(definitions).length} tables, ${projected} projected columns, ${indexes} declared indexes, ${relational} relational tables.`);
} catch (error) {
  console.error('Projected-schema migration failed:', error.message);
  process.exit(1);
}

// ===== scripts/migrate-to-sqlite.js =====
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');
const db = require('../src/db');

const jsonPath = path.join(__dirname, '..', 'data', 'db.json');
if (!fs.existsSync(jsonPath)) {
  console.log('No data/db.json found. Nothing to migrate.');
  process.exit(0);
}

let jsonData;
try {
  jsonData = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(jsonPath, 'utf8'));
} catch (error) {
  console.error('Failed to parse db.json:', error.message);
  process.exit(1);
}

const backupPath = `${jsonPath}.${new Date().toISOString().replace(/[:.]/g, '-')}.bak`;
fs.copyFileSync(jsonPath, backupPath);
db.ensureDb();

try {
  db.mutate(db.collections, (data) => {
    for (const name of db.collections) {
      const items = Array.isArray(jsonData[name]) ? jsonData[name] : [];
      for (const item of items) {
        if (!item || !item.id) continue;
        const existing = data[name].find((candidate) => candidate.id === item.id);
        if (!existing) {
          data[name].push(item);
        }
      }
    }
  });

  const migratedPath = `${jsonPath}.migrated`;
  fs.renameSync(jsonPath, migratedPath);
  console.log(`Migration complete. Source preserved at ${migratedPath}; pre-migration backup at ${backupPath}.`);
} catch (error) {
  console.error('Migration failed and was rolled back:', error.message);
  console.error(`Original JSON remains at ${jsonPath}; backup at ${backupPath}.`);
  process.exit(1);
}

// ===== scripts/seed.js =====
const bcrypt = require('bcryptjs');
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');
const db = require('../src/db');
const { scanJob } = require('../src/services/riskScanner');
const { paymentFeeEstimate } = require('../src/services/marketplace');
const { addAudit, openModerationCase, acceptLegal } = require('../src/services/audit');

async function run() {
  if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production' && process.env.ALLOW_PRODUCTION_SEED !== 'true') {
    throw new Error('Refusing to seed production without ALLOW_PRODUCTION_SEED=true.');
  }
  db.ensureDb();
  const data = db.readDb();
  const demoPassword = process.env.DEMO_PASSWORD || 'ChangeMe123!';
  const passwordHash = await bcrypt.hash(demoPassword, 12);

  function ensureUser(email, attrs) {
    let user = data.users.find((candidate) => candidate.email === email);
    if (!user) {
      user = {
        id: uuidv4(),
        email,
        passwordHash,
        name: attrs.name,
        phone: attrs.phone || '',
        role: attrs.role,
        city: attrs.city || 'Toronto',
        postalCode: attrs.postalCode || 'M5T',
        isAdmin: Boolean(attrs.isAdmin),
        phoneVerified: Boolean(attrs.phoneVerified),
        accountStatus: 'active',
        createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
        updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      };
      data.users.push(user);
    }
    return user;
  }

  const admin = ensureUser('admin@neighbourtask.local', { name: 'Admin User', role: 'both', isAdmin: true, phoneVerified: true });
  const poster = ensureUser('poster@example.com', { name: 'Sample Poster', role: 'poster', phoneVerified: true });
  const worker = ensureUser('worker@example.com', { name: 'Sample Worker', role: 'worker', phoneVerified: true });

  // Keep demo account passwords in sync with the current seed password.
  for (const demo of [admin, poster, worker]) {
    demo.passwordHash = passwordHash;
    demo.updatedAt = new Date().toISOString();
  }

  if (!data.workerProfiles.some((profile) => profile.userId === worker.id)) {
    data.workerProfiles.push({
      id: uuidv4(),
      userId: worker.id,
      displayName: 'Sample Worker',
      bio: 'Reliable local helper with experience in moving, patio work, furniture assembly, mounting, and basic repairs. I bring common hand tools and can provide references.',
      skills: ['moving', 'furniture assembly', 'mounting', 'patio work', 'general labour'],
      tools: 'Cordless drill, hand tools, level, dolly, moving straps.',
      hourlyRate: 35,
      minimumBooking: 2,
      hasVehicle: true,
      availability: 'Weekdays after 4pm, weekends flexible',
      serviceRadiusKm: 15,
      insuranceStatus: 'verified',
      wsibStatus: 'not-provided',
      tradeCertificationStatus: 'not-provided',
      verificationLevel: 'verified-documents',
      status: 'active',
      averageRating: null,
      completedJobs: 0,
      portfolioPhotos: [],
      boostedUntil: null,
      createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    });
  }

  if (!data.workerProfiles.some((profile) => profile.userId === admin.id)) {
    data.workerProfiles.push({
      id: uuidv4(),
      userId: admin.id,
      displayName: 'Admin Worker Profile',
      bio: 'Admin test profile.',
      skills: ['admin testing'],
      tools: '',
      hourlyRate: null,
      minimumBooking: null,
      hasVehicle: false,
      availability: '',
      serviceRadiusKm: null,
      insuranceStatus: 'not-provided',
      wsibStatus: 'not-provided',
      tradeCertificationStatus: 'not-provided',
      verificationLevel: 'basic',
      status: 'active',
      averageRating: null,
      completedJobs: 0,
      portfolioPhotos: [],
      boostedUntil: null,
      createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    });
  }

  if (!data.jobs.length) {
    const sampleJobs = [
      {
        title: 'Move boxes and shelves from storage room',
        categoryId: 'general-labour',
        description: 'Need help moving boxes and lightweight shelving from a basement storage room to a main floor office. No special tools needed. About 2 to 3 hours.',
        city: 'Toronto',
        postalCode: 'M5T',
        payType: 'hourly',
        budgetMin: 25,
        budgetMax: 35,
        estimatedHours: 3,
        urgency: 'this-week',
        riskFlags: ['Heavy lifting'],
      },
      {
        title: 'Level small brick patio section',
        categoryId: 'yard-patio',
        description: 'A 5 ft by 5 ft section of patio brick is uneven. Sand is available. Worker should bring basic tools if possible.',
        city: 'Toronto',
        postalCode: 'M5T',
        payType: 'quote',
        budgetMin: 100,
        budgetMax: 250,
        estimatedHours: 2,
        urgency: 'flexible',
        riskFlags: [],
      },
      {
        title: 'Mount heavy AC outdoor unit bracket into concrete wall',
        categoryId: 'handyman',
        description: 'Need concrete drilling to mount bracket. Outdoor unit is about 140 lbs and roof access is nearby. No HVAC hookup, electrical, or refrigerant work requested.',
        city: 'Toronto',
        postalCode: 'M5T',
        payType: 'quote',
        budgetMin: 150,
        budgetMax: 400,
        estimatedHours: 3,
        urgency: 'this-week',
        riskFlags: ['Concrete drilling', 'Heavy lifting', 'Roof access', 'HVAC / refrigeration'],
      },
    ];

    sampleJobs.forEach((sample) => {
      const riskScan = scanJob(sample);
      data.jobs.push({
        id: uuidv4(),
        posterId: poster.id,
        ...sample,
        locationVisibility: 'neighbourhood',
        desiredDate: null,
        requiresTools: sample.title.includes('AC'),
        requiresInsurance: sample.title.includes('AC'),
        requiresWsib: false,
        requiresCertification: false,
        riskLevel: riskScan.riskLevel,
        riskScan,
        photos: [],
        featuredUntil: null,
        status: riskScan.riskLevel === 'high' ? 'review' : 'open',
        adminNotes: '',
        createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
        updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      });
    });
  }



  const hiredJob = data.jobs.find((job) => job.posterId === poster.id && job.status === 'open');
  if (hiredJob && !data.quotes.some((quote) => quote.jobId === hiredJob.id && quote.workerId === worker.id)) {
    const acceptedQuote = {
      id: uuidv4(),
      jobId: hiredJob.id,
      workerId: worker.id,
      message: 'I can do this with my own tools and can arrive this week.',
      quoteType: hiredJob.payType === 'hourly' ? 'hourly' : 'fixed',
      amount: hiredJob.payType === 'hourly' ? 35 : 180,
      estimatedHours: hiredJob.estimatedHours || 2,
      availability: 'This week after 4pm',
      toolsIncluded: true,
      status: 'accepted',
      createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    };
    data.quotes.push(acceptedQuote);
    hiredJob.status = 'hired';
    hiredJob.hiredWorkerId = worker.id;
    hiredJob.updatedAt = new Date().toISOString();

    data.messages.push({
      id: uuidv4(),
      jobId: hiredJob.id,
      quoteId: acceptedQuote.id,
      senderId: worker.id,
      recipientId: poster.id,
      body: `Quote submitted: ${acceptedQuote.message}`,
      attachments: [],
      safetyScan: { flagged: false, flags: [], notices: [] },
      reported: false,
      createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      readAt: null,
    });
  }

  const acceptedQuoteForPayment = data.quotes.find((quote) => quote.workerId === worker.id && quote.status === 'accepted');
  const paymentJob = acceptedQuoteForPayment ? data.jobs.find((job) => job.id === acceptedQuoteForPayment.jobId) : null;
  if (acceptedQuoteForPayment && paymentJob && !data.paymentRequests.some((payment) => payment.quoteId === acceptedQuoteForPayment.id)) {
    const amount = acceptedQuoteForPayment.quoteType === 'hourly'
      ? acceptedQuoteForPayment.amount * (acceptedQuoteForPayment.estimatedHours || 1)
      : acceptedQuoteForPayment.amount;
    const fees = paymentFeeEstimate(amount, 'poster-5');
    const paymentRequest = {
      id: uuidv4(),
      jobId: paymentJob.id,
      quoteId: acceptedQuoteForPayment.id,
      posterId: paymentJob.posterId,
      workerId: acceptedQuoteForPayment.workerId,
      amount,
      paymentType: 'final',
      feeModel: 'poster-5',
      platformFee: fees.platformFee,
      posterServiceFee: fees.posterServiceFee,
      workerPlatformFee: fees.workerPlatformFee,
      posterTotal: fees.posterTotal,
      workerNetAmount: fees.workerNetAmount,
      milestones: ['Final payment after poster confirms completion'],
      currency: 'CAD',
      processorMode: 'invoice',
      status: 'requested',
      paymentReference: 'INV-DEMO-1001',
      dueDate: new Date(Date.now() + 1000 * 60 * 60 * 24 * 7).toISOString().slice(0, 10),
      note: 'Sample invoice/e-transfer payment request.',
      complianceNote: 'Demo record only. The app does not hold customer funds. Use a regulated payment processor such as Stripe Connect before accepting real marketplace payments.',
      createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    };
    data.paymentRequests.push(paymentRequest);
  }

  const firstPayment = data.paymentRequests.find((payment) => payment.posterId === poster.id && payment.workerId === worker.id);

  if (paymentJob && acceptedQuoteForPayment && !data.appointments.some((appointment) => appointment.jobId === paymentJob.id)) {
    data.appointments.push({
      id: uuidv4(), jobId: paymentJob.id, quoteId: acceptedQuoteForPayment.id, posterId: paymentJob.posterId, workerId: acceptedQuoteForPayment.workerId, proposedById: poster.id,
      startsAt: new Date(Date.now() + 1000 * 60 * 60 * 24 * 3).toISOString(), locationNote: 'Demo address/access note hidden from public browse pages.', scopeNote: 'Confirm original scope before work starts.',
      status: 'confirmed', posterConfirmedAt: new Date().toISOString(), workerConfirmedAt: new Date().toISOString(), createdAt: new Date().toISOString(), updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    });
  }

  if (firstPayment && !data.paymentEvidence.some((evidence) => evidence.paymentRequestId === firstPayment.id)) {
    data.paymentEvidence.push({ id: uuidv4(), paymentRequestId: firstPayment.id, uploadedById: poster.id, type: 'invoice', note: 'Demo invoice evidence note.', fileUrl: null, originalName: '', status: 'submitted', adminNotes: '', createdAt: new Date().toISOString(), updatedAt: new Date().toISOString() });
  }

  if (!data.payoutAccounts.some((account) => account.userId === worker.id)) {
    data.payoutAccounts.push({ id: uuidv4(), userId: worker.id, processor: 'stripe-connect-demo', status: 'ready-for-onboarding', businessType: 'individual', displayName: 'Sample Worker', email: worker.email, notes: 'Demo payout placeholder; no live funds held.', createdAt: new Date().toISOString(), updatedAt: new Date().toISOString() });
  }

  if (paymentJob && firstPayment && !data.disputes.length) {
    data.disputes.push({
      id: uuidv4(),
      jobId: paymentJob.id,
      paymentRequestId: firstPayment.id,
      openedById: poster.id,
      respondentId: worker.id,
      reason: 'Scope disagreement',
      requestedOutcome: 'Admin review and note-taking only',
      description: 'Sample dispute record for testing the Phase 4 dispute centre.',
      status: 'reviewing',
      adminNotes: 'Demo item. No real dispute.',
      resolution: '',
      createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    });
  }


  const demoDispute = data.disputes[0];
  if (demoDispute && !data.disputeEvidence.some((evidence) => evidence.disputeId === demoDispute.id)) {
    data.disputeEvidence.push({ id: uuidv4(), disputeId: demoDispute.id, uploadedById: poster.id, type: 'note', description: 'Demo evidence record attached to the sample dispute.', fileUrl: null, originalName: '', status: 'submitted', adminNotes: '', createdAt: new Date().toISOString(), updatedAt: new Date().toISOString() });
  }

  if (!data.notifications.some((notification) => notification.userId === worker.id && notification.type === 'worker-invite')) {
    data.notifications.push({ id: uuidv4(), userId: worker.id, type: 'worker-invite', title: 'Demo invitation to quote', body: 'A poster invited you to quote on a local odd job.', url: paymentJob ? `/jobs/${paymentJob.id}` : '/jobs', meta: {}, channel: 'in-app', readAt: null, createdAt: new Date().toISOString() });
  }

  if (!data.jobAlerts.some((alert) => alert.userId === worker.id)) {
    data.jobAlerts.push({
      id: uuidv4(),
      userId: worker.id,
      name: 'Toronto general labour alerts',
      categoryId: 'general-labour',
      city: 'Toronto',
      keyword: 'moving',
      maxDistanceKm: 15,
      minBudget: 50,
      frequency: 'daily',
      channel: 'email',
      enabled: true,
      lastMatchedAt: null,
      createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    });
  }


  if (!data.businessAccounts.some((account) => account.userId === poster.id)) {
    data.businessAccounts.push({
      id: uuidv4(),
      userId: poster.id,
      businessName: 'Sample Small Business',
      businessType: 'restaurant-venue',
      website: 'https://example.com',
      phone: '416-555-0100',
      billingEmail: poster.email,
      locations: 'Toronto / Kensington Market sample location',
      plan: 'starter',
      status: 'active',
      createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    });
  }


  const business = data.businessAccounts.find((account) => account.userId === poster.id);
  if (business && !data.businessLocations.some((location) => location.businessId === business.id)) {
    data.businessLocations.push({
      id: uuidv4(), businessId: business.id, userId: poster.id, name: 'Kensington Market sample location', address: '319 Augusta Ave', city: 'Toronto', postalCode: 'M5T 2M2',
      contactName: 'Sample Poster', contactPhone: '416-555-0100', notes: 'Demo business location for one-off maintenance and event setup tasks.', status: 'active',
      createdAt: new Date().toISOString(), updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    });
  }

  if (business && !data.recurringTaskTemplates.some((template) => template.businessId === business.id)) {
    const template = {
      id: uuidv4(), businessId: business.id, userId: poster.id, title: 'Weekly patio and storage helper', categoryId: 'general-labour',
      description: 'Recurring demo template for patio cleanup, moving stock, and light general labour. Review worker classification before using recurring supervised work.',
      defaultBudgetMin: 80, defaultBudgetMax: 160, estimatedHours: 3, recurringPattern: 'weekly as needed', toolsRequired: false, insuranceRequired: false,
      safetyWarningsAccepted: true, status: 'active', createdAt: new Date().toISOString(), updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    };
    data.recurringTaskTemplates.push(template);
    openModerationCase(data, { targetType: 'recurringTaskTemplate', targetId: template.id, reason: 'Recurring demo template may require worker-classification review', priority: 'normal' });
  }

  const workerProfile = data.workerProfiles.find((profile) => profile.userId === worker.id);
  if (business && workerProfile && !data.preferredWorkers.some((item) => item.businessId === business.id && item.profileId === workerProfile.id)) {
    data.preferredWorkers.push({
      id: uuidv4(), businessId: business.id, userId: poster.id, profileId: workerProfile.id, workerId: worker.id,
      status: 'preferred', tags: 'tools, vehicle, reliable', notes: 'Demo preferred worker note for business repeat hiring.',
      createdAt: new Date().toISOString(), updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    });
  }

  if (business && !data.businessInvoices.some((invoice) => invoice.businessId === business.id)) {
    data.businessInvoices.push({
      id: uuidv4(), businessId: business.id, userId: poster.id, title: 'May odd-job export record', periodStart: '2026-05-01', periodEnd: '2026-05-31',
      amount: 185, currency: 'CAD', status: 'draft', notes: 'Demo invoice/export record for business dashboard.',
      createdAt: new Date().toISOString(), updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    });
  }

  if (!data.legalAcceptances.some((item) => item.userId === poster.id && item.documentType === 'posterAgreement')) {
    acceptLegal(data, poster.id, 'posterAgreement', '2026-05-31', 'seed');
    acceptLegal(data, worker.id, 'workerAgreement', '2026-05-31', 'seed');
    acceptLegal(data, poster.id, 'safetyAcknowledgement', '2026-05-31', 'seed');
  }

  if (!data.auditLog.some((entry) => entry.action === 'seed.phase12to15')) {
    addAudit(data, admin.id, 'seed.phase12to15', 'system', 'neighbourtask', { phases: '12-15', features: ['business accounts', 'mobile pwa', 'admin compliance', 'seo growth'] });
  }

  db.writeDb(data);
  console.log('Seed complete.');
  console.log('Demo users created. Set DEMO_PASSWORD to control their password.');
  console.log('Admin: admin@neighbourtask.local');
  console.log('Poster: poster@example.com');
  console.log('Worker: worker@example.com');
}

run().catch((error) => {
  console.error(error);
  process.exit(1);
});

// ===== scripts/verify-architecture.js =====
const assert = require('assert');
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');

const root = path.join(__dirname, '..');
const routeRoots = [path.join(root, 'src', 'routes'), path.join(root, 'src', 'domains')];
const files = [];
function walk(directory) {
  for (const entry of fs.readdirSync(directory, { withFileTypes: true })) {
    const full = path.join(directory, entry.name);
    if (entry.isDirectory()) walk(full);
    else if (entry.isFile() && entry.name.endsWith('.js')) files.push(full);
  }
}
routeRoots.forEach(walk);
for (const file of files) {
  const source = fs.readFileSync(file, 'utf8');
  const relative = path.relative(root, file);
  assert(!/db\.(?:readDb|writeDb|mutate)\s*\(/.test(source), `${relative} must use repositories or targeted database operations.`);
  assert(!/require\(['"](?:\.\.\/)+db['"]\)/.test(source), `${relative} must not import db directly.`);
  assert(!/\/phase-\d/.test(source), `${relative} must not reference phase-numbered modules.`);
}

const wrappers = [
  'src/routes/adminRoutes.js', 'src/routes/authRoutes.js', 'src/routes/jobRoutes.js',
  'src/routes/messageRoutes.js', 'src/routes/workerRoutes.js',
];
for (const relative of wrappers) {
  const source = fs.readFileSync(path.join(root, relative), 'utf8');
  assert(source.split('\n').length <= 5, `${relative} should remain a thin compatibility wrapper.`);
}

assert(!fs.existsSync(path.join(root, 'src/routes/phaseRoutes.js')), 'Legacy phaseRoutes.js must be removed.');
const appSource = fs.readFileSync(path.join(root, 'app.js'), 'utf8');
assert(!appSource.includes('phaseRoutes'), 'app.js must not mount phase-numbered routes.');

const dbSource = fs.readFileSync(path.join(root, 'src/db.js'), 'utf8');
for (const capability of ['function paginate(', 'function cursorPage(', 'function transaction(', 'function groupAll(', 'function sum(']) {
  assert(dbSource.includes(capability), `Database is missing ${capability}`);
}
assert(!dbSource.includes('function mutate('), 'Database must not export legacy mutate.');
console.log(`Architecture verification passed for ${files.length} route/domain files.`);

// ===== scripts/verify-implementation.js =====
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');
const { spawnSync } = require('child_process');

const root = path.join(__dirname, '..');
const ignored = new Set(['.git', 'node_modules']);

function walk(directory) {
  return fs.readdirSync(directory, { withFileTypes: true }).flatMap((entry) => {
    if (ignored.has(entry.name)) return [];
    const fullPath = path.join(directory, entry.name);
    return entry.isDirectory() ? walk(fullPath) : [fullPath];
  });
}

function resolveRelative(fromFile, request) {
  const base = path.resolve(path.dirname(fromFile), request);
  const candidates = [base, `${base}.js`, path.join(base, 'index.js')];
  return candidates.find((candidate) => fs.existsSync(candidate));
}

const jsFiles = walk(root).filter((file) => file.endsWith('.js'));
const failures = [];
for (const file of jsFiles) {
  const syntax = spawnSync(process.execPath, ['--check', file], { encoding: 'utf8' });
  if (syntax.status !== 0) failures.push(`${path.relative(root, file)}: ${syntax.stderr.trim()}`);

  const source = fs.readFileSync(file, 'utf8');
  for (const match of source.matchAll(/require\((['"])(\.\.?\/[^'"]+)\1\)/g)) {
    if (!resolveRelative(file, match[2])) failures.push(`${path.relative(root, file)}: unresolved ${match[2]}`);
  }
}

if (failures.length) {
  console.error(failures.join('\n'));
  process.exit(1);
}
console.log(`Implementation verification passed for ${jsFiles.length} JavaScript files.`);

const assert = require('assert');
const fs = require('fs');

const req = {

};

assert.equal(canTransition('job', 'open', 'completed'), false);
assert.equal(canTransition('quote', 'accepted', 'submitted'), false);

const poster = { id: 'poster', isAdmin: false };
const worker = { id: 'worker', isAdmin: false };
const stranger = { id: 'stranger', isAdmin: false };

const quote = { id: 'quote', jobId: job.id, workerId: worker.id };
assert.equal(canViewJob(stranger, job), false);
assert.equal(canViewJob(poster, job), true);
assert.equal(canViewQuote(worker, job, quote), true);
assert.equal(canViewQuote(stranger, job, quote), false);
assert.equal(relationshipExists({ messages: [], quotes: [quote], jobs: [job] }, poster.id, worker.id), true);

const appSource = read('app.js');
const localsSource = read('src/middleware/locals.js');
const quickPostSource = read('src/domains/jobs/postingRoutes.js');
