assert(!appSource.includes('contentSecurityPolicy: false'), 'CSP must not be disabled.');
assert(!localsSource.includes('res.locals.apiKey'), 'API secrets must not be exposed to templates.');
assert(!quickPostSource.includes('req.session.userId = user.id'), 'Quick post must not authenticate by contact match.');
assert(!authSource.includes("data.users.find((candidate) => candidate.id === req.body.userId"), 'Account claim must not trust a user ID.');
assert(!serviceWorkerSource.includes("cache.put(request, copy)\n      return response"), 'Authenticated pages must not be runtime cached.');
assert(!uploadUiSource.includes("fileInput.value = ''"), 'File selection must not be cleared after synchronization.');
assert(jobServiceSource.includes('validateJobInput') && jobServiceSource.includes('scanJob'), 'Job creation must use shared validation and risk scanning.');
assert(dbSource.includes('function transaction(') && dbSource.includes('function paginate(') && dbSource.includes('seoLocations') && dbSource.includes('categories'), 'Database must expose atomic, paginated operations and reference data.');
assert(!appSource.includes("'unsafe-inline'"), 'CSP must not allow unsafe inline scripts or styles.');
assert(appSource.includes('createLayoutEngine') && !appSource.includes('attachUxAssets'), 'UX must use the native EJS layout engine.');

const multipartRoutes = [
  'src/domains/jobs/postingRoutes.js',
  'src/domains/workers/workerRoutes.js',
  'src/routes/posterRoutes.js',
  'src/domains/messages/messageRoutes.js',
];
for (const relativePath of multipartRoutes) {
  const source = read(relativePath);
  const uploadCalls = (source.match(/(?:upload|privateUpload)\.(?:single|array)\(/g) || []).length;
  const validators = (source.match(/validateMultipartCsrf/g) || []).length - 1; // exclude import
  assert(validators >= uploadCalls, `${relativePath} has an upload route without multipart CSRF/content validation.`);
}

console.log('Security regression checks passed.');

// ===== src/db/driver.js =====
const fs = require('fs');

function wrapNodeStatement(statement) {
  return {
    run(...parameters) {
      const result = statement.run(...parameters);
      return {
        changes: Number(result.changes || 0),
        lastInsertRowid: result.lastInsertRowid,
      };
    },
    get(...parameters) {
      return statement.get(...parameters);
    },
    all(...parameters) {
      return statement.all(...parameters);
    },
  };
}

class NodeSqliteDatabase {
  constructor(filename) {
    const { DatabaseSync } = require('node:sqlite');
    this.filename = filename;
    this.raw = new DatabaseSync(filename);
  }

  prepare(sql) {
    return wrapNodeStatement(this.raw.prepare(sql));
  }

  exec(sql) {
    this.raw.exec(sql);
    return this;
  }

  pragma(statement) {
    const sql = `PRAGMA ${statement}`;
    if (String(statement).includes('=')) {
      this.raw.exec(sql);
      return [];
    }
    return this.raw.prepare(sql).all();
  }

  transaction(callback) {
    const execute = (mode = '') => {
      if (this.raw.isTransaction) return callback();
      this.raw.exec(`BEGIN${mode ? ` ${mode}` : ''}`);
      try {
        const result = callback();
        if (result && typeof result.then === 'function') {
          throw new Error('SQLite transactions must be synchronous.');
        }
        this.raw.exec('COMMIT');
        return result;
      } catch (error) {
        try { this.raw.exec('ROLLBACK'); } catch (_rollbackError) { /* transaction may already be closed */ }
        throw error;
      }
    };
    const transaction = () => execute();
    transaction.deferred = () => execute('DEFERRED');
    transaction.immediate = () => execute('IMMEDIATE');
    transaction.exclusive = () => execute('EXCLUSIVE');
    return transaction;
  }

  async backup(destination) {
    this.pragma('wal_checkpoint(FULL)');
    fs.copyFileSync(this.filename, destination);
    return destination;
  }

  close() {
    this.raw.close();
  }
}

function loadDriver() {
  if (process.env.SQLITE_DRIVER !== 'node') {
    try {
      // eslint-disable-next-line global-require
      return require('better-sqlite3');
    } catch (error) {
      if (process.env.SQLITE_DRIVER === 'better-sqlite3') throw error;
    }
  }
  return NodeSqliteDatabase;
}

module.exports = loadDriver();
module.exports.NodeSqliteDatabase = NodeSqliteDatabase;

function migrate(data) {
  const result = { ...data };
  for (const name of collections) {
    if (!Array.isArray(result[name])) result[name] = [];
  }
  result.seoLocations = seoLocations;
  result.categoryGuides = categoryGuides;
  result.categories = categories;

  result.users = result.users.map((user) => ({
    phoneVerified: false,
    accountStatus: 'active',
    ...user,
  }));
  result.workerProfiles = result.workerProfiles.map((profile) => ({
    availability: '',
    serviceRadiusKm: null,
    complianceAcceptedAt: null,
    boostedUntil: null,
    lastActiveAt: profile.updatedAt || profile.createdAt || null,
    ...profile,
    portfolioPhotos: profile.portfolioPhotos || [],
  }));
  result.jobs = result.jobs.map((job) => ({
    featuredUntil: null,
    quoteCount: 0,
    hiredWorkerId: job.hiredWorkerId || null,
    ...job,
    photos: job.photos || [],
  }));
  result.paymentRequests = result.paymentRequests.map((payment) => ({
    currency: 'CAD',
    platformFee: 0,
    posterServiceFee: 0,
    workerPlatformFee: 0,
    posterTotal: payment.amount || 0,
    workerNetAmount: payment.amount || 0,
    feeModel: 'none',
    paymentType: 'final',
    processorMode: 'invoice',
    milestones: [],
    complianceNote: 'Demo record only. The app does not hold customer funds.',
    ...payment,
  }));
  result.paymentEvidence = result.paymentEvidence.map((evidence) => ({ status: 'submitted', adminNotes: '', ...evidence }));
  result.payoutAccounts = result.payoutAccounts.map((account) => ({ status: 'not-connected', processor: 'stripe-connect-demo', ...account }));
  result.disputes = result.disputes.map((dispute) => ({
    status: 'open',
    adminNotes: '',
    resolution: '',
    evidenceSummary: '',
    ...dispute,
  }));
  result.disputeEvidence = result.disputeEvidence.map((evidence) => ({ status: 'submitted', adminNotes: '', ...evidence }));
  result.messageReports = result.messageReports.map((report) => ({ status: 'open', adminNotes: '', ...report }));
  result.userBlocks = result.userBlocks.map((block) => ({ status: 'active', ...block }));
  result.appointments = result.appointments.map((appointment) => ({ status: 'proposed', posterConfirmedAt: null, workerConfirmedAt: null, ...appointment }));
  result.completionConfirmations = result.completionConfirmations.map((confirmation) => ({ notes: '', ...confirmation }));
  result.quoteRevisions = result.quoteRevisions.map((revision) => ({ status: 'proposed', ...revision }));
  result.notifications = result.notifications.map((notification) => ({ readAt: null, channel: 'in-app', ...notification }));
  result.businessAccounts = result.businessAccounts.map((account) => ({
    status: 'active',
    plan: 'free',
    insuranceRequirements: '',
    paymentTerms: '',
    preferredWorkerNotes: '',
    ...account,
  }));
  result.businessLocations = result.businessLocations.map((location) => ({ status: 'active', notes: '', ...location }));
  result.recurringTaskTemplates = result.recurringTaskTemplates.map((template) => ({ status: 'active', safetyWarningsAccepted: false, ...template }));
  result.preferredWorkers = result.preferredWorkers.map((item) => ({ status: 'preferred', notes: '', ...item }));
  result.businessInvoices = result.businessInvoices.map((invoice) => ({ status: 'draft', currency: 'CAD', ...invoice }));
  result.jobAlerts = result.jobAlerts.map((alert) => ({
    enabled: true,
    channel: 'email',
    frequency: 'daily',
    ...alert,
  }));
  result.auditLog = result.auditLog.map((entry) => ({ severity: 'info', meta: {}, ...entry }));
  result.moderationCases = result.moderationCases.map((item) => ({ status: 'open', priority: 'normal', adminNotes: '', ...item }));
  result.legalAcceptances = result.legalAcceptances.map((item) => ({ status: 'accepted', ...item }));
  return result;
}

function getDb() {
  if (_db) return _db;
  if (!fs.existsSync(dataDir)) fs.mkdirSync(dataDir, { recursive: true });
  _db = new Database(dbPath);
  _db.pragma('journal_mode = WAL');
  _db.pragma('foreign_keys = ON');
  _db.pragma('busy_timeout = 5000');
  _db.pragma('synchronous = NORMAL');
  return _db;
}

function quoteIdentifier(value) {
  return `"${String(value).replace(/"/g, '""')}"`;
}

function storageTable(name) {
  return tableFor(name);
}

function queryColumn(name, field) {
  if (isRelational(name)) {
    const column = relationalColumn(name, field);
    if (!column) throw new Error(`Field ${field} is not queryable on ${name}`);
    return column;
  }
  return columnForField(name, field);
}

function decodeStoredRow(name, row) {
  if (!row) return null;
  if (isRelational(name)) return normalizeItem(name, itemFromRow(name, row));
  return normalizeItem(name, JSON.parse(row.data));
}

function selectList(name) {
  return isRelational(name) ? '*' : 'data, version';
}

function decodeStoredRows(name, rows) {
  return rows.map((row) => decodeStoredRow(name, row));
}

function selectAllRows(sqlite, name, suffix = '', parameters = []) {
  return sqlite.prepare(`SELECT ${selectList(name)} FROM ${quoteIdentifier(storageTable(name))}${suffix}`).all(...parameters);
}

function selectStoredRow(sqlite, name, id) {
  return sqlite.prepare(`SELECT ${selectList(name)} FROM ${quoteIdentifier(storageTable(name))} WHERE id = ?`).get(id);
}

function tableColumns(db, name) {
  return new Set(db.prepare(`PRAGMA table_info(${quoteIdentifier(name)})`).all().map((row) => row.name));
}

function ensureCollectionTable(db, name) {
  const projections = projectedColumns(name);
  const columnsSql = projections.map((item) => `${quoteIdentifier(item.column)} ${item.type}`).join(', ');
  db.exec(`CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ${quoteIdentifier(name)} (
    id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    data TEXT NOT NULL,
    version INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 1${columnsSql ? `, ${columnsSql}` : ''}
  )`);

  const existing = tableColumns(db, name);
  let projectionChanged = false;
  if (!existing.has('version')) {
    db.exec(`ALTER TABLE ${quoteIdentifier(name)} ADD COLUMN version INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 1`);
    projectionChanged = true;
  }
  for (const item of projections) {
    if (!existing.has(item.column)) {
      db.exec(`ALTER TABLE ${quoteIdentifier(name)} ADD COLUMN ${quoteIdentifier(item.column)} ${item.type}`);
      projectionChanged = true;
    }
  }

  if (projectionChanged) {
    const rows = db.prepare(`SELECT id, data FROM ${quoteIdentifier(name)}`).all();
    if (rows.length) {
      const assignments = projections.map((item) => `${quoteIdentifier(item.column)} = ?`).join(', ');
      const statement = db.prepare(`UPDATE ${quoteIdentifier(name)} SET ${assignments} WHERE id = ?`);
      const backfill = db.transaction(() => {
        for (const row of rows) {
          const item = normalizeItem(name, JSON.parse(row.data));
          statement.run(...projectionValues(name, item), row.id);
        }
      });
      backfill();
    }
  }

  for (const fields of definition(name).indexes || []) {
    const columns = fields.map((field) => quoteIdentifier(queryColumn(name, field))).join(', ');
    const suffix = fields.join('_').replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9_]/g, '_').toLowerCase();
    db.exec(`CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS ${quoteIdentifier(`${name}_${suffix}_idx`)} ON ${quoteIdentifier(name)} (${columns})`);
  }
}

function ensureDb() {
  if (_ensured) return;
  const db = getDb();
  const create = db.transaction(() => {
    const pending = inspectPendingMigrations(db);
    if (pending.length && process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production' && process.env.AUTO_MIGRATE !== 'true') {
      const error = new Error(`Database migrations are pending: ${pending.map((item) => item.version).join(', ')}`);
      error.code = 'DB_MIGRATION_REQUIRED';
      throw error;
    }
    if (pending.length) applyMigrations(db);
    const prepareControlTables = db.transaction(() => {
      for (const name of collections) {
        if (!isRelational(name)) ensureCollectionTable(db, name);
      }
      db.exec('CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS sessions (sid TEXT PRIMARY KEY, data TEXT NOT NULL, expires INTEGER NOT NULL)');
      db.exec('CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS sessions_expires_idx ON sessions(expires)');
      db.exec('CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS schema_meta (key TEXT PRIMARY KEY, value TEXT NOT NULL, updated_at TEXT NOT NULL)');
      db.prepare(`INSERT INTO schema_meta (key, value, updated_at) VALUES ('storage_format', 'relational-core-v1', ?)
        ON CONFLICT(key) DO UPDATE SET value = excluded.value, updated_at = excluded.updated_at`)
        .run(new Date().toISOString());
    });
    prepareControlTables.immediate();
  });
  create.immediate();
  _ensured = true;
}

function assertCollection(name) {
  if (!collections.includes(name)) throw new Error(`Unknown collection: ${name}`);
}

function stableStringify(value) {
  if (Array.isArray(value)) return `[${value.map(stableStringify).join(',')}]`;
  if (value && typeof value === 'object') {
    return `{${Object.keys(value).sort().map((key) => `${JSON.stringify(key)}:${stableStringify(value[key])}`).join(',')}}`;
  }
  return JSON.stringify(value);
}

function normalizeItem(name, item) {
  const shell = {};
  for (const collectionName of collections) shell[collectionName] = [];
  shell[name] = [item];
  return migrate(shell)[name][0];
}

function rowInsertStatement(db, name) {
  if (isRelational(name)) return null;
  const projections = projectedColumns(name);
  const columnNames = ['id', 'data', 'version', ...projections.map((item) => item.column)];
  const sql = `INSERT INTO ${quoteIdentifier(name)} (${columnNames.map(quoteIdentifier).join(', ')})
    VALUES (${columnNames.map(() => '?').join(', ')})`;
  return db.prepare(sql);
}

function insertRow(db, name, item, version = 1) {
  const normalized = normalizeItem(name, item);
  if (isRelational(name)) {
    const row = splitItem(name, { ...normalized, version });
    const columns = Object.keys(row);
    db.prepare(`INSERT INTO ${quoteIdentifier(storageTable(name))} (${columns.map(quoteIdentifier).join(', ')})
      VALUES (${columns.map(() => '?').join(', ')})`).run(...columns.map((column) => row[column]));
    return normalized;
  }
  rowInsertStatement(db, name).run(
    normalized.id,
    JSON.stringify(normalized),
    version,
    ...projectionValues(name, normalized),
  );
  return normalized;
}

function updateRow(db, name, item, expectedVersion) {
  const normalized = normalizeItem(name, item);
  if (isRelational(name)) {
    const row = splitItem(name, { ...normalized, version: expectedVersion });
    const columns = Object.keys(row).filter((c) => c !== 'id' && c !== 'version');
    const assignments = columns.map((column) => `${quoteIdentifier(column)} = ?`).join(', ');
    const result = db.prepare(`UPDATE ${quoteIdentifier(storageTable(name))} SET ${assignments}, version = version + 1
      WHERE id = ? AND version = ?`).run(
      ...columns.map((column) => row[column]),
      normalized.id,
      expectedVersion,
    );
    if (result.changes !== 1) {
      const error = new Error(`Concurrent update detected for ${name}/${normalized.id}`);
      error.code = 'DB_CONFLICT';
      throw error;
    }
    return normalized;
  }
  const projections = projectedColumns(name);
  const assignments = ['data = ?', 'version = version + 1', ...projections.map((entry) => `${quoteIdentifier(entry.column)} = ?`)];
  const result = db.prepare(`UPDATE ${quoteIdentifier(name)} SET ${assignments.join(', ')}
    WHERE id = ? AND version = ?`).run(
    JSON.stringify(normalized),
    ...projectionValues(name, normalized),
    normalized.id,
    expectedVersion,
  );
  if (result.changes !== 1) {
    const error = new Error(`Concurrent update detected for ${name}/${normalized.id}`);
    error.code = 'DB_CONFLICT';
    throw error;
  }
  return normalized;
}

function createDataView() {
  const db = getDb();
  const data = { seoLocations, categoryGuides, categories };
  const snapshot = {};
  const cache = {};
  const loaded = new Set();

  function loadCollection(name) {
    if (loaded.has(name)) return cache[name];
    const rows = selectAllRows(db, name);
    const items = decodeStoredRows(name, rows);
    cache[name] = items;
    snapshot[name] = new Map(items.map((item, index) => [
      item.id,
      { value: stableStringify(item), version: rows[index].version },
    ]));
    loaded.add(name);
    return items;
  }

  for (const name of collections) {
    Object.defineProperty(data, name, {
      enumerable: true,
      configurable: false,
      get: () => loadCollection(name),
      set: (value) => {
        loadCollection(name);
        cache[name] = Array.isArray(value) ? value : [];
      },
    });
  }
  Object.defineProperty(data, '__snapshot', { value: snapshot, enumerable: false });
  Object.defineProperty(data, '__cache', { value: cache, enumerable: false });
  Object.defineProperty(data, '__loaded', { value: loaded, enumerable: false });
  return data;
}

function readDb() {
  ensureDb();
  return createDataView();
}

function persistChanges(data, { checkConflicts = true } = {}) {
  const db = getDb();
  const snapshot = data.__snapshot || {};
  const loadedNames = data.__loaded ? [...data.__loaded] : collections;

  for (const name of loadedNames) {
    assertCollection(name);
    const sourceItems = data.__cache ? (data.__cache[name] || []) : (data[name] || []);
    const desiredItems = sourceItems.map((item) => normalizeItem(name, item));
    const desired = new Map(desiredItems.map((item) => [item.id, item]));
    const original = snapshot[name] || new Map();
    const ids = new Set([...original.keys(), ...desired.keys()]);
    const select = db.prepare(`SELECT ${selectList(name)} FROM ${quoteIdentifier(storageTable(name))} WHERE id = ?`);
    const deleteStatement = db.prepare(`DELETE FROM ${quoteIdentifier(storageTable(name))} WHERE id = ? AND version = ?`);

    for (const id of ids) {
      const desiredItem = desired.get(id);
      const desiredValue = desiredItem ? stableStringify(desiredItem) : null;
      const originalRecord = original.get(id) || null;
      const originalValue = originalRecord ? originalRecord.value : null;
      if (desiredValue === originalValue) continue;

      const currentRow = select.get(id);
      if (!originalRecord) {
        if (currentRow) {
          const error = new Error(`Concurrent insert detected for ${name}/${id}`);
          error.code = 'DB_CONFLICT';
          throw error;
        }
        if (desiredItem) insertRow(db, name, desiredItem);
        continue;
      }

      if (!currentRow) {
        const error = new Error(`Concurrent delete detected for ${name}/${id}`);
        error.code = 'DB_CONFLICT';
        throw error;
      }

      if (checkConflicts) {
        const currentValue = stableStringify(decodeStoredRow(name, currentRow));
        if (currentRow.version !== originalRecord.version || currentValue !== originalValue) {
          const error = new Error(`Concurrent update detected for ${name}/${id}`);
          error.code = 'DB_CONFLICT';
          throw error;
        }
      }

      if (!desiredItem) {
        const deleted = deleteStatement.run(id, currentRow.version);
        if (deleted.changes !== 1) {
          const error = new Error(`Concurrent delete detected for ${name}/${id}`);
          error.code = 'DB_CONFLICT';
          throw error;
        }
      } else {
        updateRow(db, name, desiredItem, currentRow.version);
      }
    }
  }
}

function writeDb(data) {
  ensureDb();
  const transaction = getDb().transaction(() => persistChanges(data, { checkConflicts: true }));
  transaction.immediate();
}

function collection(name) {
  assertCollection(name);
  ensureDb();
  return decodeStoredRows(name, selectAllRows(getDb(), name));
}

function findById(name, id) {
  assertCollection(name);
  ensureDb();
  return decodeStoredRow(name, selectStoredRow(getDb(), name, id));
}

function parseCondition(name, field, condition, parameters) {
  const column = quoteIdentifier(queryColumn(name, field));
  if (condition && typeof condition === 'object' && !Array.isArray(condition)) {
    const clauses = [];
    for (const [operator, value] of Object.entries(condition)) {
      if (operator === '$in') {
        const values = Array.isArray(value) ? value : [];
        if (!values.length) clauses.push('1 = 0');
        else {
          clauses.push(`${column} IN (${values.map(() => '?').join(', ')})`);
          parameters.push(...values);
        }
      } else if (operator === '$ne') {
        clauses.push(`${column} IS NOT ?`);
        parameters.push(value);
      } else if (operator === '$like') {
        clauses.push(`${column} LIKE ? ESCAPE '\\'`);
        parameters.push(value);
      } else if (operator === '$gt' || operator === '$gte' || operator === '$lt' || operator === '$lte') {
        const sqlOperator = { $gt: '>', $gte: '>=', $lt: '<', $lte: '<=' }[operator];
        clauses.push(`${column} ${sqlOperator} ?`);
        parameters.push(value);
      } else if (operator === '$null') {
        clauses.push(value ? `${column} IS NULL` : `${column} IS NOT NULL`);
      } else {
        throw new Error(`Unsupported query operator ${operator}`);
      }
    }
    return clauses.length > 1 ? `(${clauses.join(' AND ')})` : clauses[0];
  }
  if (condition === null || condition === undefined) return `${column} IS NULL`;
  parameters.push(condition === true ? 1 : condition === false ? 0 : condition);
  return `${column} = ?`;
}

function buildQuery(name, options = {}, countOnly = false) {
  const parameters = [];
  const where = options.where || {};
  const clauses = Object.entries(where).map(([field, condition]) => parseCondition(name, field, condition, parameters));
  if (Array.isArray(options.or) && options.or.length) {
    const orClauses = options.or.map((branch) => {
      const branchClauses = Object.entries(branch || {}).map(([field, condition]) => parseCondition(name, field, condition, parameters));
      return branchClauses.length ? `(${branchClauses.join(' AND ')})` : '(1 = 1)';
    });
    clauses.push(`(${orClauses.join(' OR ')})`);
  }
  const whereSql = clauses.length ? ` WHERE ${clauses.join(' AND ')}` : '';

  let orderSql = '';
  if (!countOnly && options.orderBy) {
    const orderEntries = Array.isArray(options.orderBy) ? options.orderBy : [options.orderBy];
    const orders = orderEntries.map((entry) => {
      const field = typeof entry === 'string' ? entry : entry.field;
      const direction = typeof entry === 'object' && String(entry.direction).toLowerCase() === 'asc' ? 'ASC' : 'DESC';
      return `${quoteIdentifier(queryColumn(name, field))} ${direction}`;
    });
    if (orders.length) orderSql = ` ORDER BY ${orders.join(', ')}`;
  }

  let pagingSql = '';
  if (!countOnly && options.limit !== undefined) {
    const limit = Math.min(500, Math.max(1, Number.parseInt(options.limit, 10) || 50));
    const offset = Math.max(0, Number.parseInt(options.offset, 10) || 0);
    pagingSql = ' LIMIT ? OFFSET ?';
    parameters.push(limit, offset);
  }

  return { whereSql, orderSql, pagingSql, parameters };
}

function findManyWithDb(sqlite, name, options = {}) {
  const { whereSql, orderSql, pagingSql, parameters } = buildQuery(name, options);
  const rows = selectAllRows(sqlite, name, `${whereSql}${orderSql}${pagingSql}`, parameters);
  return decodeStoredRows(name, rows);
}

function findByIdWithDb(sqlite, name, id) {
  return decodeStoredRow(name, selectStoredRow(sqlite, name, id));
}

function countWithDb(sqlite, name, where = {}) {
  const { whereSql, parameters } = buildQuery(name, { where }, true);
  return sqlite.prepare(`SELECT COUNT(*) AS total FROM ${quoteIdentifier(storageTable(name))}${whereSql}`).get(...parameters).total;
}

function updateWithDb(sqlite, name, id, updates) {
  const row = selectStoredRow(sqlite, name, id);
  if (!row) return null;
  const next = normalizeItem(name, {
    ...decodeStoredRow(name, row),
    ...updates,
    updatedAt: Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(updates || {}, 'updatedAt')
      ? updates.updatedAt
      : new Date().toISOString(),
  });
  return updateRow(sqlite, name, next, row.version);
}

function findMany(name, options = {}) {
  return findManyWithDb(getDb(), name, options);
}

function findOne(name, options = {}) {
  return findMany(name, { ...options, limit: 1, offset: 0 })[0] || null;
}

function count(name, where = {}) {
  return countWithDb(getDb(), name, where);
}

function groupCount(name, field, values, where = {}) {
  assertCollection(name);
  ensureDb();
  const uniqueValues = [...new Set((values || []).filter((value) => value !== undefined && value !== null))];
  if (!uniqueValues.length) return new Map();
  const parameters = [];
  const groupColumn = quoteIdentifier(queryColumn(name, field));
  const clauses = [`${groupColumn} IN (${uniqueValues.map(() => '?').join(', ')})`];
  parameters.push(...uniqueValues);
  for (const [whereField, condition] of Object.entries(where)) {
    clauses.push(parseCondition(name, whereField, condition, parameters));
  }
  const rows = getDb().prepare(`SELECT ${groupColumn} AS value, COUNT(*) AS total
    FROM ${quoteIdentifier(storageTable(name))} WHERE ${clauses.join(' AND ')} GROUP BY ${groupColumn}`).all(...parameters);
  return new Map(rows.map((row) => [row.value, row.total]));
}

function paginate(name, { page = 1, perPage = 25, ...options } = {}) {
  const safePerPage = Math.min(100, Math.max(1, Number.parseInt(perPage, 10) || 25));
  const safePage = Math.max(1, Number.parseInt(page, 10) || 1);
  const total = count(name, options.where || {});
  const pageCount = Math.max(1, Math.ceil(total / safePerPage));
  const currentPage = Math.min(safePage, pageCount);
  const items = findMany(name, {
    ...options,
    limit: safePerPage,
    offset: (currentPage - 1) * safePerPage,
  });
  return {
    items,
    pagination: {
      page: currentPage,
      perPage: safePerPage,
      total,
      pageCount,
      hasPrevious: currentPage > 1,
      hasNext: currentPage < pageCount,
    },
  };
}

function insert(name, item) {
  assertCollection(name);
  if (!item || !item.id) throw new Error(`Cannot insert into ${name} without an id.`);
  ensureDb();
  return insertRow(getDb(), name, item);
}

function update(name, id, updates) {
  return updateWithDb(getDb(), name, id, updates);
}

function remove(name, id) {
  assertCollection(name);
  ensureDb();
  return getDb().prepare(`DELETE FROM ${quoteIdentifier(storageTable(name))} WHERE id = ?`).run(id).changes > 0;
}

function createTransactionContext(sqlite) {
  const context = {
    findById(name, id) {
      assertCollection(name);
      return findByIdWithDb(sqlite, name, id);
    },
    findOne(name, options = {}) {
      assertCollection(name);
      return findManyWithDb(sqlite, name, { ...options, limit: 1, offset: 0 })[0] || null;
    },
    findMany(name, options = {}) {
      assertCollection(name);
      return findManyWithDb(sqlite, name, options);
    },
    count(name, where = {}) {
      assertCollection(name);
      return countWithDb(sqlite, name, where);
    },
    insert(name, item) {
      assertCollection(name);
      if (!item || !item.id) throw new Error(`Cannot insert into ${name} without an id.`);
      return insertRow(sqlite, name, item);
    },
    update(name, id, updates) {
      assertCollection(name);
      return updateWithDb(sqlite, name, id, updates || {});
    },
    remove(name, id) {
      assertCollection(name);
      return sqlite.prepare(`DELETE FROM ${quoteIdentifier(storageTable(name))} WHERE id = ?`).run(id).changes > 0;
    },
    raw: sqlite,
  };
  for (const name of collections) {
    Object.defineProperty(context, name, {
      enumerable: true,
      value: Object.freeze({
        findById: (id) => context.findById(name, id),
        findOne: (options) => context.findOne(name, options),
        findMany: (options) => context.findMany(name, options),
        count: (where) => context.count(name, where),
        insert: (item) => context.insert(name, item),
        update: (id, updates) => context.update(name, id, updates),
        remove: (id) => context.remove(name, id),
      }),
    });
  }
  return Object.freeze(context);
}

function transaction(callback, mode = 'immediate') {
  if (typeof callback !== 'function') throw new TypeError('db.transaction requires a callback.');
  ensureDb();
  const sqlite = getDb();
  const runner = sqlite.transaction(() => {
    const result = callback(createTransactionContext(sqlite));
    if (result && typeof result.then === 'function') {
      throw new Error('db.transaction callbacks must be synchronous.');
    }
    return result;
  });
  const execute = runner[mode] || runner.immediate || runner;
  return execute.call(runner);
}

function checkpoint() {
  ensureDb();
  return getDb().pragma('wal_checkpoint(TRUNCATE)');
}

function close() {
  if (_db) {
    try { _db.close(); } finally { _db = null; _ensured = false; }
  }
}

function groupAll(name, field, where = {}) {
  assertCollection(name);
  ensureDb();
  const column = quoteIdentifier(queryColumn(name, field));
  const parameters = [];
  const clauses = Object.entries(where).map(([whereField, condition]) => parseCondition(name, whereField, condition, parameters));
  const whereSql = clauses.length ? ` WHERE ${clauses.join(' AND ')}` : '';
  const rows = getDb().prepare(`SELECT ${column} AS value, COUNT(*) AS total
    FROM ${quoteIdentifier(storageTable(name))}${whereSql} GROUP BY ${column}`).all(...parameters);
  return new Map(rows.map((row) => [row.value, row.total]));
}

function sum(name, field, where = {}) {
  assertCollection(name);
  ensureDb();
  const column = quoteIdentifier(queryColumn(name, field));
  const parameters = [];
  const clauses = Object.entries(where).map(([whereField, condition]) => parseCondition(name, whereField, condition, parameters));
  const whereSql = clauses.length ? ` WHERE ${clauses.join(' AND ')}` : '';
  const result = getDb().prepare(`SELECT COALESCE(SUM(${column}), 0) AS total
    FROM ${quoteIdentifier(storageTable(name))}${whereSql}`).get(...parameters);
  return result.total;
}

function cursorPage(name, { cursor, limit = 25, ...options } = {}) {
  assertCollection(name);
  ensureDb();
  const safeLimit = Math.min(100, Math.max(1, Number.parseInt(limit, 10) || 25));
  const opts = { ...options, limit: safeLimit + 1 };
  if (cursor) {
    const cursorItem = findById(name, cursor);
    if (cursorItem) {
      opts.where = { ...opts.where, createdAt: { $lt: cursorItem.createdAt } };
    }
  }
  const items = findMany(name, opts);
  const hasMore = items.length > safeLimit;
  const pageItems = hasMore ? items.slice(0, safeLimit) : items;
  return {
    items: pageItems,
    nextCursor: hasMore && pageItems.length ? pageItems[pageItems.length - 1].id : null,
    hasMore,
  };
}

function countOptions(name, options = {}) {
  return count(name, options.where || {});
}

module.exports = {
  dbPath,
  collections,
  seoLocations,
  categoryGuides,
  categories,
  getDb,
  ensureDb,
  readDb,
  writeDb,
  collection,
  findById,
  findMany,
  findOne,
  count,
  countOptions,
  groupCount,
  groupAll,
  sum,
  paginate,
  cursorPage,
  insert,
  update,
  remove,
  transaction,
  close,
  checkpoint,
  storageTable,
  queryColumn,
  decodeStoredRow,
};

// ===== src/db/migrations/index.js =====
const { splitItem, tableFor, definitions: relationalDefinitions } = require('../relational');

const CORE_ORDER = [

};

function sqliteType(type) {
  if (type === 'number') return 'REAL';
  if (type === 'integer' || type === 'boolean') return 'INTEGER';
  return 'TEXT';
}

function createSupportingTable(db, name) {
  const config = relationalDefinitions[name];
  const meta = SUPPORT_META[name] || {};
  const columns = Object.entries(config.fields).map(([field, [column, type]]) => {
    const fk = meta.fks && meta.fks[field];
    const reference = fk ? ` REFERENCES "${fk[0]}"(id) ON DELETE ${fk[1]}` : '';
    return `"${column}" ${sqliteType(type)}${reference}`;
  });
  db.exec(`CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS "${tableFor(name)}" (
    id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    ${columns.join(',\n    ')},
    extra_json TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT '{}',
    version INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 1
  )`);
  for (const fields of meta.uniques || []) {
    const columnsSql = fields.map((field) => `"${config.fields[field][0]}"`).join(', ');
    db.exec(`CREATE UNIQUE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS "${tableFor(name)}_${fields.join('_')}_unique" ON "${tableFor(name)}" (${columnsSql})`);
  }
  for (const fields of meta.indexes || []) {
    const columnsSql = fields.map((field) => `"${config.fields[field][0]}"`).join(', ');
    db.exec(`CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS "${tableFor(name)}_${fields.join('_')}_idx" ON "${tableFor(name)}" (${columnsSql})`);
  }
}

function copyLegacyRows(db, names) {
  for (const name of names) {
    const sourceExists = db.prepare("SELECT 1 FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table' AND name = ?").get(name);
    if (!sourceExists) continue;
    const target = tableFor(name);
    const targetCount = db.prepare(`SELECT COUNT(*) AS total FROM "${target}"`).get().total;
    if (targetCount > 0) continue;
    const rows = db.prepare(`SELECT data, version FROM "${name}"`).all();
    for (const source of rows) {
      const item = JSON.parse(source.data);
      const row = splitItem(name, { ...item, version: source.version || 1 });
      const columns = Object.keys(row);
      const statement = db.prepare(`INSERT INTO "${target}" (${columns.map((column) => `"${column}"`).join(', ')}) VALUES (${columns.map(() => '?').join(', ')})`);
      statement.run(...columns.map((column) => row[column]));
    }
  }
}

function ensureMigrationTable(db) {
  db.exec(`CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS schema_migrations (
    version TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    checksum TEXT,
    applied_at TEXT NOT NULL
  )`);
  const columns = new Set(db.prepare('PRAGMA table_info(schema_migrations)').all().map((row) => row.name));
  if (!columns.has('checksum')) db.exec('ALTER TABLE schema_migrations ADD COLUMN checksum TEXT');
}

function inspectPendingMigrations(db) {
  const exists = db.prepare("SELECT 1 FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table' AND name='schema_migrations'").get();
  if (!exists) return [...migrations];
  const applied = new Map(db.prepare('SELECT version, checksum FROM schema_migrations').all().map((row) => [row.version, row.checksum]));
  for (const migration of migrations) {
    const checksum = applied.get(migration.version);
    if (checksum && checksum !== migration.checksum) {
      throw new Error(`Migration checksum mismatch for ${migration.version}. Refusing to continue.`);
    }
  }
  return migrations.filter((migration) => !applied.has(migration.version));
}

function pendingMigrations(db) {
  ensureMigrationTable(db);
  const applied = new Map(db.prepare('SELECT version, checksum FROM schema_migrations').all().map((row) => [row.version, row.checksum]));
  for (const migration of migrations) {
    const checksum = applied.get(migration.version);
    if (checksum && checksum !== migration.checksum) {
      throw new Error(`Migration checksum mismatch for ${migration.version}. Refusing to continue.`);
    }
    if (applied.has(migration.version) && !checksum) {
      db.prepare('UPDATE schema_migrations SET checksum = ? WHERE version = ?').run(migration.checksum, migration.version);
    }
  }
  return migrations.filter((migration) => !applied.has(migration.version));
}

function applyMigrations(db) {
  ensureMigrationTable(db);
  const pending = pendingMigrations(db);
  const run = db.transaction(() => {
    for (const migration of pending) {
      migration.up(db);
      db.prepare('INSERT INTO schema_migrations (version, checksum, applied_at) VALUES (?, ?, ?)')
        .run(migration.version, migration.checksum, new Date().toISOString());
    }
  });
  run.immediate();
  return pending.map((migration) => migration.version);
}

module.exports = { migrations, inspectPendingMigrations, pendingMigrations, applyMigrations, ensureMigrationTable };

function isRelational(name) {
  return Boolean(TABLES[name]);
}

function tableFor(name) {
  return TABLES[name] || name;
}

function definition(name) {
  return definitions[name] || null;
}

function encode(type, value) {
  if (value === undefined || value === null) return null;
  if (type === 'boolean') return value ? 1 : 0;
  if (type === 'number' || type === 'integer') {
    const number = Number(value);
    return Number.isFinite(number) ? number : null;
  }
  if (type === 'json') return JSON.stringify(value);
  return String(value);
}

function decode(type, value) {
  if (value === undefined || value === null) return null;
  if (type === 'boolean') return Boolean(value);
  if (type === 'number' || type === 'integer') return Number(value);
  if (type === 'json') {
    try { return JSON.parse(value); } catch (_error) { return type === 'json' ? [] : value; }
  }
  return value;
}

function splitItem(name, item) {
  const config = definition(name);
  if (!config) throw new Error(`No relational definition for ${name}`);
  const row = { id: item.id, version: Number(item.version || 1) };
  const mapped = new Set(['id', 'version']);
  for (const [field, [column, type]] of Object.entries(config.fields)) {
    row[column] = encode(type, item[field]);
    mapped.add(field);
  }
  const extra = {};
  for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(item || {})) {
    if (!mapped.has(key) && value !== undefined) extra[key] = value;
  }
  row.extra_json = JSON.stringify(extra);
  return row;
}

function itemFromRow(name, row) {
  const config = definition(name);
  if (!config || !row) return null;
  let extra = {};
  try { extra = row.extra_json ? JSON.parse(row.extra_json) : {}; } catch (_error) { extra = {}; }
  const item = { ...extra, id: row.id };
  for (const [field, [column, type]] of Object.entries(config.fields)) {
    const value = decode(type, row[column]);
    if (value !== null || Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(row, column)) item[field] = value;
  }
  return item;
}

function relationalColumn(name, field) {
  if (field === 'id') return 'id';
  const config = definition(name);
  const mapping = config && config.fields[field];
  if (!mapping) return null;
  return mapping[0];
}

module.exports = {
  TABLES,
  definitions,
  isRelational,
  tableFor,
  definition,
  splitItem,
  itemFromRow,
  relationalColumn,
};

const collections = Object.freeze(Object.keys(definitions));

function sqlColumn(field) {
  return field.replace(/[A-Z]/g, (match) => `_${match.toLowerCase()}`);
}

function definition(name) {
  const value = definitions[name];
  if (!value) throw new Error(`Unknown collection: ${name}`);
  return value;
}

function projectedColumns(name) {
  return Object.entries(definition(name).fields).map(([field, type]) => ({ field, column: sqlColumn(field), type }));
}

function columnForField(name, field) {
  if (field === 'id') return 'id';
  const match = projectedColumns(name).find((item) => item.field === field);
  if (!match) throw new Error(`Field ${field} is not queryable on ${name}`);
  return match.column;
}

function dbValue(type, value) {
  if (value === undefined || value === null || value === '') return null;
  if (type === 'INTEGER') return value === true ? 1 : value === false ? 0 : Number(value);
  if (type === 'REAL') {
    const number = Number(value);
    return Number.isFinite(number) ? number : null;
  }
  return String(value);
}

function projectionValues(name, item) {
  return projectedColumns(name).map(({ field, type }) => dbValue(type, item[field]));
}

module.exports = {
  definitions,
  collections,
  definition,
  projectedColumns,
  columnForField,
  projectionValues,
};

// ===== src/domains/admin/adminHelpers.js =====
const db = require('../../repositories/store');
const { addAuditTx } = require('../../services/audit');
const { publicUser } = require('../../services/viewModels');
const { recordsByIds, pageRequest, paginationLinks } = require('../../repositories/queryHelpers');

function page(req, collection, options = {}) {
  const requested = pageRequest(req, { perPage: options.perPage || 30, maxPerPage: 100 });
  const result = db.paginate(collection, {
    ...requested,
    where: options.where || {},
    or: options.or || [],
    orderBy: options.orderBy || { field: 'createdAt', direction: 'desc' },
  });
  return { ...result, pagination: paginationLinks(req, result.pagination) };
}

function userMap(ids) {
  const records = recordsByIds('users', ids);
  return new Map([...records.entries()].map(([id, user]) => [id, publicUser(user)]));
}

function mutateWithAudit(_collections, actorId, action, targetType, targetId, updater, meta = {}) {
  return db.transaction((tx) => {
    const result = updater(tx);
    addAuditTx(tx, actorId, action, targetType, targetId, typeof meta === 'function' ? meta(result) : meta);
    return result;
  });
}

function redirectError(req, res, destination, message) {
  req.flash('error', message);
  return res.redirect(destination);
}

module.exports = { page, userMap, mutateWithAudit, redirectError };

// ===== src/domains/admin/adminRoutes.js =====
const express = require('express');
const { requireAdmin } = require('../../middleware/auth');
const dashboardRoutes = require('./dashboardRoutes');
const marketplaceRoutes = require('./marketplaceRoutes');
const trustSafetyRoutes = require('./trustSafetyRoutes');
const operationsRoutes = require('./operationsRoutes');

const router = express.Router();
router.use(requireAdmin);
router.use(dashboardRoutes);
router.use(marketplaceRoutes);
router.use(trustSafetyRoutes);
router.use(operationsRoutes);

module.exports = router;

// ===== src/domains/admin/dashboardRoutes.js =====
const express = require('express');
const db = require('../../repositories/store');
const { formatDateTime } = require('../../utils/format');

const router = express.Router();

router.get('/', (_req, res) => {
  const flaggedJobs = db.findMany('jobs', {
    or: [{ status: 'review' }, { riskLevel: 'high' }],
    orderBy: { field: 'createdAt', direction: 'desc' },
    limit: 10,
  });
  const openReports = db.findMany('reports', { where: { status: { $ne: 'closed' } }, orderBy: { field: 'createdAt', direction: 'desc' }, limit: 10 });
  const pendingDocuments = db.findMany('documents', { where: { status: 'pending' }, orderBy: { field: 'createdAt', direction: 'desc' }, limit: 10 });
  const pendingPromotions = db.findMany('promotions', { where: { status: 'pending' }, orderBy: { field: 'createdAt', direction: 'desc' }, limit: 10 });
  const openDisputes = db.findMany('disputes', { where: { status: { $ne: 'closed' } }, orderBy: { field: 'createdAt', direction: 'desc' }, limit: 10 });

  return res.render('admin/index', {
    title: 'Admin dashboard',
    stats: {
      users: db.count('users'),
      jobs: db.count('jobs'),
      openJobs: db.count('jobs', { status: 'open' }),
      quotes: db.count('quotes'),
      flaggedJobs: db.countOptions('jobs', { or: [{ status: 'review' }, { riskLevel: 'high' }] }),
      reports: db.count('reports', { status: { $ne: 'closed' } }),
      documents: db.count('documents', { status: 'pending' }),
      promotions: db.count('promotions', { status: 'pending' }),
      payments: db.count('paymentRequests'),
      disputes: db.count('disputes', { status: { $ne: 'closed' } }),
      alerts: db.count('jobAlerts'),
      businesses: db.count('businessAccounts'),
      moderation: db.count('moderationCases', { status: { $ne: 'closed' } }),
      auditLog: db.count('auditLog'),
      legalAcceptances: db.count('legalAcceptances'),
    },
    flaggedJobs,
    openReports,
    pendingDocuments,
    pendingPromotions,
    openDisputes,
    formatDateTime,
  });
});

router.get('/metrics', (_req, res) => {
  const categoryTotals = db.groupAll('jobs', 'categoryId');
  const categoryOpen = new Map(db.groupAll('jobs', 'categoryId', { status: 'open' }).map((row) => [row.value, row.total]));
  const categoryById = new Map(db.categories.map((category) => [category.id, category]));
  const jobsByCategory = categoryTotals.map((row) => ({
    category: categoryById.get(row.value)?.name || row.value || 'Unknown',
    count: row.total,
    open: categoryOpen.get(row.value) || 0,
  }));
  const jobsByCity = db.groupAll('jobs', 'city').map((row) => ({ city: row.value || 'Unknown', count: row.total }));
  const jobs = db.count('jobs');
  const quotes = db.count('quotes');
  const revenueRecords = db.sum('paymentRequests', 'platformFee')
    || db.sum('paymentRequests', 'posterServiceFee')
    || db.sum('paymentRequests', 'workerPlatformFee');
  return res.render('admin/metrics', {
    title: 'Admin metrics',
    totals: {
      users: db.count('users'),
      workers: db.count('workerProfiles'),
      jobs,
      quotes,
      payments: db.count('paymentRequests'),
      disputes: db.count('disputes'),
      revenueRecords,
      quoteRate: jobs ? (quotes / jobs).toFixed(2) : '0.00',
    },
    jobsByCategory,
    jobsByCity,
    formatDateTime,
  });
});

module.exports = router;

// ===== src/domains/admin/marketplaceRoutes.js =====
const express = require('express');
const db = require('../../repositories/store');
const { formatDateTime } = require('../../utils/format');
const { assertTransition } = require('../../services/stateMachine');
const { adminText: validateAdminText } = require('../../services/inputSchemas');
const { publicUser } = require('../../services/viewModels');
const { recordsByIds, recordsByField } = require('../../repositories/queryHelpers');
const jobRepository = require('../../repositories/jobRepository');
const { page, userMap, mutateWithAudit, redirectError } = require('./adminHelpers');

const router = express.Router();

function parsedAdmin(req, res, redirect, statuses) {
  const status = statuses.includes(req.body.status) ? req.body.status : null;
  const parsed = validateAdminText(req.body);
  if (!status || !parsed.success) {
    redirectError(req, res, redirect, status ? parsed.errors.join(' ') : 'Choose a valid status.');
    return null;
  }
  return { status, data: parsed.data };
}

router.get('/jobs', (req, res) => {
  const result = jobRepository.adminPage(req);
  return res.render('admin/jobs', { title: 'Manage jobs', ...result, formatDateTime });
});

router.post('/jobs/:id/status', (req, res) => {
  const parsed = parsedAdmin(req, res, '/admin/jobs', ['review', 'open', 'closed', 'removed', 'hired', 'completed']);
  if (!parsed) return undefined;
  const job = db.findById('jobs', req.params.id);
  if (!job) return redirectError(req, res, '/admin/jobs', 'Job not found.');
  try { assertTransition('job', job.status, parsed.status); } catch (_error) {
    return redirectError(req, res, '/admin/jobs', `Cannot change a job from ${job.status} to ${parsed.status}.`);
  }
  mutateWithAudit(['jobs'], res.locals.currentUser.id, 'admin.job.statusUpdated', 'job', job.id, (tx) => tx.jobs.update(job.id, {
    status: parsed.status,
    adminNotes: parsed.data.adminNotes || job.adminNotes || '',
    updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
  }), { status: parsed.status });
  req.flash('success', 'Job updated.');
  return res.redirect('/admin/jobs');
});

router.get('/users', (req, res) => {
  const result = page(req, 'users', { perPage: 40, orderBy: { field: 'createdAt', direction: 'desc' } });
  const ids = result.items.map((user) => user.id);
  const profiles = recordsByField('workerProfiles', 'userId', ids);
  const businesses = recordsByField('businessAccounts', 'userId', ids);
  const users = result.items.map((user) => ({
    ...user,
    passwordHash: undefined,
    resetTokenHash: undefined,
    profile: profiles.get(user.id),
    business: businesses.get(user.id),
  }));
  return res.render('admin/users', { title: 'Manage users', users, pagination: result.pagination, formatDateTime });
});

router.post('/users/:id/admin', (req, res) => {
  const user = db.findById('users', req.params.id);
  if (!user) return redirectError(req, res, '/admin/users', 'User not found.');
  const nextStatus = ['active', 'suspended', 'deleted', 'service'].includes(req.body.accountStatus) ? req.body.accountStatus : user.accountStatus;
  const nextIsAdmin = req.body.isAdmin === 'on';
  if (user.id === res.locals.currentUser.id && (!nextIsAdmin || nextStatus !== 'active')) {
    return redirectError(req, res, '/admin/users', 'You cannot remove your own admin access or suspend your own account.');
  }
  try { assertTransition('account', user.accountStatus, nextStatus); } catch (_error) {
    return redirectError(req, res, '/admin/users', `Cannot change an account from ${user.accountStatus} to ${nextStatus}.`);
  }
  mutateWithAudit(['users'], res.locals.currentUser.id, 'admin.user.updated', 'user', user.id, (tx) => tx.users.update(user.id, {
    isAdmin: nextIsAdmin,
    phoneVerified: req.body.phoneVerified === 'on',
    accountStatus: nextStatus,
    updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
  }), { accountStatus: nextStatus, isAdmin: nextIsAdmin });
  req.flash('success', 'User updated.');
  return res.redirect('/admin/users');
});

router.get('/promotions', (req, res) => {
  const result = page(req, 'promotions');
  const users = userMap(result.items.map((item) => item.userId));
  const jobs = recordsByIds('jobs', result.items.filter((item) => item.type === 'job-feature').map((item) => item.targetId));
  const profiles = recordsByIds('workerProfiles', result.items.filter((item) => item.type === 'profile-boost').map((item) => item.targetId));
  const promotions = result.items.map((item) => ({ ...item, user: users.get(item.userId), job: jobs.get(item.targetId), profile: profiles.get(item.targetId) }));
  return res.render('admin/promotions', { title: 'Manage promotions', promotions, pagination: result.pagination, formatDateTime });
});

router.post('/promotions/:id/status', (req, res) => {
  const parsed = parsedAdmin(req, res, '/admin/promotions', ['pending', 'active', 'rejected', 'expired']);
  if (!parsed) return undefined;
  const promotion = db.findById('promotions', req.params.id);
  if (!promotion) return redirectError(req, res, '/admin/promotions', 'Promotion not found.');
  try { assertTransition('promotion', promotion.status, parsed.status); } catch (_error) {
    return redirectError(req, res, '/admin/promotions', `Cannot change a promotion from ${promotion.status} to ${parsed.status}.`);
  }
  db.transaction((tx) => {
    const target = tx.promotions.findById(promotion.id);
    const wasActive = target.status === 'active';
    const now = new Date().toISOString();
    const updates = {
      status: parsed.status,
      paymentStatus: String(req.body.paymentStatus || target.paymentStatus || 'demo-unpaid').slice(0, 100),
      adminNotes: parsed.data.adminNotes || target.adminNotes || '',
      updatedAt: now,
    };
    if (parsed.status === 'active' && !wasActive) {
      const endDate = new Date();
      endDate.setDate(endDate.getDate() + Number(target.durationDays || 7));
      updates.startsAt = now;
      updates.endsAt = endDate.toISOString();
      if (target.type === 'job-feature') tx.jobs.update(target.targetId, { featuredUntil: updates.endsAt, updatedAt: now });
      if (target.type === 'profile-boost') tx.workerProfiles.update(target.targetId, { boostedUntil: updates.endsAt, updatedAt: now });
    }
    tx.promotions.update(target.id, updates);
    const { addAuditTx } = require('../../services/audit');
    addAuditTx(tx, res.locals.currentUser.id, 'admin.promotion.statusUpdated', 'promotion', target.id, { status: parsed.status });
  });
  req.flash('success', 'Promotion updated.');
  return res.redirect('/admin/promotions');
});

router.get('/alerts', (req, res) => {
  const result = page(req, 'jobAlerts');
  const users = userMap(result.items.map((item) => item.userId));
  return res.render('admin/alerts', { title: 'Job alerts', alerts: result.items.map((item) => ({ ...item, user: users.get(item.userId) })), pagination: result.pagination, formatDateTime });
});

router.get('/businesses', (req, res) => {
  const result = page(req, 'businessAccounts');
  const users = userMap(result.items.map((item) => item.userId));
  return res.render('admin/businesses', { title: 'Business accounts', businesses: result.items.map((item) => ({ ...item, user: users.get(item.userId) })), pagination: result.pagination, formatDateTime });
});

module.exports = router;

// ===== src/domains/admin/operationsRoutes.js =====
const express = require('express');
const db = require('../../repositories/store');
const { formatDateTime } = require('../../utils/format');
const { assertTransition } = require('../../services/stateMachine');
const { adminText: validateAdminText } = require('../../services/inputSchemas');
const { recordsByIds } = require('../../repositories/queryHelpers');
const { page, userMap, redirectError } = require('./adminHelpers');

const router = express.Router();

router.get('/payments', (req, res) => {
  const result = page(req, 'paymentRequests');
  const jobs = recordsByIds('jobs', result.items.map((item) => item.jobId));
  const quotes = recordsByIds('quotes', result.items.map((item) => item.quoteId));
  const users = userMap(result.items.flatMap((item) => [item.posterId, item.workerId]));
  const payments = result.items.map((item) => ({ ...item, job: jobs.get(item.jobId), quote: quotes.get(item.quoteId), poster: users.get(item.posterId), worker: users.get(item.workerId) }));
  return res.render('admin/payments', { title: 'Manage payments', payments, pagination: result.pagination, formatDateTime });
});

router.post('/payments/:id/status', (req, res) => {
  const statuses = ['requested', 'invoice-sent', 'authorized-demo', 'external-paid', 'released', 'cancelled', 'refunded-demo'];
  const nextStatus = statuses.includes(req.body.status) ? req.body.status : null;
  const parsed = validateAdminText(req.body);
  if (!nextStatus || !parsed.success) return redirectError(req, res, '/admin/payments', nextStatus ? parsed.errors.join(' ') : 'Choose a valid payment status.');
  const payment = db.findById('paymentRequests', req.params.id);
  if (!payment) return redirectError(req, res, '/admin/payments', 'Payment record not found.');
  try { assertTransition('payment', payment.status, nextStatus); } catch (_error) {
    return redirectError(req, res, '/admin/payments', `Cannot change a payment from ${payment.status} to ${nextStatus}.`);
  }
  db.update('paymentRequests', payment.id, {
    status: nextStatus,
    paymentReference: parsed.data.paymentReference || payment.paymentReference || '',
    note: parsed.data.note || payment.note || '',
    releasedAt: nextStatus === 'released' ? payment.releasedAt || new Date().toISOString() : payment.releasedAt,
    paidAt: nextStatus === 'external-paid' ? payment.paidAt || new Date().toISOString() : payment.paidAt,
  });
  req.flash('success', 'Payment record updated.');
  return res.redirect('/admin/payments');
});

router.get('/audit', (req, res) => {
  const result = page(req, 'auditLog', { perPage: 50 });
  const actors = userMap(result.items.map((item) => item.actorId));
  return res.render('admin/audit', { title: 'Audit log', auditLog: result.items.map((item) => ({ ...item, actor: actors.get(item.actorId) })), pagination: result.pagination, formatDateTime });
});

router.get('/compliance', (req, res) => {
  const result = page(req, 'legalAcceptances', { perPage: 50, orderBy: { field: 'acceptedAt', direction: 'desc' } });
  const users = userMap(result.items.map((item) => item.userId));
  const acceptances = result.items.map((item) => ({ ...item, user: users.get(item.userId) }));
  const documentVersions = [
    { type: 'terms', version: '2026-05-31', purpose: 'General marketplace terms' },
    { type: 'privacy', version: '2026-05-31', purpose: 'PIPEDA-style privacy consent summary' },
    { type: 'posterAgreement', version: '2026-05-31', purpose: 'Poster responsibility and worker-classification acknowledgement' },
    { type: 'workerAgreement', version: '2026-05-31', purpose: 'Independent worker acknowledgement' },
    { type: 'safetyAcknowledgement', version: '2026-05-31', purpose: 'Worksite hazards and regulated-trade warning' },
  ];
  return res.render('admin/compliance', { title: 'Compliance centre', acceptances, pagination: result.pagination, documentVersions, formatDateTime });
});

module.exports = router;

// ===== src/domains/admin/trustSafetyRoutes.js =====
const express = require('express');
const db = require('../../repositories/store');
const { formatDateTime } = require('../../utils/format');
const { assertTransition } = require('../../services/stateMachine');
const { adminText: validateAdminText } = require('../../services/inputSchemas');
const { recordsByIds, recordsByField } = require('../../repositories/queryHelpers');
const { page, userMap, mutateWithAudit, redirectError } = require('./adminHelpers');

const router = express.Router();

function validateStatus(req, res, redirect, values) {
  const status = values.includes(req.body.status) ? req.body.status : null;
  const parsed = validateAdminText(req.body);
  if (!status || !parsed.success) {
    redirectError(req, res, redirect, status ? parsed.errors.join(' ') : 'Choose a valid status.');
    return null;
  }
  return { status, data: parsed.data };
}

router.get('/reports', (req, res) => {
  const result = page(req, 'reports');
  const users = userMap(result.items.flatMap((item) => [item.reporterId, item.reportedUserId]));
  const jobs = recordsByIds('jobs', result.items.map((item) => item.jobId));
  const reports = result.items.map((item) => ({ ...item, reporter: users.get(item.reporterId), reportedUser: users.get(item.reportedUserId), job: jobs.get(item.jobId) }));
  return res.render('admin/reports', { title: 'Manage reports', reports, pagination: result.pagination, formatDateTime });
});

router.post('/reports/:id/status', (req, res) => {
  const parsed = validateStatus(req, res, '/admin/reports', ['open', 'reviewing', 'closed']);
  if (!parsed) return undefined;
  const record = db.findById('reports', req.params.id);
  if (!record) return redirectError(req, res, '/admin/reports', 'Report not found.');
  try { assertTransition('report', record.status, parsed.status); } catch (_error) {
    return redirectError(req, res, '/admin/reports', `Cannot change a report from ${record.status} to ${parsed.status}.`);
  }
  db.update('reports', record.id, { status: parsed.status, adminNotes: parsed.data.adminNotes || record.adminNotes || '' });
  req.flash('success', 'Report updated.');
  return res.redirect('/admin/reports');
});

router.get('/documents', (req, res) => {
  const result = page(req, 'documents');
  const users = userMap(result.items.map((item) => item.workerId));
  const profiles = recordsByField('workerProfiles', 'userId', result.items.map((item) => item.workerId));
  const documents = result.items.map((item) => ({ ...item, worker: users.get(item.workerId), profile: profiles.get(item.workerId) }));
  return res.render('admin/documents', { title: 'Verify documents', documents, pagination: result.pagination, formatDateTime });
});

router.post('/documents/:id/status', (req, res) => {
  const parsed = validateStatus(req, res, '/admin/documents', ['pending', 'verified', 'rejected', 'expired']);
  if (!parsed) return undefined;
  const document = db.findById('documents', req.params.id);
  if (!document) return redirectError(req, res, '/admin/documents', 'Document not found.');
  try { assertTransition('document', document.status, parsed.status); } catch (_error) {
    return redirectError(req, res, '/admin/documents', `Cannot change a document from ${document.status} to ${parsed.status}.`);
  }
  mutateWithAudit(['documents', 'workerProfiles'], res.locals.currentUser.id, 'admin.document.statusUpdated', 'document', document.id, (tx) => {
    const now = new Date().toISOString();
    const target = tx.documents.update(document.id, {
      status: parsed.status,
      adminNotes: parsed.data.adminNotes || document.adminNotes || '',
      reviewedBy: res.locals.currentUser.id,
      updatedAt: now,
    });
    const profile = tx.workerProfiles.findOne({ where: { userId: target.workerId } });
    if (profile) {
      const field = target.type === 'insurance' ? 'insuranceStatus' : target.type === 'wsib' ? 'wsibStatus' : target.type === 'trade_certificate' ? 'tradeCertificationStatus' : null;
      const profileUpdates = { updatedAt: now };
      if (field) profileUpdates[field] = target.status === 'verified' ? 'verified' : ['rejected', 'expired'].includes(target.status) ? 'not-provided' : profile[field];
      if (target.status === 'verified') profileUpdates.verificationLevel = 'verified-documents';
      tx.workerProfiles.update(profile.id, profileUpdates);
    }
    return target;
  }, { status: parsed.status, type: document.type });
  req.flash('success', 'Document status updated.');
  return res.redirect('/admin/documents');
});

router.get('/disputes', (req, res) => {
  const result = page(req, 'disputes');
  const users = userMap(result.items.flatMap((item) => [item.openedById, item.respondentId]));
  const jobs = recordsByIds('jobs', result.items.map((item) => item.jobId));
  const payments = recordsByIds('paymentRequests', result.items.map((item) => item.paymentRequestId));
  const disputes = result.items.map((item) => ({ ...item, job: jobs.get(item.jobId), payment: payments.get(item.paymentRequestId), openedBy: users.get(item.openedById), respondent: users.get(item.respondentId) }));
  return res.render('admin/disputes', { title: 'Manage disputes', disputes, pagination: result.pagination, formatDateTime });
});

router.post('/disputes/:id/status', (req, res) => {
  const parsed = validateStatus(req, res, '/admin/disputes', ['open', 'reviewing', 'waiting-on-poster', 'waiting-on-worker', 'resolved', 'closed']);
  if (!parsed) return undefined;
  const record = db.findById('disputes', req.params.id);
  if (!record) return redirectError(req, res, '/admin/disputes', 'Dispute not found.');
  try { assertTransition('dispute', record.status, parsed.status); } catch (_error) {
    return redirectError(req, res, '/admin/disputes', `Cannot change a dispute from ${record.status} to ${parsed.status}.`);
  }
  db.update('disputes', record.id, {
    status: parsed.status,
    adminNotes: parsed.data.adminNotes || record.adminNotes || '',
    resolution: parsed.data.resolution || record.resolution || '',
    resolvedAt: ['resolved', 'closed'].includes(parsed.status) ? new Date().toISOString() : record.resolvedAt,
  });
  req.flash('success', 'Dispute updated.');
  return res.redirect('/admin/disputes');
});

router.get('/moderation', (req, res) => {
  const result = page(req, 'moderationCases');
  const users = userMap(result.items.map((item) => item.assignedToId));
  const jobs = recordsByIds('jobs', result.items.filter((item) => item.targetType === 'job').map((item) => item.targetId));
  const templates = recordsByIds('recurringTaskTemplates', result.items.filter((item) => item.targetType === 'recurringTaskTemplate').map((item) => item.targetId));
  const messages = recordsByIds('messages', result.items.filter((item) => item.targetType === 'message').map((item) => item.targetId));
  const cases = result.items.map((item) => ({ ...item, actor: users.get(item.assignedToId), job: jobs.get(item.targetId), template: templates.get(item.targetId), message: messages.get(item.targetId) }));
  return res.render('admin/moderation', { title: 'Moderation cases', cases, pagination: result.pagination, formatDateTime });
});

router.post('/moderation/:id/status', (req, res) => {
  const parsed = validateStatus(req, res, '/admin/moderation', ['open', 'reviewing', 'needs-edits', 'escalated', 'closed']);
  if (!parsed) return undefined;
  const record = db.findById('moderationCases', req.params.id);
  if (!record) return redirectError(req, res, '/admin/moderation', 'Moderation case not found.');
  try { assertTransition('moderation', record.status, parsed.status); } catch (_error) {
    return redirectError(req, res, '/admin/moderation', `Cannot change a moderation case from ${record.status} to ${parsed.status}.`);
  }
  const priority = ['low', 'normal', 'high', 'urgent'].includes(req.body.priority) ? req.body.priority : record.priority || 'normal';
  mutateWithAudit(['moderationCases'], res.locals.currentUser.id, 'admin.moderation.statusUpdated', 'moderationCase', record.id, (tx) => tx.moderationCases.update(record.id, {
    status: parsed.status,
    priority,
    assignedToId: res.locals.currentUser.id,
    adminNotes: parsed.data.adminNotes || record.adminNotes || '',
    updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
  }), { status: parsed.status, priority });
  req.flash('success', 'Moderation case updated.');
  return res.redirect('/admin/moderation');
});

module.exports = router;

// ===== src/domains/auth/authRoutes.js =====
const express = require('express');
const bcrypt = require('bcryptjs');
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const db = require('../../repositories/store');
const { compact } = require('../../utils/format');
const { validateCsrf } = require('../../middleware/csrf');
const { normalizeEmail, isStrongPassword, regenerateSession, publicBaseUrl } = require('../../utils/security');
const {
  issueTokenTx,
  findValidTokenTx,
  consumeTokenTx,
  revokeUserTokensTx,
  pruneTokensTx,
} = require('../../services/tokenService');
const { sendEmail } = require('../../utils/mailer');
const { invalidateUserSessions } = require('../../services/sessionSecurity');
const { acceptLegalTx } = require('../../services/audit');
const { registration: validateRegistration } = require('../../services/inputSchemas');

const router = express.Router();
const rateLimitHandler = (req, res) => {
  req.flash('error', 'Too many attempts. Try again later.');
  res.redirect('/auth/login');
};
const limiter = (max) => rateLimit({ windowMs: 10 * 60 * 1000, max, standardHeaders: true, legacyHeaders: false, handler: rateLimitHandler });
const loginLimiter = limiter(10);
const registerLimiter = limiter(5);
const forgotLimiter = limiter(5);
const completeRegLimiter = limiter(10);

function validToken(rawToken, purpose) {
  if (!rawToken) return null;
  return db.transaction((tx) => findValidTokenTx(tx, rawToken, purpose), 'deferred');
}

router.get('/register', (_req, res) => res.render('auth/register', { title: 'Create account', formData: {} }));

router.post('/register', registerLimiter, validateCsrf, async (req, res, next) => {
  try {
    const parsed = validateRegistration(req.body);
    if (!parsed.success) {
      req.flash('error', parsed.errors.join(' '));
      return res.redirect('/auth/register');
    }
    const { name, email, phone, password, role, city, postalCode } = parsed.data;
    const existing = db.findOne('users', { where: { email } });
    if (existing && existing.accountStatus !== 'deleted') {
      req.flash('error', 'An account with that email already exists.');
      return res.redirect('/auth/register');
    }
    const now = new Date().toISOString();
    const user = {
      id: uuidv4(), name: compact(name), email, phone: compact(phone),
      passwordHash: await bcrypt.hash(password, 12), role, city: compact(city),
      postalCode: compact(postalCode).toUpperCase(), isAdmin: false, phoneVerified: false,
      accountStatus: 'active', createdAt: now, updatedAt: now,
    };
    db.transaction((tx) => {
      tx.users.insert(user);
      acceptLegalTx(tx, user.id, 'terms', '2026-05-31', 'registration');
      acceptLegalTx(tx, user.id, 'privacy', '2026-05-31', 'registration');
      if (['worker', 'both'].includes(user.role)) {
        tx.workerProfiles.insert({
          id: uuidv4(), userId: user.id, displayName: user.name, bio: '', skills: [], tools: [],
          hourlyRate: null, minimumBooking: null, hasVehicle: false, availability: '', serviceRadiusKm: null,
          insuranceStatus: 'not-provided', wsibStatus: 'not-provided', tradeCertificationStatus: 'not-provided',
          verificationLevel: 'none', onboardingCompleted: false, complianceAcceptedAt: null,
          portfolioPhotos: [], createdAt: now, updatedAt: now,
        });
      }
    });
    await regenerateSession(req, user.id);
    req.flash('success', 'Account created.');
    return res.redirect('/dashboard');
  } catch (error) { return next(error); }
});

router.get('/login', (_req, res) => res.render('auth/login', { title: 'Log in' }));

router.post('/login', loginLimiter, validateCsrf, async (req, res, next) => {
  try {
    const user = db.findOne('users', { where: { email: normalizeEmail(req.body.email) } });
    if (!user || !user.passwordHash || !(await bcrypt.compare(req.body.password || '', user.passwordHash))) {
      req.flash('error', 'Invalid email or password.');
      return res.redirect('/auth/login');
    }
    if (user.accountStatus !== 'active') {
      req.flash('error', 'This account is not currently active. Contact support if you believe this is an error.');
      return res.redirect('/auth/login');
    }
    await regenerateSession(req, user.id);
    req.flash('success', 'Logged in.');
    return res.redirect('/dashboard');
  } catch (error) { return next(error); }
});

router.get('/complete-registration', (req, res) => {
  const rawToken = compact(req.query.token) || req.session.pendingClaimToken;
  if (!rawToken) return res.redirect('/auth/login');
  if (!validToken(rawToken, 'claim_guest_account')) {
    req.flash('error', 'That account-claim link is invalid or expired.');
    return res.redirect('/auth/register');
  }
  return res.render('auth/completeRegistration', { title: 'Complete registration', userId: rawToken, token: rawToken, formData: {} });
});

router.post('/complete-registration', completeRegLimiter, validateCsrf, async (req, res, next) => {
  try {
    const rawToken = compact(req.body.token) || compact(req.body.userId) || req.session.pendingClaimToken;
    const name = compact(req.body.name);
    const password = req.body.password;
    if (!rawToken || !name || !isStrongPassword(password)) {
      req.flash('error', 'Name and a 10+ character password with upper-case, lower-case, and a number are required.');
      return res.redirect(`/auth/complete-registration?token=${encodeURIComponent(rawToken || '')}`);
    }
    const preview = validToken(rawToken, 'claim_guest_account');
    const guest = preview ? db.findById('users', preview.userId) : null;
    if (!guest || guest.accountStatus !== 'guest') {
      req.flash('error', 'That account-claim link is invalid or expired.');
      return res.redirect('/auth/register');
    }
    const claimedEmail = normalizeEmail(guest.contactEmail || guest.email);
    const duplicate = claimedEmail ? db.findOne('users', { where: { email: claimedEmail } }) : null;
    if (duplicate && duplicate.id !== guest.id && duplicate.accountStatus !== 'deleted') {
      req.flash('error', 'That email is already linked to an account. Log in to the existing account or contact support.');
      return res.redirect('/auth/login');
    }
    const passwordHash = await bcrypt.hash(password, 12);
    const user = db.transaction((tx) => {
      const token = consumeTokenTx(tx, rawToken, 'claim_guest_account');
      const target = token && tx.users.findById(token.userId);
      if (!target || target.accountStatus !== 'guest') return null;
      const updated = tx.users.update(target.id, {
        name,
        email: claimedEmail,
        phone: compact(target.contactPhone || target.phone),
        contactEmail: undefined,
        contactPhone: undefined,
        passwordHash,
        accountStatus: 'active',
        updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      });
      pruneTokensTx(tx);
      return updated;
    });
    if (!user) {
      req.flash('error', 'That account-claim link is invalid or expired.');
      return res.redirect('/auth/register');
    }
    delete req.session.pendingClaimToken;
    await regenerateSession(req, user.id);
    req.flash('success', 'Account claimed. You can now manage your tasks.');
    return res.redirect('/dashboard');
  } catch (error) { return next(error); }
});

router.post('/logout', validateCsrf, (req, res) => {
  req.session.destroy((error) => {
    res.clearCookie('neighbourtask.sid');
    return res.redirect(error ? '/' : '/');
  });
});

router.get('/forgot-password', (_req, res) => res.render('auth/forgotPassword', { title: 'Forgot password' }));

router.post('/forgot-password', forgotLimiter, validateCsrf, async (req, res, next) => {
  try {
    const user = db.findOne('users', { where: { email: normalizeEmail(req.body.email), accountStatus: 'active' } });
    if (user) {
      const rawToken = db.transaction((tx) => {
        revokeUserTokensTx(tx, user.id, 'password_reset');
        const issued = issueTokenTx(tx, { userId: user.id, purpose: 'password_reset', ttlMinutes: 60 });
        pruneTokensTx(tx);
        return issued.rawToken;
      });
      const resetUrl = `${publicBaseUrl(req)}/auth/reset-password/${encodeURIComponent(rawToken)}`;
      await sendEmail({
        to: user.email,
        subject: '[NeighbourTask] Reset your password',
        text: `Use this one-time link within 60 minutes to reset your password:\n\n${resetUrl}\n\nIf you did not request this, ignore this email.`,
      }).catch((error) => console.error('[password-reset-email]', error.message));
      if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'production' && !process.env.SMTP_HOST) req.flash('info', `Development reset link: ${resetUrl}`);
    }
    req.flash('success', 'If that email exists, a reset link has been sent.');
    return res.redirect('/auth/login');
  } catch (error) { return next(error); }
});

router.get('/reset-password/:token', (req, res) => {
  if (!validToken(req.params.token, 'password_reset')) {
    req.flash('error', 'Invalid or expired reset link.');
    return res.redirect('/auth/forgot-password');
  }
  return res.render('auth/resetPassword', { title: 'Reset password', token: req.params.token });
});

router.post('/reset-password/:token', completeRegLimiter, validateCsrf, async (req, res, next) => {
  try {
    const password = req.body.password;
    if (!isStrongPassword(password) || password !== req.body.confirm) {
      req.flash('error', 'Passwords must match and use 10+ characters with upper-case, lower-case, and a number.');
      return res.redirect(`/auth/reset-password/${encodeURIComponent(req.params.token)}`);
    }
    const passwordHash = await bcrypt.hash(password, 12);
    const userId = db.transaction((tx) => {
      const token = consumeTokenTx(tx, req.params.token, 'password_reset');
      const user = token && tx.users.findById(token.userId);
      if (!user || user.accountStatus !== 'active') return null;
      tx.users.update(user.id, { passwordHash, updatedAt: new Date().toISOString() });
      revokeUserTokensTx(tx, user.id, 'password_reset');
      pruneTokensTx(tx);
      return user.id;
    });
    if (!userId) {
      req.flash('error', 'Invalid or expired reset link.');
      return res.redirect('/auth/forgot-password');
    }
    invalidateUserSessions(userId);
    req.flash('success', 'Password reset. Log in with your new password.');
    return res.redirect('/auth/login');
  } catch (error) { return next(error); }
});

module.exports = router;
