// ===== src/domains/drafts/draftRoutes.js =====
const express = require('express');
const { requireAuthApi } = require('../../middleware/auth');
const draftRepository = require('../../repositories/draftRepository');

const router = express.Router();
const MAX_FIELDS = 80;
const MAX_PAYLOAD_BYTES = 64 * 1024;

router.use(requireAuthApi);

function cleanPayload(input) {
  if (!input || typeof input !== 'object' || Array.isArray(input)) return null;
  const entries = Object.entries(input);
  if (entries.length > MAX_FIELDS) return null;
  const payload = {};
  for (const [key, raw] of entries) {
    if (!/^[a-zA-Z0-9_.:[\]-]{1,100}$/.test(key)) return null;
    if (Array.isArray(raw)) {
      if (raw.length > 50 || raw.some((value) => String(value).length > 5000)) return null;
      payload[key] = raw.map((value) => String(value));
    } else if (['string', 'number', 'boolean'].includes(typeof raw)) {
      const value = String(raw);
      if (value.length > 10000) return null;
      payload[key] = value;
    } else if (raw === null) {
      payload[key] = '';
    } else {
      return null;
    }
  }
  return Buffer.byteLength(JSON.stringify(payload), 'utf8') <= MAX_PAYLOAD_BYTES ? payload : null;
}

router.get('/:kind', (req, res) => {
  const draft = draftRepository.findForUser(req.currentUser.id, req.params.kind);
  if (!draft) return res.status(404).json({ draft: null });
  return res.json({
    draft: {
      kind: draft.kind,
      route: draft.route,
      values: draft.payload || {},
      savedAt: draft.updatedAt,
      expiresAt: draft.expiresAt,
    },
  });
});

router.put('/:kind', (req, res) => {
  const payload = cleanPayload(req.body && req.body.values);
  if (!payload) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'The draft is too large or contains unsupported fields.' });
  const draft = draftRepository.saveForUser({
    userId: req.currentUser.id,
    kind: req.params.kind,
    route: req.body && req.body.route,
    payload,
  });
  return res.json({ savedAt: draft.updatedAt, expiresAt: draft.expiresAt });
});

router.delete('/:kind', (req, res) => {
  draftRepository.removeForUser(req.currentUser.id, req.params.kind);
  return res.status(204).end();
});

module.exports = router;

// ===== src/domains/jobs/browseRoutes.js =====
const express = require('express');
const db = require('../../repositories/store');
const { canViewJob } = require('../../services/accessPolicy');
const { formatDate, formatDateTime } = require('../../utils/format');
const jobRepository = require('../../repositories/jobRepository');
const { lifecycleForJob } = require('../../services/jobLifecycle');

const router = express.Router();

router.get('/', (req, res) => {
  const currentUser = res.locals.currentUser;
  const currentProfile = currentUser ? db.findOne('workerProfiles', { where: { userId: currentUser.id } }) : null;
  const result = jobRepository.browse(req, currentUser, currentProfile);
  return res.render('jobs/index', {
    title: 'Browse jobs', jobs: result.jobs, filters: req.query, formatDate, currentProfile, pagination: result.pagination,
  });
});

router.get('/:id', (req, res) => {
  const currentUser = res.locals.currentUser;
  const result = jobRepository.detail(req.params.id, currentUser);
  if (!result || !canViewJob(currentUser, result.job)) return res.status(404).render('pages/404', { title: 'Job not found' });
  return res.render('jobs/show', {
    title: result.job.title,
    ...result,
    lifecycle: lifecycleForJob(result.job),
    formatDate,
    formatDateTime,
    guestQuoteCount: currentUser ? null : ((req.session.guestQuotes && req.session.guestQuotes[result.job.id]) || 0),
  });
});

module.exports = router;

// ===== src/domains/jobs/completionRoutes.js =====
const express = require('express');
const { requireAuth } = require('../../middleware/auth');
const { completeJob, confirmCompletion, WorkflowError } = require('../../services/jobWorkflow');

const router = express.Router();
router.post('/:id/complete', requireAuth, (req, res, next) => {
  try {
    completeJob({ jobId: req.params.id, actor: res.locals.currentUser });
    req.flash('success', 'Job marked completed. You can now leave a review.');
    return res.redirect(`/jobs/${req.params.id}`);
  } catch (error) {
    if (error instanceof WorkflowError || error.code === 'INVALID_STATE_TRANSITION') {
      req.flash('error', error.message);
      return res.redirect(error.code === 'NOT_FOUND' ? '/dashboard' : `/jobs/${req.params.id}`);
    }
    return next(error);
  }
});
router.post('/:id/completion-confirmation', requireAuth, (req, res, next) => {
  try {
    const result = confirmCompletion({ jobId: req.params.id, actor: res.locals.currentUser, notes: req.body.notes });
    req.flash('success', result.bothConfirmed ? 'Job completed by both sides.' : 'Completion confirmation recorded.');
    return res.redirect(`/jobs/${req.params.id}`);
  } catch (error) {
    if (error instanceof WorkflowError || error.code === 'INVALID_STATE_TRANSITION') {
      req.flash('error', error.message);
      return res.redirect(error.code === 'FORBIDDEN' ? '/dashboard' : `/jobs/${req.params.id}`);
    }
    return next(error);
  }
});
module.exports = router;

// ===== src/domains/jobs/jobRoutes.js =====
const express = require('express');

module.exports = router;

// ===== src/domains/jobs/postingRoutes.js =====
const express = require('express');
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const db = require('../../repositories/store');
const upload = require('../../middleware/upload');
const { handleMulterError } = require('../../middleware/upload');
const { requireAuth } = require('../../middleware/auth');
const { validateCsrf, validateMultipartCsrf } = require('../../middleware/csrf');
const { issueTokenTx } = require('../../services/tokenService');
const { normalizeEmail, publicBaseUrl, safeRedirectTarget } = require('../../utils/security');
const { discardUploadedFiles } = require('../../utils/uploads');
const { validEmail } = require('../../services/validation');
const { createJobTx, JobInputError } = require('../../services/jobService');
const { compact } = require('../../utils/format');
const { sendEmail } = require('../../utils/mailer');
const { improveJobPost } = require('../../services/postAssistant');

const router = express.Router();
const quickPostLimiter = rateLimit({
  windowMs: 60 * 1000, max: 5, standardHeaders: true, legacyHeaders: false,
  handler: (req, res) => {
    req.flash('error', 'Too many attempts. Try again in a minute.');
    res.redirect(safeRedirectTarget(req, req.get('Referrer'), '/jobs/quick'));
  },
});

router.get('/quick', (_req, res) => res.render('jobs/quickNew', { title: 'Quick post a task', autosave: { key: 'quick-job', enabled: true } }));

router.post('/quick', quickPostLimiter, validateCsrf, async (req, res, next) => {
  try {
    const currentUser = res.locals.currentUser;
    const email = normalizeEmail(req.body.email);
    const phone = compact(req.body.phone);
    if (!currentUser && !email && !phone) {
      req.flash('error', 'Provide an email or phone number so you can claim and manage the task.');
      return res.redirect('/jobs/quick');
    }
    if (email && !validEmail(email)) {
      req.flash('error', 'Enter a valid email address.');
      return res.redirect('/jobs/quick');
    }
    const existingAccount = !currentUser ? db.findOne('users', {
      where: { accountStatus: { $ne: 'guest' } },
      or: [email ? { email } : null, phone ? { phone } : null].filter(Boolean),
    }) : null;
    if (existingAccount) {
      req.flash('info', 'Please log in to post using that contact information.');
      return res.redirect('/auth/login');
    }
    const result = db.transaction((tx) => {
      const now = new Date().toISOString();
      const user = currentUser || {
        id: uuidv4(), email: '', phone: '', contactEmail: email, contactPhone: phone,
        name: 'Guest poster', passwordHash: '', role: 'poster', city: compact(req.body.city),
        postalCode: '', isAdmin: false, phoneVerified: false, accountStatus: 'guest', createdAt: now, updatedAt: now,
      };
      if (!currentUser) tx.users.insert(user);
      const categoryId = db.categories.some((category) => category.id === compact(req.body.categoryId))
        ? compact(req.body.categoryId) : 'general-labour';
      const riskFlags = Array.isArray(req.body.riskFlags) ? req.body.riskFlags : req.body.riskFlags ? [req.body.riskFlags] : [];
      const job = createJobTx(tx, {
        posterId: user.id,
        input: {
          title: compact(req.body.title), description: compact(req.body.description), categoryId,
          city: compact(req.body.city), postalCode: '', locationVisibility: 'neighbourhood',
          payType: 'quote', urgency: 'flexible', riskFlags,
        },
      });
      if (currentUser) return { job, rawToken: null };
      const issued = issueTokenTx(tx, { userId: user.id, purpose: 'claim_guest_account', ttlMinutes: 24 * 60, meta: { jobId: job.id } });
      return { job, rawToken: issued.rawToken };
    });
    const { job, rawToken } = result;
    if (currentUser) {
      req.flash(job.status === 'review' ? 'info' : 'success', job.status === 'review' ? 'Your task was submitted for safety review.' : 'Your task is live.');
      return res.redirect(`/jobs/${job.id}`);
    }
    let canClaimInCurrentBrowser = !email;
    if (email) {
      const claimUrl = `${publicBaseUrl(req)}/auth/complete-registration?token=${encodeURIComponent(rawToken)}`;
      try {
        await sendEmail({ to: email, subject: '[NeighbourTask] Claim your task', text: `Use this one-time link within 24 hours to claim and manage your task:\n\n${claimUrl}` });
      } catch (_error) {
        req.flash('error', 'The task was saved, but the claim email could not be delivered. Contact support to recover it.');
      }
      canClaimInCurrentBrowser = process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'production' && !process.env.SMTP_HOST;
    }
    if (canClaimInCurrentBrowser) req.session.pendingClaimToken = rawToken;
    req.flash(job.status === 'review' ? 'info' : 'success', email
      ? 'Task submitted. Check your email for the secure account-claim link.'
      : 'Task submitted. Complete registration in this browser to manage it.');
    return canClaimInCurrentBrowser ? res.redirect('/auth/complete-registration') : res.redirect(`/jobs/${job.id}`);
  } catch (error) {
    if (error instanceof JobInputError) { req.flash('error', error.message); return res.redirect('/jobs/quick'); }
    return next(error);
  }
});

router.get('/assist', requireAuth, (_req, res) => res.render('jobs/new', {
  title: 'Post a task with guided assistance', assistedMode: true, autosave: { key: 'assisted-job', enabled: true },
}));

router.post('/assist', requireAuth, validateCsrf, (req, res) => {
  req.session.assistedJobDraft = improveJobPost(req.body);
  req.flash('info', 'We improved the structure of your task. Review every field before publishing.');
  return res.redirect('/jobs/new');
});

router.get('/new', requireAuth, (req, res) => {
  const assistedDraft = req.session.assistedJobDraft || null;
  delete req.session.assistedJobDraft;
  return res.render('jobs/new', {
    title: 'Post a task', assistedDraft, autosave: { key: 'new-job', enabled: true },
  });
});

router.post('/', requireAuth, upload.array('photos', 6), handleMulterError('/jobs/new'), validateMultipartCsrf, (req, res, next) => {
  const photos = (req.files || []).map((file) => `/uploads/${file.filename}`);
  try {
    const job = db.transaction((tx) => createJobTx(tx, {
      posterId: res.locals.currentUser.id,
      input: req.body,
      photos,
    }));
    req.flash(job.status === 'review' ? 'info' : 'success', job.status === 'review'
      ? 'Your task was saved for admin review because it may involve regulated or safety-sensitive work.'
      : 'Your task is live.');
    return res.redirect(`/jobs/${job.id}`);
  } catch (error) {
    discardUploadedFiles(req);
    if (error instanceof JobInputError) { req.flash('error', error.message); return res.redirect('/jobs/new'); }
    return next(error);
  }
});

module.exports = router;

// ===== src/domains/jobs/quoteRoutes.js =====
const express = require('express');
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');
const db = require('../../repositories/store');
const { requireAuth } = require('../../middleware/auth');
const { canViewQuote } = require('../../services/accessPolicy');
const { publicUser } = require('../../services/viewModels');
const { assertTransition } = require('../../services/stateMachine');
const { acceptQuote, WorkflowError } = require('../../services/jobWorkflow');
const { validateQuoteInput } = require('../../services/validation');
const { createNotificationTx } = require('../../services/marketplace');
const { formatDate, formatDateTime, compact } = require('../../utils/format');
const { sendEmail } = require('../../utils/mailer');
const { recordsByIds } = require('../../repositories/queryHelpers');

const router = express.Router();

router.post('/:id/quotes', (req, res, next) => {
  const job = db.findById('jobs', req.params.id);
  const currentUser = res.locals.currentUser;
  if (!job || job.status !== 'open') { req.flash('error', 'That job is not accepting quotes.'); return res.redirect('/jobs'); }
  if (!currentUser && !compact(req.body.email) && !compact(req.body.phone)) {
    req.flash('error', 'Please provide your email or phone number so employers can respond to your quote.');
    return res.redirect(`/jobs/${job.id}`);
  }
  if (currentUser) {
    if (job.posterId === currentUser.id) { req.flash('error', 'You cannot quote on your own job.'); return res.redirect(`/jobs/${job.id}`); }
    if (!['worker', 'both'].includes(currentUser.role)) { req.flash('error', 'Only workers can submit quotes.'); return res.redirect(`/jobs/${job.id}`); }
    if (db.findOne('quotes', { where: { jobId: job.id, workerId: currentUser.id } })) {
      req.flash('error', 'You already submitted a quote for this job.');
      return res.redirect(`/jobs/${job.id}`);
    }
  } else {
    req.session.guestQuotes = req.session.guestQuotes || {};
    if ((req.session.guestQuotes[job.id] || 0) >= 2) {
      req.flash('error', 'You have reached the guest quote limit. Create an account to continue.');
      return res.redirect(`/jobs/${job.id}`);
    }
  }
  const validation = validateQuoteInput(req.body);
  if (validation.errors.length) { req.flash('error', validation.errors.join(' ')); return res.redirect(`/jobs/${job.id}`); }
  const values = validation.values;
  const poster = db.findById('users', job.posterId);
  try {
    const quote = db.transaction((tx) => {
      const now = new Date().toISOString();
      const item = {
        id: uuidv4(), jobId: job.id, workerId: currentUser ? currentUser.id : null,
        message: values.message, quoteType: values.quoteType, amount: values.amount,
        estimatedHours: values.estimatedHours, availability: values.availability,
        toolsIncluded: values.toolsIncluded, status: 'submitted', createdAt: now, updatedAt: now,
        guestContactEmail: currentUser ? currentUser.email : values.email,
        guestContactPhone: currentUser ? currentUser.phone : values.phone,
      };
      tx.quotes.insert(item);
      if (currentUser) {
        createNotificationTx(tx, job.posterId, 'quote-received', `New quote on ${job.title}`, `${currentUser.name} submitted a quote`, `/jobs/${job.id}`, { quoteId: item.id });
        tx.messages.insert({
          id: uuidv4(), jobId: job.id, quoteId: item.id, senderId: currentUser.id, recipientId: job.posterId,
          body: `Quote submitted: ${item.message || 'No message provided.'}`, createdAt: now, readAt: null,
          attachments: [], safetyScan: { flagged: false, flags: [], notices: [] }, reported: false,
        });
      }
      return item;
    });
    if (!currentUser) req.session.guestQuotes[job.id] = (req.session.guestQuotes[job.id] || 0) + 1;
    if (poster && (currentUser?.email || quote.guestContactEmail)) {
      sendEmail({
        to: poster.email,
        replyTo: currentUser?.email || quote.guestContactEmail,
        subject: `[NeighbourTask] New quote on: ${job.title}`,
        text: `Hi ${poster.name},\n\nA new quote was submitted for "${job.title}".\n\n${quote.message || 'No message provided.'}\n\n${process.env.BASE_URL || 'http://localhost:3000'}/jobs/${job.id}`,
      }).catch((error) => console.error('[quote-email]', error.message));
    }
    req.flash('success', currentUser ? 'Quote submitted.' : 'Your guest quote was submitted. Create an account to track it.');
    return res.redirect(`/jobs/${job.id}`);
  } catch (error) {
    if (String(error.code || '').startsWith('SQLITE_CONSTRAINT')) {
      req.flash('error', 'You already submitted a quote for this job.');
      return res.redirect(`/jobs/${job.id}`);
    }
    return next(error);
  }
});

router.get('/:id/quotes/:quoteId', requireAuth, (req, res) => {
  const job = db.findById('jobs', req.params.id);
  const quote = db.findById('quotes', req.params.quoteId);
  if (!job || !quote || quote.jobId !== job.id) return res.status(404).render('pages/404', { title: 'Quote not found' });
  const currentUser = res.locals.currentUser;
  if (!canViewQuote(currentUser, job, quote)) { req.flash('error', 'You are not authorized to view this quote.'); return res.redirect('/dashboard'); }
  const poster = db.findById('users', job.posterId);
  const worker = quote.workerId ? db.findById('users', quote.workerId) : null;
  const profile = quote.workerId ? db.findOne('workerProfiles', { where: { userId: quote.workerId } }) : null;
  const messages = db.findMany('messages', { where: { quoteId: quote.id }, orderBy: { field: 'createdAt', direction: 'asc' }, limit: 200 });
  const senders = recordsByIds('users', messages.map((message) => message.senderId));
  return res.render('jobs/quoteShow', {
    title: `Quote from ${worker ? worker.name : 'Worker'}`, job, quote,
    poster: publicUser(poster), worker: publicUser(worker), profile,
    messages: messages.map((message) => ({ ...message, sender: publicUser(senders.get(message.senderId)) })),
    canManage: currentUser.id === job.posterId || currentUser.isAdmin,
    formatDate, formatDateTime,
  });
});

router.post('/:jobId/quotes/:quoteId/status', requireAuth, (req, res, next) => {
  const nextStatus = ['submitted', 'shortlisted', 'accepted', 'declined'].includes(req.body.status) ? req.body.status : null;
  if (!nextStatus) { req.flash('error', 'Choose a valid quote status.'); return res.redirect(`/jobs/${req.params.jobId}`); }
  try {
    if (nextStatus === 'accepted') acceptQuote({ jobId: req.params.jobId, quoteId: req.params.quoteId, actor: res.locals.currentUser });
    else db.transaction((tx) => {
      const job = tx.jobs.findById(req.params.jobId);
      const quote = tx.quotes.findById(req.params.quoteId);
      if (!job || !quote || quote.jobId !== req.params.jobId) throw new WorkflowError('Quote not found.', 'NOT_FOUND');
      if (job.posterId !== res.locals.currentUser.id && !res.locals.currentUser.isAdmin) throw new WorkflowError('Only the poster can manage quotes for this job.', 'FORBIDDEN');
      assertTransition('quote', quote.status, nextStatus);
      tx.quotes.update(quote.id, { status: nextStatus, updatedAt: new Date().toISOString() });
    });
    req.flash('success', 'Quote updated.');
    return res.redirect(`/jobs/${req.params.jobId}`);
  } catch (error) {
    if (error instanceof WorkflowError || error.code === 'INVALID_STATE_TRANSITION') {
      req.flash('error', error.message || 'That quote status change is not allowed.');
      return res.redirect(`/jobs/${req.params.jobId}`);
    }
    return next(error);
  }
});

module.exports = router;

// ===== src/domains/messages/messageRoutes.js =====
const express = require('express');
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');
const db = require('../../repositories/store');
const privateUpload = require('../../middleware/privateUpload');
const { handleMulterError } = require('../../middleware/upload');
const { requireAuth } = require('../../middleware/auth');
const { validateMultipartCsrf } = require('../../middleware/csrf');
const { publicUser } = require('../../services/viewModels');
const { compact } = require('../../utils/format');
const { safeRedirectTarget } = require('../../utils/security');
const { discardUploadedFiles } = require('../../utils/uploads');
const { sendEmail } = require('../../utils/mailer');
const { message: validateMessage, messageReport: validateMessageReport } = require('../../services/inputSchemas');
const { openModerationCaseTx } = require('../../services/audit');
const relationshipRepository = require('../../repositories/relationshipRepository');
const { recordsByIds } = require('../../repositories/queryHelpers');
const { sendMessage } = require('./messageService');

const router = express.Router();
router.use(requireAuth);

router.get('/new', (req, res) => {
  const currentUser = res.locals.currentUser;
  const ids = relationshipRepository.relatedUserIds(currentUser.id);
  const users = ids.length ? db.findMany('users', { where: { id: { $in: ids }, accountStatus: 'active' } }) : [];
  const profiles = new Map(db.findMany('workerProfiles', { where: { userId: { $in: ids } } }).map((profile) => [profile.userId, profile]));
  const recipients = users.map((user) => ({ ...publicUser(user), profile: profiles.get(user.id) || null }));
  return res.render('messages/new', { title: 'New message', recipients });
});

router.get('/', (req, res) => {
  const currentUser = res.locals.currentUser;
  const result = db.cursorPage('messages', {
    cursor: req.query.cursor || null,
    limit: 100,
    or: [{ senderId: currentUser.id }, { recipientId: currentUser.id }],
  });
  const usersById = recordsByIds('users', result.items.flatMap((message) => [message.senderId, message.recipientId]));
  const jobsById = recordsByIds('jobs', result.items.map((message) => message.jobId));
  const quotesById = recordsByIds('quotes', result.items.map((message) => message.quoteId));
  const threadMap = new Map();
  for (const raw of result.items) {
    const message = {
      ...raw,
      sender: publicUser(usersById.get(raw.senderId)),
      recipient: publicUser(usersById.get(raw.recipientId)),
      job: jobsById.get(raw.jobId) || null,
      quote: quotesById.get(raw.quoteId) || null,
    };
    const key = `${message.jobId || 'general'}:${message.quoteId || 'none'}:${[message.senderId, message.recipientId].sort().join('-')}`;
    if (!threadMap.has(key)) threadMap.set(key, []);
    threadMap.get(key).push(message);
  }
  const threads = [...threadMap.values()].map((messages) => {
    const sorted = messages.sort((a, b) => new Date(a.createdAt) - new Date(b.createdAt));
    return {
      latest: sorted[sorted.length - 1],
      unreadCount: sorted.filter((message) => message.recipientId === currentUser.id && !message.readAt).length,
      messages: sorted,
    };
  }).sort((a, b) => new Date(b.latest.createdAt) - new Date(a.latest.createdAt));
  return res.render('messages/index', { title: 'Messages', threads, pageInfo: result.pageInfo });
});

router.post('/', privateUpload.array('attachments', 4), handleMulterError('/messages'), validateMultipartCsrf, (req, res, next) => {
  const currentUser = res.locals.currentUser;
  const parsed = validateMessage(req.body);
  const back = safeRedirectTarget(req, req.get('Referrer'), '/messages');
  const reject = (message) => {
    discardUploadedFiles(req);
    req.flash('error', message);
    return res.redirect(back);
  };
  if (!parsed.success) return reject(parsed.errors.join(' '));
  if (!parsed.data.body && !(req.files || []).length) return reject('Add a message or attachment.');
  const recipient = db.findOne('users', { where: { id: parsed.data.recipientId, accountStatus: 'active' } });
  if (!recipient || recipient.id === currentUser.id) return reject('Recipient not found.');
  const job = parsed.data.jobId ? db.findById('jobs', parsed.data.jobId) : null;
  const quote = parsed.data.quoteId ? db.findById('quotes', parsed.data.quoteId) : null;
  try {
    const message = sendMessage({ sender: currentUser, recipient, job, quote, body: parsed.data.body, files: req.files || [] });
    sendEmail({
      to: recipient.email, replyTo: currentUser.email,
      subject: job ? `[NeighbourTask] New message about: ${job.title}` : '[NeighbourTask] New message',
      text: `You received a new message in NeighbourTask. Sign in to view and reply:\n\n${process.env.BASE_URL || 'http://localhost:3000'}/messages`,
    }).catch((error) => console.error('[message-email]', error.message));
    req.flash(message.safetyScan.flagged ? 'info' : 'success', message.safetyScan.flagged ? 'Message sent and queued for safety review.' : 'Message sent.');
    return res.redirect(back);
  } catch (error) {
    if (error.code === 'FORBIDDEN') return reject(error.message);
    discardUploadedFiles(req);
    return next(error);
  }
});

router.post('/:id/read', (req, res) => {
  const message = db.findById('messages', req.params.id);
  if (message && message.recipientId === res.locals.currentUser.id && !message.readAt) db.update('messages', message.id, { readAt: new Date().toISOString() });
  return res.redirect(safeRedirectTarget(req, req.get('Referrer'), '/messages'));
});

router.post('/:id/report', (req, res) => {
  const currentUser = res.locals.currentUser;
  const message = db.findById('messages', req.params.id);
  if (!message || ![message.senderId, message.recipientId].includes(currentUser.id)) {
    req.flash('error', 'Message not found.');
    return res.redirect('/messages');
  }
  const parsed = validateMessageReport(req.body);
  if (!parsed.success) {
    req.flash('error', parsed.errors.join(' '));
    return res.redirect('/messages');
  }
  db.transaction((tx) => {
    if (tx.messageReports.findOne({ where: { messageId: message.id, reporterId: currentUser.id, status: { $ne: 'closed' } } })) return;
    tx.messageReports.insert({
      id: uuidv4(), messageId: message.id, reporterId: currentUser.id,
      reason: parsed.data.reason, description: parsed.data.description,
      status: 'open', adminNotes: '', createdAt: new Date().toISOString(), updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    });
    tx.messages.update(message.id, { reported: true });
    openModerationCaseTx(tx, { targetType: 'message', targetId: message.id, reason: parsed.data.reason, priority: 'high' });
  });
  req.flash('success', 'Message reported for review.');
  return res.redirect('/messages');
});

router.post('/block/:userId', (req, res, next) => {
  const currentUser = res.locals.currentUser;
  try {
    db.transaction((tx) => {
      const blocked = tx.users.findById(req.params.userId);
      if (!blocked || blocked.accountStatus !== 'active' || blocked.id === currentUser.id) {
        const error = new Error('User not found.'); error.code = 'NOT_FOUND'; throw error;
      }
      if (!tx.userBlocks.findOne({ where: { blockerId: currentUser.id, blockedId: blocked.id, status: 'active' } })) {
        tx.userBlocks.insert({
          id: uuidv4(), blockerId: currentUser.id, blockedId: blocked.id,
          reason: compact(req.body.reason).slice(0, 500), status: 'active',
          createdAt: new Date().toISOString(), updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
        });
      }
    });
    req.flash('success', 'User blocked.');
    return res.redirect('/messages');
  } catch (error) {
    if (error.code === 'NOT_FOUND') { req.flash('error', error.message); return res.redirect('/messages'); }
    return next(error);
  }
});

module.exports = router;

// ===== src/domains/messages/messageService.js =====
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');
const db = require('../../repositories/store');
const { scanMessage } = require('../../services/messageSafety');
const { createNotificationTx } = require('../../services/marketplace');
const { registerPrivateFile } = require('../../services/privateFiles');
const { canViewQuote } = require('../../services/accessPolicy');
const relationshipRepository = require('../../repositories/relationshipRepository');

function sendMessage({ sender, recipient, job, quote, body, files = [] }) {
  if (relationshipRepository.usersAreBlocked(sender.id, recipient.id)) {
    const error = new Error('Messaging is blocked between these users.');
    error.code = 'FORBIDDEN';
    throw error;
  }
  if ((job || quote) && (!job || !quote || !canViewQuote(sender, job, quote))) {
    const error = new Error('Unable to send that message.');
    error.code = 'FORBIDDEN';
    throw error;
  }
  if (job || quote) {
    if (![job.posterId, quote.workerId].includes(recipient.id)) {
      const error = new Error('The recipient is not connected to this quote.');
      error.code = 'FORBIDDEN';
      throw error;
    }
  } else if (!sender.isAdmin && !relationshipRepository.relationshipExists(sender.id, recipient.id)) {
    const error = new Error('You can only message users connected to one of your jobs or quotes.');
    error.code = 'FORBIDDEN';
    throw error;
  }

  const id = uuidv4();
  const safetyScan = scanMessage(body);
  return db.transaction((tx) => {
    const attachments = files.map((file) => {
      const privateFile = registerPrivateFile(tx, file, { ownerId: sender.id, contextType: 'message', contextId: id });
      return { fileId: privateFile.id, url: `/files/${privateFile.id}`, originalName: privateFile.originalName, mimeType: privateFile.mimeType };
    });
    const message = {
      id, jobId: job ? job.id : null, quoteId: quote ? quote.id : null,
      senderId: sender.id, recipientId: recipient.id, body, attachments, safetyScan,
      reported: false, createdAt: new Date().toISOString(), readAt: null,
    };
    tx.messages.insert(message);
    createNotificationTx(
      tx, recipient.id, 'message-received',
      job ? `New message about ${job.title}` : `New message from ${sender.name}`,
      body.slice(0, 120), '/messages', job ? { jobId: job.id, quoteId: quote ? quote.id : null } : {},
    );
    return message;
  });
}

module.exports = { sendMessage };

// ===== src/domains/posters/posterService.js =====
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');
const db = require('../../repositories/store');

function createDefaultProfile(user) {
  const now = new Date().toISOString();
  return {
    id: uuidv4(),
    userId: user.id,
    displayName: user.name,
    bio: '',
    companyName: '',
    website: '',
    phone: user.phone || '',
    city: user.city || '',
    postalCode: user.postalCode || '',
    logoUrl: null,
    completedJobs: 0,
    averageRating: null,
    createdAt: now,
    updatedAt: now,
  };
}

function saveProfile({ userId, values, logoUrl }) {
  return db.transaction((tx) => {
    const user = tx.users.findById(userId);
    if (!user) return null;
    let profile = tx.posterProfiles.findOne({ where: { userId } });
    if (!profile) {
      profile = createDefaultProfile(user);
      tx.posterProfiles.insert(profile);
    }
    return tx.posterProfiles.update(profile.id, {
      displayName: values.displayName,
      bio: values.bio,
      companyName: values.companyName,
      website: values.website,
      phone: values.phone,
      city: values.city,
      postalCode: values.postalCode,
      logoUrl: logoUrl || profile.logoUrl || null,
      updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    });
  });
}

module.exports = { createDefaultProfile, saveProfile };

// ===== src/domains/workers/workerRoutes.js =====
const express = require('express');
const upload = require('../../middleware/upload');
const privateUpload = require('../../middleware/privateUpload');
const { handleMulterError } = require('../../middleware/upload');
const { validateMultipartCsrf } = require('../../middleware/csrf');
const { requireAuth } = require('../../middleware/auth');
const db = require('../../repositories/store');
const { compact, formatDateTime } = require('../../utils/format');
const { workerProfile: validateWorkerProfile } = require('../../services/inputSchemas');
const { safeRedirectTarget } = require('../../utils/security');
const { discardUploadedFiles } = require('../../utils/uploads');
const workerRepository = require('../../repositories/workerRepository');
const workerService = require('./workerService');
const { workerChecklist } = require('../../services/onboarding');

const router = express.Router();

function normalizeSkills(value) {
  if (Array.isArray(value)) return value.map(compact).filter(Boolean);
  return String(value || '').split(',').map(compact).filter(Boolean);
}

router.get('/', (req, res) => {
  const result = workerRepository.browse(req, res.locals.currentUser);
  return res.render('workers/index', {
    title: 'Browse workers', profiles: result.profiles, filters: req.query, pagination: result.pagination,
  });
});

router.get('/profile', requireAuth, (req, res) => {
  const currentUser = res.locals.currentUser;
  const profile = workerService.profileForUser(currentUser);
  const documents = db.findMany('documents', {
    where: { workerId: currentUser.id },
    orderBy: { field: 'createdAt', direction: 'desc' },
    limit: 100,
  });
  const payoutAccount = db.findOne('payoutAccounts', { where: { userId: currentUser.id } });
  return res.render('workers/profile', {
    title: 'Worker profile', profile, documents, payoutAccount,
    onboardingChecklist: workerChecklist(currentUser, profile, documents, payoutAccount),
    autosave: { key: 'worker-profile', enabled: true }, formatDateTime,
  });
});

router.post('/profile', requireAuth, upload.array('portfolioPhotos', 6), handleMulterError('/workers/profile'), validateMultipartCsrf, (req, res) => {
  const currentUser = res.locals.currentUser;
  const parsed = validateWorkerProfile({
    ...req.body,
    displayName: compact(req.body.displayName) || currentUser.name,
    skills: normalizeSkills(req.body.skills),
  });
  if (!parsed.success) {
    discardUploadedFiles(req);
    req.flash('error', parsed.errors.join(' '));
    return res.redirect('/workers/profile');
  }
  const photoUrls = (req.files || []).map((file) => `/uploads/${file.filename}`);
  workerService.saveProfile({ userId: currentUser.id, values: parsed.data, photoUrls });
  req.flash('success', 'Worker profile saved.');
  return res.redirect('/workers/profile');
});

router.post('/profile/documents', requireAuth, privateUpload.single('document'), handleMulterError('/workers/profile'), validateMultipartCsrf, (req, res) => {
  const allowed = ['insurance', 'wsib', 'trade_certificate', 'id'];
  if (!req.file || !allowed.includes(req.body.type)) {
    discardUploadedFiles(req);
    req.flash('error', 'Please upload a valid document type as a PDF or image.');
    return res.redirect('/workers/profile');
  }
  workerService.addDocument({
    userId: res.locals.currentUser.id,
    file: req.file,
    type: req.body.type,
    expiryDate: req.body.expiryDate,
  });
  req.flash('success', 'Document uploaded for admin review.');
  return res.redirect('/workers/profile');
});

router.post('/:id/save', requireAuth, (req, res) => {
  const result = workerService.toggleSaved({
    posterId: res.locals.currentUser.id,
    profileId: req.params.id,
    notes: req.body.notes,
  });
  if (!result) {
    req.flash('error', 'Worker profile not found.');
    return res.redirect('/workers');
  }
  req.flash('success', result.saved ? 'Worker saved.' : 'Worker removed from saved list.');
  return res.redirect(safeRedirectTarget(req, req.get('Referrer'), `/workers/${result.profile.id}`));
});

router.get('/:id', (req, res) => {
  const result = workerRepository.detail(req.params.id, res.locals.currentUser);
  if (!result) return res.status(404).render('pages/404', { title: 'Worker not found' });
  return res.render('workers/show', {
    title: result.profile.displayName,
    ...result,
    documents: [],
    formatDateTime,
  });
});

module.exports = router;

// ===== src/domains/workers/workerService.js =====
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');
const db = require('../../repositories/store');
const { registerPrivateFile } = require('../../services/privateFiles');

function createDefaultProfile(user) {
  const now = new Date().toISOString();
  return {
    id: uuidv4(), userId: user.id, displayName: user.name, bio: '', skills: [], tools: '',
    hourlyRate: null, minimumBooking: null, availability: '', serviceRadiusKm: null,
    hasVehicle: false, insuranceStatus: 'not-provided', wsibStatus: 'not-provided',
    tradeCertificationStatus: 'not-provided', verificationLevel: 'basic', status: 'active',
    averageRating: null, completedJobs: 0, portfolioPhotos: [], complianceAcceptedAt: null,
    boostedUntil: null, lastActiveAt: now, createdAt: now, updatedAt: now,
  };
}

function profileForUser(user) {
  return db.findOne('workerProfiles', { where: { userId: user.id } }) || createDefaultProfile(user);
}

function saveProfile({ userId, values, photoUrls = [] }) {
  return db.transaction((tx) => {
    const user = tx.users.findById(userId);
    if (!user) return null;
    let profile = tx.workerProfiles.findOne({ where: { userId } });
    if (!profile) {
      profile = createDefaultProfile(user);
      tx.workerProfiles.insert(profile);
    }
    const now = new Date().toISOString();
    tx.workerProfiles.update(profile.id, {
      displayName: values.displayName,
      bio: values.bio,
      skills: values.skills,
      tools: values.tools,
      hourlyRate: values.hourlyRate,
      minimumBooking: values.minimumBooking,
      availability: values.availability,
      serviceRadiusKm: values.serviceRadiusKm,
      hasVehicle: values.hasVehicle,
      insuranceStatus: profile.insuranceStatus || 'not-provided',
      wsibStatus: profile.wsibStatus || 'not-provided',
      tradeCertificationStatus: profile.tradeCertificationStatus || 'not-provided',
      status: 'active',
      lastActiveAt: now,
      updatedAt: now,
      portfolioPhotos: [...(profile.portfolioPhotos || []), ...photoUrls].slice(-12),
      complianceAcceptedAt: values.complianceAccepted && !profile.complianceAcceptedAt ? now : profile.complianceAcceptedAt,
    });
    if (user.role === 'poster') {
      tx.users.update(user.id, { role: 'both', updatedAt: now });
    }
    return tx.workerProfiles.findOne({ where: { userId } });
  });
}

function addDocument({ userId, file, type, expiryDate }) {
  return db.transaction((tx) => {
    const user = tx.users.findById(userId);
    if (!user) return null;
    let profile = tx.workerProfiles.findOne({ where: { userId } });
    if (!profile) {
      profile = createDefaultProfile(user);
      tx.workerProfiles.insert(profile);
    }
    const now = new Date().toISOString();
    const document = {
      id: uuidv4(), workerId: userId, profileId: profile.id, type, fileUrl: null, fileId: null,
      originalName: file.originalname, status: 'pending', expiryDate: expiryDate || null,
      reviewedBy: null, adminNotes: '', createdAt: now, updatedAt: now,
    };
    const privateFile = registerPrivateFile(tx, file, {
      ownerId: userId,
      contextType: 'workerDocument',
      contextId: document.id,
    });
    document.fileId = privateFile.id;
    document.fileUrl = `/files/${privateFile.id}`;
    tx.documents.insert(document);
    const profileUpdates = { updatedAt: now };
    if (type === 'insurance') profileUpdates.insuranceStatus = 'uploaded-pending';
    if (type === 'wsib') profileUpdates.wsibStatus = 'uploaded-pending';
    if (type === 'trade_certificate') profileUpdates.tradeCertificationStatus = 'uploaded-pending';
    tx.workerProfiles.update(profile.id, profileUpdates);
    return document;
  });
}

function toggleSaved({ posterId, profileId, notes = '' }) {
  return db.transaction((tx) => {
    const profile = tx.workerProfiles.findOne({ where: { id: profileId } });
    if (!profile) return null;
    const existing = tx.savedWorkers.findOne({ where: { posterId, profileId } });
    if (existing) {
      tx.savedWorkers.delete(existing.id);
      return { profile, saved: false };
    }
    tx.savedWorkers.insert({
      id: uuidv4(), posterId, workerId: profile.userId, profileId,
      notes: String(notes || '').trim().slice(0, 1000), createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    });
    return { profile, saved: true };
  });
}

module.exports = { createDefaultProfile, profileForUser, saveProfile, addDocument, toggleSaved };

// ===== src/middleware/apiKey.js =====
const crypto = require('crypto');

function safeEqual(left, right) {
  const a = Buffer.from(String(left || ''));
  const b = Buffer.from(String(right || ''));
  return a.length > 0 && a.length === b.length && crypto.timingSafeEqual(a, b);
}

function requireApiKey(req, res, next) {
  const expected = process.env.HERMES_API_KEY;
  const authorization = String(req.headers.authorization || '');
  const bearer = authorization.startsWith('Bearer ') ? authorization.slice(7).trim() : '';
  const apiKey = req.headers['x-api-key'] || bearer;
  if (!expected) return res.status(503).json({ error: 'API access is not configured.' });
  if (!safeEqual(apiKey, expected)) {
    return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized. Provide a valid API key.' });
  }
  return next();
}

module.exports = { requireApiKey };

// ===== src/middleware/auth.js =====
function isActiveUser(user) {
  return Boolean(user && user.accountStatus === 'active');
}

function requireAuth(req, res, next) {
  const user = res.locals.currentUser;
  if (!isActiveUser(user)) {
    if (req.session && req.session.userId) delete req.session.userId;
    req.flash('error', 'Please log in first.');
    return res.redirect('/auth/login');
  }
  return next();
}

function requireAdmin(req, res, next) {
  const user = res.locals.currentUser;
  if (!isActiveUser(user) || !user.isAdmin) {
    req.flash('error', 'Admin access is required.');
    return res.redirect('/');
  }
  return next();
}

function requireWorker(req, res, next) {
  const user = res.locals.currentUser;
  if (!isActiveUser(user) || !['worker', 'both'].includes(user.role)) {
    req.flash('error', 'A worker account is required for that action.');
    return res.redirect('/workers/profile');
  }
  return next();
}

function requireAuthApi(req, res, next) {
  if (!isActiveUser(res.locals.currentUser)) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Authentication required.' });
  return next();
}

function requireAdminApi(req, res, next) {
  const user = res.locals.currentUser;
  if (!isActiveUser(user) || !user.isAdmin) return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Admin access required.' });
  return next();
}

module.exports = { requireAuth, requireAdmin, requireWorker, requireAuthApi, requireAdminApi, isActiveUser };

// ===== src/middleware/csrf.js =====
const crypto = require('crypto');
const { safeRedirectTarget } = require('../utils/security');
const { discardUploadedFiles, requestFilesMatchDeclaredTypes } = require('../utils/uploads');

function ensureCsrfToken(req, res, next) {
  if (!req.session.csrfToken) {
    req.session.csrfToken = crypto.randomBytes(32).toString('base64url');
  }
  res.locals.csrfToken = req.session.csrfToken;
  res.cookie('XSRF-TOKEN', req.session.csrfToken, {
    httpOnly: false,
    sameSite: 'lax',
    secure: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production',
    path: '/',
  });
  next();
}

function tokensMatch(expected, supplied) {
  const first = Buffer.from(String(expected || ''));
  const second = Buffer.from(String(supplied || ''));
  return first.length > 0 && first.length === second.length && crypto.timingSafeEqual(first, second);
}

function rejectCsrf(req, res) {
  if (req.accepts(['html', 'json']) === 'json' || req.path.startsWith('/api/')) {
    return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Invalid or expired CSRF token.' });
  }
  req.flash('error', 'Your session expired. Please go back and submit the form again.');
  if (req.baseUrl === '/auth' || String(req.path || '').startsWith('/auth')) {
    return res.redirect('/auth/login');
  }
  return res.redirect(safeRedirectTarget(req, req.get('Referrer'), '/'));
}

function validateCsrf(req, res, next) {
  if (!['POST', 'PUT', 'PATCH', 'DELETE'].includes(req.method)) return next();
  const token = (req.body && req.body._csrf)
    || req.headers['x-csrf-token']
    || req.headers['csrf-token']
    || '';
  if (!tokensMatch(req.session.csrfToken, token)) return rejectCsrf(req, res);
  return next();
}

function validateMultipartCsrf(req, res, next) {
  const token = (req.body && req.body._csrf) || req.headers['x-csrf-token'] || req.headers['csrf-token'] || '';
  if (!tokensMatch(req.session.csrfToken, token)) {
    discardUploadedFiles(req);
    return rejectCsrf(req, res);
  }
  if (!requestFilesMatchDeclaredTypes(req)) {
    discardUploadedFiles(req);
    req.flash('error', 'The uploaded file content does not match an allowed image or PDF type.');
    return res.redirect(safeRedirectTarget(req, req.get('Referrer'), '/'));
  }
  return next();
}

function csrfProtection(req, res, next) {
  if (!['POST', 'PUT', 'PATCH', 'DELETE'].includes(req.method)) return next();
  if (req.baseUrl === '/api' || req.path.startsWith('/api/')) return next();
  if (req.is('multipart/form-data')) return next();
  return validateCsrf(req, res, next);
}

module.exports = { ensureCsrfToken, validateCsrf, validateMultipartCsrf, csrfProtection };

// ===== src/middleware/locals.js =====
const db = require('../db');
const { ensureCsrfToken } = require('./csrf');
const { formatDate, formatDateTime } = require('../utils/format');
const { accountUser } = require('../services/viewModels');
const { statusLabel, statusTone } = require('../services/ux');

function attachLocals(req, res, next) {
  const sessionUser = req.session.userId ? db.findById('users', req.session.userId) : null;
  const currentUser = sessionUser && sessionUser.accountStatus === 'active' ? sessionUser : null;

  if (sessionUser && !currentUser) delete req.session.userId;
  if (currentUser) res.set('Cache-Control', 'private, no-store, max-age=0');

  req.currentUser = currentUser;
  res.locals.currentUser = accountUser(currentUser);
  res.locals.unreadNotifications = currentUser
    ? db.count('notifications', { userId: currentUser.id, readAt: null })
    : 0;
  res.locals.unreadMessages = currentUser
    ? db.count('messages', { recipientId: currentUser.id, readAt: null })
    : 0;
  res.locals.isAuthenticated = Boolean(currentUser);
  res.locals.flash = {
    success: req.flash('success'),
    error: req.flash('error'),
    info: req.flash('info'),
  };
  res.locals.categories = db.categories;
  res.locals.currentPath = req.path;
  res.locals.statusLabel = statusLabel;
  res.locals.statusTone = statusTone;
  res.locals.formatDate = formatDate;
  res.locals.formatDateTime = formatDateTime;
  res.locals.formatCurrency = (value) => {
    if (value === undefined || value === null || value === '') return 'Contact for quote';
    const numberValue = Number(value);
    if (Number.isNaN(numberValue)) return String(value);
    return new Intl.NumberFormat('en-CA', { style: 'currency', currency: 'CAD' }).format(numberValue);
  };
  return ensureCsrfToken(req, res, next);
}

module.exports = { attachLocals };

// ===== src/middleware/privateUpload.js =====
const multer = require('multer');
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');
const { privateRoot, ensurePrivateRoot } = require('../services/privateFiles');
const { extensionForMime } = require('../utils/uploads');

const allowedMimeTypes = new Set([
  'image/jpeg', 'image/png', 'image/webp', 'image/gif', 'application/pdf',
]);

const storage = multer.diskStorage({
  destination: (_req, _file, cb) => {
    ensurePrivateRoot();
    cb(null, privateRoot);
  },
  filename: (_req, file, cb) => {
    const extension = extensionForMime(file.mimetype);
    cb(null, `${uuidv4()}${extension}`);
  },
});

module.exports = multer({
  storage,
  fileFilter: (_req, file, cb) => cb(
    allowedMimeTypes.has(file.mimetype) ? null : new Error('Only images and PDFs are allowed.'),
    allowedMimeTypes.has(file.mimetype),
  ),
  limits: { fileSize: 5 * 1024 * 1024, files: 6 },
});

// ===== src/middleware/requestContext.js =====
const crypto = require('crypto');

function requestContext(req, res, next) {
  const incoming = String(req.get('X-Request-Id') || '').trim();
  const requestId = /^[a-zA-Z0-9._:-]{8,128}$/.test(incoming) ? incoming : crypto.randomUUID();
  const startedAt = process.hrtime.bigint();

  req.requestId = requestId;
  res.locals.requestId = requestId;
  res.locals.cspNonce = crypto.randomBytes(18).toString('base64');
  res.setHeader('X-Request-Id', requestId);

  res.once('finish', () => {
    const durationMs = Number(process.hrtime.bigint() - startedAt) / 1e6;
    const record = {
      requestId,
      method: req.method,
      path: req.originalUrl ? req.originalUrl.split('?')[0] : req.path,
      status: res.statusCode,
      durationMs: Number(durationMs.toFixed(1)),
    };
    const log = res.statusCode >= 500 ? console.error : (res.statusCode >= 400 ? console.warn : console.info);
    log('[request]', record);
  });

  next();
}

module.exports = { requestContext };

// ===== src/middleware/sessionStore.js =====
const { getDb } = require('../db');

class SQLiteStore extends require('express-session').Store {
  constructor(options = {}) {
    super(options);
    this.cleanupIntervalMs = Number(options.cleanupIntervalMs || 15 * 60 * 1000);
    this.cleanupTimer = setInterval(() => this.clearExpired(() => {}), this.cleanupIntervalMs);
    if (this.cleanupTimer.unref) this.cleanupTimer.unref();
  }

  get(sid, cb) {
    try {
      const db = getDb();
      const row = db.prepare('SELECT data, expires FROM sessions WHERE sid = ?').get(sid);
      if (!row) return cb(null, null);
      if (Number(row.expires) <= Date.now()) {
        db.prepare('DELETE FROM sessions WHERE sid = ?').run(sid);
        return cb(null, null);
      }
      return cb(null, JSON.parse(row.data));
    } catch (err) {
      return cb(err);
    }
  }

  set(sid, session, cb) {
    try {
      const db = getDb();
      const expires = session.cookie && session.cookie.expires
        ? new Date(session.cookie.expires).getTime()
        : Date.now() + 86400000;
      db.prepare('INSERT OR REPLACE INTO sessions (sid, data, expires) VALUES (?, ?, ?)')
        .run(sid, JSON.stringify(session), expires);
      return cb(null);
    } catch (err) {
      return cb(err);
    }
  }

  destroy(sid, cb) {
    try {
      getDb().prepare('DELETE FROM sessions WHERE sid = ?').run(sid);
      return cb(null);
    } catch (err) {
      return cb(err);
    }
  }

  touch(sid, session, cb) {
    try {
      const expires = session.cookie && session.cookie.expires
        ? new Date(session.cookie.expires).getTime()
        : Date.now() + 86400000;
      getDb().prepare('UPDATE sessions SET expires = ?, data = ? WHERE sid = ?')
        .run(expires, JSON.stringify(session), sid);
      return cb(null);
    } catch (err) {
      return cb(err);
    }
  }

  clearExpired(cb) {
    try {
      getDb().prepare('DELETE FROM sessions WHERE expires <= ?').run(Date.now());
      return cb(null);
    } catch (err) {
      return cb(err);
    }
  }
}

module.exports = SQLiteStore;

// ===== src/middleware/upload.js =====
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');
const multer = require('multer');
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');
const { safeRedirectTarget } = require('../utils/security');
const { extensionForMime } = require('../utils/uploads');

const publicUploadRoot = path.join(__dirname, '..', '..', 'public', 'uploads');
fs.mkdirSync(publicUploadRoot, { recursive: true });

const storage = multer.diskStorage({
  destination: (_req, _file, cb) => cb(null, publicUploadRoot),
  filename: (_req, file, cb) => {
    const extension = extensionForMime(file.mimetype);
    cb(null, `${uuidv4()}${extension}`);
  },
});

function fileFilter(_req, file, cb) {
  const allowed = ['image/jpeg', 'image/png', 'image/webp', 'image/gif'];
  if (!allowed.includes(file.mimetype)) return cb(new Error('Only images are allowed for public uploads.'));
  return cb(null, true);
}

const upload = multer({
  storage,
  fileFilter,
  limits: { fileSize: 5 * 1024 * 1024, files: 6 },
});

function handleMulterError(redirectTo) {
  return (err, req, res, next) => {
    const rawUrl = typeof redirectTo === 'function' ? redirectTo(req) : redirectTo;
    const url = safeRedirectTarget(req, rawUrl, '/');
    if (err instanceof multer.MulterError) {
      if (err.code === 'LIMIT_FILE_SIZE') req.flash('error', 'File is too large. Maximum size is 5 MB per file.');
      else if (err.code === 'LIMIT_FILE_COUNT') req.flash('error', 'Too many files. Maximum is 6 files.');
      else if (err.code === 'LIMIT_UNEXPECTED_FILE') req.flash('error', 'Unexpected file field.');
      else req.flash('error', `File upload error: ${err.message}`);
      return res.redirect(url);
    }
    if (err && /Only images/.test(err.message)) {
      req.flash('error', err.message);
      return res.redirect(url);
    }
    return next(err);
  };
}

module.exports = upload;
module.exports.handleMulterError = handleMulterError;

// ===== src/repositories/draftRepository.js =====
const crypto = require('crypto');
const store = require('./store');

const MAX_AGE_MS = 1000 * 60 * 60 * 24 * 14;

function normalizeKind(value) {
  const kind = String(value || '').trim().toLowerCase();
  return /^[a-z0-9][a-z0-9:_-]{0,79}$/.test(kind) ? kind : null;
}

function findForUser(userId, kind) {
  const normalized = normalizeKind(kind);
  if (!normalized) return null;
  const draft = store.findOne('drafts', { userId, kind: normalized });
  if (!draft) return null;
  if (new Date(draft.expiresAt).getTime() <= Date.now()) {
    store.remove('drafts', draft.id);
    return null;
  }
  return draft;
}

function saveForUser({ userId, kind, route, payload }) {
  const normalized = normalizeKind(kind);
  if (!normalized) {
    const error = new Error('Invalid draft kind.');
    error.code = 'VALIDATION_ERROR';
    throw error;
  }
  const safeRoute = String(route || '').startsWith('/') && !String(route).startsWith('//')
    ? String(route).slice(0, 500)
    : '/';
  const now = new Date().toISOString();
  const expiresAt = new Date(Date.now() + MAX_AGE_MS).toISOString();
  return store.transaction((tx) => {
    const existing = tx.drafts.findOne({ userId, kind: normalized });
    if (existing) {
      return tx.drafts.update(existing.id, { route: safeRoute, payload, expiresAt, updatedAt: now });
    }
    return tx.drafts.insert({
      id: crypto.randomUUID(),
      userId,
      kind: normalized,
      route: safeRoute,
      payload,
      expiresAt,
      createdAt: now,
      updatedAt: now,
    });
  });
}

function removeForUser(userId, kind) {
  const draft = findForUser(userId, kind);
  return draft ? store.remove('drafts', draft.id) : false;
}

module.exports = { MAX_AGE_MS, normalizeKind, findForUser, saveForUser, removeForUser };

// ===== src/repositories/jobRepository.js =====
const db = require('../db');
const { recordsByIds, pageRequest, paginationLinks } = require('./queryHelpers');
const { publicUser, publicPosterProfile } = require('../services/viewModels');
const { isActiveUntil, workerMatchScore, quoteValue } = require('../services/matchScorer');
const { canManageJob } = require('../services/accessPolicy');

function escapeLike(value) {
  return String(value || '').replace(/[\\%_]/g, '\\$&');
}

function browse(req, currentUser, currentProfile) {
  const { page, perPage } = pageRequest(req, { perPage: 24, maxPerPage: 60 });
  const where = { status: 'open' };
  const or = [];
  if (req.query.category) where.categoryId = String(req.query.category);
  if (req.query.city) where.city = { $like: `%${escapeLike(req.query.city)}%` };
  if (req.query.risk) where.riskLevel = String(req.query.risk);
  if (req.query.urgency) where.urgency = String(req.query.urgency);
  if (req.query.requiresTools === 'on') where.requiresTools = true;
  if (req.query.requiresInsurance === 'on') where.requiresInsurance = true;
  if (req.query.maxBudget && Number.isFinite(Number(req.query.maxBudget))) where.budgetMin = { $lte: Number(req.query.maxBudget) };
  if (req.query.q) {
    const term = `%${escapeLike(String(req.query.q).trim())}%`;
    or.push({ title: { $like: term } }, { description: { $like: term } });
  }
  let orderBy = [
    { field: 'featuredUntil', direction: 'desc' },
    { field: 'createdAt', direction: 'desc' },
  ];
  if (req.query.sort === 'budget') orderBy = [{ field: 'budgetMax', direction: 'desc' }, { field: 'createdAt', direction: 'desc' }];
  const result = db.paginate('jobs', { page, perPage, where, or, orderBy });
  const quoteCounts = db.groupCount('quotes', 'jobId', result.items.map((job) => job.id));
  let jobs = result.items.map((job) => ({
    ...job,
    quoteCount: quoteCounts.get(job.id) || 0,
    isFeatured: isActiveUntil(job.featuredUntil),
    match: currentProfile ? workerMatchScore(currentProfile, currentUser, job) : null,
  }));
  if (req.query.sort === 'match' && currentProfile) jobs = jobs.sort((a, b) => (b.match?.score || 0) - (a.match?.score || 0));
  return { jobs, pagination: paginationLinks(req, result.pagination) };
}

function adminPage(req) {
  const { page, perPage } = pageRequest(req, { perPage: 30 });
  const where = {};
  if (req.query.status) where.status = String(req.query.status);
  const result = db.paginate('jobs', { page, perPage, where, orderBy: { field: 'createdAt', direction: 'desc' } });
  const posters = recordsByIds('users', result.items.map((job) => job.posterId));
  return {
    jobs: result.items.map((job) => ({ ...job, poster: publicUser(posters.get(job.posterId)) })),
    pagination: paginationLinks(req, result.pagination),
  };
}

function detail(jobId, currentUser) {
  const job = db.findById('jobs', jobId);
  if (!job) return null;
  const posterRecord = db.findById('users', job.posterId);
  const posterProfileRecord = posterRecord ? db.findOne('posterProfiles', { where: { userId: posterRecord.id } }) : null;
  const canManage = canManageJob(currentUser, job);
  const existingQuote = currentUser ? db.findOne('quotes', { where: { jobId: job.id, workerId: currentUser.id } }) : null;
  const visibleQuotes = canManage
    ? db.findMany('quotes', { where: { jobId: job.id }, orderBy: { field: 'createdAt', direction: 'desc' }, limit: 200 })
    : existingQuote ? [existingQuote] : [];
  const workers = recordsByIds('users', visibleQuotes.map((quote) => quote.workerId));
  const profiles = new Map(db.findMany('workerProfiles', {
    where: { userId: { $in: visibleQuotes.map((quote) => quote.workerId).filter(Boolean) } },
  }).map((profile) => [profile.userId, profile]));
  const quotes = visibleQuotes.map((quote) => {
    const worker = workers.get(quote.workerId);
    const profile = profiles.get(quote.workerId);
    return {
      ...quote,
      guestContactEmail: canManage ? quote.guestContactEmail : undefined,
      guestContactPhone: canManage ? quote.guestContactPhone : undefined,
      worker: publicUser(worker),
      profile,
      match: canManage && profile ? workerMatchScore(profile, worker, job) : null,
      estimatedTotal: quoteValue(quote),
      messages: [],
    };
  }).sort((a, b) => {
    if (a.status === 'accepted') return -1;
    if (b.status === 'accepted') return 1;
    return quoteValue(a) - quoteValue(b);
  });
  const reviews = db.findMany('reviews', { where: { jobId: job.id }, orderBy: { field: 'createdAt', direction: 'desc' }, limit: 100 });
  const reviewUsers = recordsByIds('users', reviews.flatMap((review) => [review.reviewerId, review.revieweeId]));
  const reviewViews = reviews.map((review) => ({
    ...review,
    reviewer: publicUser(reviewUsers.get(review.reviewerId)),
    reviewee: publicUser(reviewUsers.get(review.revieweeId)),
  }));
  const posterReviews = posterRecord
    ? db.findMany('reviews', { where: { revieweeId: posterRecord.id }, limit: 500 })
    : [];
  const posterRating = posterReviews.length
    ? Math.round((posterReviews.reduce((sum, review) => sum + Number(review.rating || 0), 0) / posterReviews.length) * 10) / 10
    : null;
  return {
    job: { ...job, isFeatured: isActiveUntil(job.featuredUntil) },
    poster: publicUser(posterRecord),
    posterProfile: publicPosterProfile(posterProfileRecord),
    posterRating,
    posterReviewCount: posterReviews.length,
    quotes,
    canManage,
    existingQuote,
    reviews: reviewViews,
  };
}

module.exports = { browse, adminPage, detail };

// ===== src/repositories/posterRepository.js =====
const db = require('../db');

function findById(id) {
  return db.findById('posterProfiles', id);
}

function findByUserId(userId) {
  return db.findOne('posterProfiles', { where: { userId } });
}

function jobsForPoster(userId, options = {}) {
  return db.findMany('jobs', {
    where: { posterId: userId, ...(options.where || {}) },
    orderBy: options.orderBy || { field: 'createdAt', direction: 'desc' },
    limit: options.limit,
    offset: options.offset,
  });
}

module.exports = { findById, findByUserId, jobsForPoster };

// ===== src/repositories/queryHelpers.js =====
const db = require('../db');

function unique(values) {
  return [...new Set((values || []).filter(Boolean))];
}

function mapById(items, field = 'id') {
  return new Map((items || []).map((item) => [item[field], item]));
}

function recordsByIds(collection, ids) {
  const values = unique(ids);
  if (!values.length) return new Map();
  return mapById(db.findMany(collection, { where: { id: { $in: values } } }));
}

function recordsByField(collection, field, values) {
  const uniqueValues = unique(values);
  if (!uniqueValues.length) return new Map();
  return mapById(db.findMany(collection, { where: { [field]: { $in: uniqueValues } } }), field);
}

function pageRequest(req, { perPage = 25, maxPerPage = 100 } = {}) {
  return {
    page: Math.max(1, Number.parseInt(req.query.page, 10) || 1),
    perPage: Math.min(maxPerPage, Math.max(1, Number.parseInt(req.query.perPage, 10) || perPage)),
  };
}

function paginationLinks(req, pagination) {
  const url = new URL(req.originalUrl, 'http://local');
  const link = (page) => {
    url.searchParams.set('page', String(page));
    url.searchParams.set('perPage', String(pagination.perPage));
    return `${url.pathname}${url.search}`;
  };
  return {
    ...pagination,
    previousUrl: pagination.hasPrevious ? link(pagination.page - 1) : null,
    nextUrl: pagination.hasNext ? link(pagination.page + 1) : null,
  };
}

module.exports = { unique, mapById, recordsByIds, recordsByField, pageRequest, paginationLinks };

// ===== src/repositories/relationshipRepository.js =====
const db = require('../db');

function usersAreBlocked(firstUserId, secondUserId) {
  return Boolean(db.findOne('userBlocks', {
    where: { status: 'active' },
    or: [
      { blockerId: firstUserId, blockedId: secondUserId },
      { blockerId: secondUserId, blockedId: firstUserId },
    ],
  }));
}

function relationshipExists(firstUserId, secondUserId) {
  if (!firstUserId || !secondUserId || firstUserId === secondUserId) return false;
  if (db.findOne('messages', {
    or: [
      { senderId: firstUserId, recipientId: secondUserId },
      { senderId: secondUserId, recipientId: firstUserId },
    ],
  })) return true;
  if (db.findOne('jobs', {
    or: [
      { posterId: firstUserId, hiredWorkerId: secondUserId },
      { posterId: secondUserId, hiredWorkerId: firstUserId },
    ],
  })) return true;
  const firstJobs = db.findMany('jobs', { where: { posterId: firstUserId }, limit: 500 }).map((job) => job.id);
  if (firstJobs.length && db.findOne('quotes', { where: { jobId: { $in: firstJobs }, workerId: secondUserId } })) return true;
  const secondJobs = db.findMany('jobs', { where: { posterId: secondUserId }, limit: 500 }).map((job) => job.id);
  return Boolean(secondJobs.length && db.findOne('quotes', { where: { jobId: { $in: secondJobs }, workerId: firstUserId } }));
}

function relatedUserIds(userId) {
  const ids = new Set();
  db.findMany('messages', {
    or: [{ senderId: userId }, { recipientId: userId }],
    orderBy: { field: 'createdAt', direction: 'desc' },
    limit: 1000,
  }).forEach((message) => ids.add(message.senderId === userId ? message.recipientId : message.senderId));
  const postedJobs = db.findMany('jobs', { where: { posterId: userId }, limit: 500 });
  const postedJobIds = postedJobs.map((job) => job.id);
  if (postedJobIds.length) db.findMany('quotes', { where: { jobId: { $in: postedJobIds } }, limit: 2000 }).forEach((quote) => ids.add(quote.workerId));
  db.findMany('quotes', { where: { workerId: userId }, limit: 1000 }).forEach((quote) => {
    const job = db.findById('jobs', quote.jobId);
    if (job) ids.add(job.posterId);
  });
  ids.delete(userId);
  ids.delete(null);
  return [...ids];
}

module.exports = { usersAreBlocked, relationshipExists, relatedUserIds };

// ===== src/repositories/workerRepository.js =====
const db = require('../db');
const { recordsByIds, pageRequest, paginationLinks } = require('./queryHelpers');
const { publicUser, publicWorkerProfile } = require('../services/viewModels');
const { verificationBadges, isActiveUntil } = require('../services/matchScorer');

function browse(req, currentUser) {
  const { page, perPage } = pageRequest(req, { perPage: 24, maxPerPage: 60 });
  const where = { status: 'active' };
  const or = [];
  if (req.query.q) {
    const term = `%${String(req.query.q).trim().replace(/[\\%_]/g, '\\$&')}%`;
    or.push({ displayName: { $like: term } }, { bio: { $like: term } }, { skills: { $like: term } });
  }
  if (req.query.maxRate) where.hourlyRate = { $lte: Number(req.query.maxRate) || Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER };
  if (req.query.vehicle === 'on') where.hasVehicle = true;
  if (req.query.insurance === 'verified') where.insuranceStatus = 'verified';
  if (req.query.wsib === 'verified') where.wsibStatus = 'verified';
  if (req.query.trade === 'verified') where.tradeCertificationStatus = 'verified';

  let orderBy = [
    { field: 'boostedUntil', direction: 'desc' },
    { field: 'completedJobs', direction: 'desc' },
  ];
  if (req.query.sort === 'rating') orderBy = [{ field: 'averageRating', direction: 'desc' }];
  if (req.query.sort === 'rate-low') orderBy = [{ field: 'hourlyRate', direction: 'asc' }];

  const result = db.paginate('workerProfiles', { page, perPage, where, or, orderBy });
  const users = recordsByIds('users', result.items.map((profile) => profile.userId));
  const savedProfileIds = currentUser
    ? new Set(db.findMany('savedWorkers', { where: { posterId: currentUser.id } }).map((item) => item.profileId))
    : new Set();
  let profiles = result.items.map((profile) => {
    const user = users.get(profile.userId);
    if (!user || user.accountStatus !== 'active') return null;
    return {
      ...publicWorkerProfile(profile),
      user: publicUser(user),
      badges: verificationBadges(profile, user),
      isBoosted: isActiveUntil(profile.boostedUntil),
      saved: savedProfileIds.has(profile.id),
    };
  }).filter(Boolean);
  if (req.query.city) {
    const city = String(req.query.city).toLowerCase();
    profiles = profiles.filter((profile) => String(profile.user?.city || '').toLowerCase().includes(city));
  }
  if (req.query.skill) {
    const skill = String(req.query.skill).toLowerCase();
    profiles = profiles.filter((profile) => (profile.skills || []).some((value) => String(value).toLowerCase().includes(skill)));
  }
  return { profiles, pagination: paginationLinks(req, result.pagination) };
}

function detail(profileId, currentUser) {
  const profile = db.findById('workerProfiles', profileId);
  if (!profile) return null;
  const user = db.findById('users', profile.userId);
  if (!user || user.accountStatus !== 'active') return null;
  const reviews = db.findMany('reviews', {
    where: { revieweeId: profile.userId },
    orderBy: { field: 'createdAt', direction: 'desc' },
    limit: 100,
  });
  const reviewers = recordsByIds('users', reviews.map((review) => review.reviewerId));
  const saved = currentUser
    ? Boolean(db.findOne('savedWorkers', { where: { posterId: currentUser.id, profileId } }))
    : false;
  return {
    profile: {
      ...publicWorkerProfile(profile),
      isBoosted: isActiveUntil(profile.boostedUntil),
      badges: verificationBadges(profile, user),
    },
    user: publicUser(user),
    reviews: reviews.map((review) => ({ ...review, reviewer: publicUser(reviewers.get(review.reviewerId)) })),
    saved,
  };
}

module.exports = { browse, detail };

// ===== src/routes/alertRoutes.js =====
const express = require('express');
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');
const db = require('../repositories/store');
const { requireAuth } = require('../middleware/auth');
const { formatDateTime } = require('../utils/format');
const { alert: validateAlert } = require('../services/inputSchemas');
const { pageRequest, paginationLinks } = require('../repositories/queryHelpers');

const router = express.Router();
router.use(requireAuth);

router.get('/', (req, res) => {
  const currentUser = res.locals.currentUser;
  const paging = pageRequest(req, { perPage: 25 });
  const { items: alerts, pagination } = db.paginate('jobAlerts', {
    ...paging,
    where: { userId: currentUser.id },
    orderBy: { field: 'createdAt', direction: 'desc' },
  });
  res.render('alerts/index', { title: 'Job alerts', alerts, pagination: paginationLinks(req, pagination), categories: db.categories, formatDateTime });
});

router.post('/', (req, res) => {
  const currentUser = res.locals.currentUser;
  const parsed = validateAlert(req.body);
  if (!parsed.success) {
    req.flash('error', parsed.errors.join(' '));
    return res.redirect('/alerts');
  }
  if (parsed.data.categoryId && !db.categories.some((category) => category.id === parsed.data.categoryId)) {
    req.flash('error', 'Choose a valid category.');
    return res.redirect('/alerts');
  }

  db.insert('jobAlerts', {
    id: uuidv4(),
    userId: currentUser.id,
    ...parsed.data,
    lastMatchedAt: null,
    createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
  });

  req.flash('success', 'Job alert saved. Delivery is scaffolded for email/SMS/push integration.');
  return res.redirect('/alerts');
});

router.post('/:id/toggle', (req, res) => {
  const currentUser = res.locals.currentUser;
  const alert = db.findById('jobAlerts', req.params.id);
  if (!alert || alert.userId !== currentUser.id) {
    req.flash('error', 'Alert not found.');
    return res.redirect('/alerts');
  }
  const enabled = !alert.enabled;
  db.update('jobAlerts', alert.id, { enabled });
  req.flash('success', `Alert ${enabled ? 'enabled' : 'paused'}.`);
  return res.redirect('/alerts');
});

router.post('/:id/delete', (req, res) => {
  const currentUser = res.locals.currentUser;
  const alert = db.findById('jobAlerts', req.params.id);
  if (!alert || alert.userId !== currentUser.id) {
    req.flash('error', 'Alert not found.');
    return res.redirect('/alerts');
  }
  db.remove('jobAlerts', alert.id);
  req.flash('success', 'Alert deleted.');
  return res.redirect('/alerts');
});

module.exports = router;

// ===== src/routes/apiRoutes.js =====
const express = require('express');
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');
const db = require('../repositories/store');
const { isActiveUntil } = require('../services/matchScorer');
const { publicSeoLinks } = require('../services/seo');
const { compact } = require('../utils/format');
const { createJobTx, JobInputError } = require('../services/jobService');
const { requireApiKey } = require('../middleware/apiKey');
const { requireAuthApi, requireAdminApi } = require('../middleware/auth');

const router = express.Router();

function pageParams(req, max = 100) {
  const limit = Math.min(max, Math.max(1, Number.parseInt(req.query.limit, 10) || 50));
  const offset = Math.max(0, Number.parseInt(req.query.offset, 10) || 0);
  return { limit, offset };
}

router.get('/health', (_req, res) => {
  res.set('Cache-Control', 'no-store');
  res.json({ ok: true, app: 'NeighbourTask', uptimeSeconds: Math.floor(process.uptime()) });
});

router.get('/ready', (_req, res) => {
  res.set('Cache-Control', 'no-store');
  try {
    db.ready();
    return res.json({ ok: true, database: 'ready' });
  } catch (_error) {
    return res.status(503).json({ ok: false, database: 'unavailable' });
  }
});

router.get('/jobs', (req, res) => {
  const { limit, offset } = pageParams(req);
  const total = db.count('jobs', { status: 'open' });
  const jobs = db.findMany('jobs', {
    where: { status: 'open' },
    orderBy: { field: 'createdAt', direction: 'desc' },
    limit,
    offset,
  }).map((job) => ({
    id: job.id,
    title: job.title,
    city: job.city,
    categoryId: job.categoryId,
    payType: job.payType,
    budgetMin: job.budgetMin,
    budgetMax: job.budgetMax,
    urgency: job.urgency,
    riskLevel: job.riskLevel,
    isFeatured: isActiveUntil(job.featuredUntil),
    createdAt: job.createdAt,
    url: `/jobs/${job.id}`,
  })).sort((a, b) => {
    if (a.isFeatured !== b.isFeatured) return a.isFeatured ? -1 : 1;
    return new Date(b.createdAt) - new Date(a.createdAt);
  });
  res.json({ jobs, total, limit, offset });
});

router.get('/workers', (req, res) => {
  const { limit, offset } = pageParams(req);
  const profiles = db.findMany('workerProfiles', {
    where: { status: 'active' },
    limit,
    offset,
  });
  const userIds = profiles.map((profile) => profile.userId).filter(Boolean);
  const usersById = new Map(db.findMany('users', {
    where: { id: { $in: userIds }, accountStatus: 'active' },
  }).map((user) => [user.id, user]));
  const workers = profiles.map((profile) => {
    const user = usersById.get(profile.userId);
    if (!user) return null;
    return {
      id: profile.id,
      displayName: profile.displayName,
      city: user.city || '',
      skills: profile.skills || [],
      hourlyRate: profile.hourlyRate,
      completedJobs: profile.completedJobs,
      averageRating: profile.averageRating,
      isBoosted: isActiveUntil(profile.boostedUntil),
      url: `/workers/${profile.id}`,
    };
  }).filter(Boolean);
  res.json({ workers, total: db.count('workerProfiles', { status: 'active' }), limit, offset });
});

router.get('/businesses/:userId/summary', requireAuthApi, (req, res) => {
  const currentUser = res.locals.currentUser;
  if (currentUser.id !== req.params.userId && !currentUser.isAdmin) {
    return res.status(403).json({ error: 'You cannot access that business account.' });
  }
  const business = db.findOne('businessAccounts', { where: { userId: req.params.userId } });
  if (!business) return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Business account not found.' });
  return res.json({
    business: {
      id: business.id,
      businessName: business.businessName,
      businessType: business.businessType,
      website: business.website,
      phone: business.phone,
      billingEmail: business.billingEmail,
      plan: business.plan,
      status: business.status,
    },
    locations: db.findMany('businessLocations', { where: { businessId: business.id } }),
    templates: db.findMany('recurringTaskTemplates', { where: { businessId: business.id } }),
    preferredWorkers: db.findMany('preferredWorkers', { where: { businessId: business.id } }),
  });
});

router.get('/seo-links', (_req, res) => {
  res.json({ links: publicSeoLinks({
    seoLocations: db.seoLocations,
    categoryGuides: db.categoryGuides,
    categories: db.categories,
  }) });
});

router.get('/admin-metrics-lite', requireAdminApi, (_req, res) => {
  res.set('Cache-Control', 'private, no-store');
  res.json({
    users: db.count('users'),
    jobs: db.count('jobs'),
    quotes: db.count('quotes'),
    businesses: db.count('businessAccounts'),
    moderationCases: db.count('moderationCases', { status: { $ne: 'closed' } }),
    auditEntries: db.count('auditLog'),
  });
});

router.post('/jobs', requireApiKey, (req, res, next) => {
  try {
    const job = db.transaction((tx) => {
      let hermesUser = tx.users.findOne({ where: { email: 'hermes@neighbourtask.local' } });
      if (!hermesUser) {
        const now = new Date().toISOString();
        hermesUser = {
          id: uuidv4(),
          email: 'hermes@neighbourtask.local',
          phone: '',
          passwordHash: '',
          name: 'Hermes API',
          role: 'poster',
          city: 'Toronto',
          postalCode: '',
          isAdmin: false,
          phoneVerified: false,
          accountStatus: 'active',
          createdAt: now,
          updatedAt: now,
        };
        tx.users.insert(hermesUser);
      }

      return createJobTx(tx, db.categories, {
        posterId: hermesUser.id,
        input: {
          ...req.body,
          photos: [],
        },
      });
    });
    res.status(201).json({ id: job.id });
  } catch (error) {
    if (error instanceof JobInputError) return res.status(422).json({ errors: error.errors });
    return next(error);
  }
});

module.exports = router;

// ===== src/routes/businessRoutes.js =====
