// ===== src/routes/dashboardRoutes.js =====
const express = require('express');
const db = require('../repositories/store');
const { requireAuth } = require('../middleware/auth');
const { isActiveUntil } = require('../services/matchScorer');
const { lifecycleForJob } = require('../services/jobLifecycle');
const { workerChecklist, posterChecklist } = require('../services/onboarding');
const { formatDate, formatDateTime } = require('../utils/format');
const { accountUser } = require('../services/viewModels');

const router = express.Router();

function mapBy(items, key = 'id') {
  return new Map(items.map((item) => [item[key], item]));
}

router.get('/', requireAuth, (req, res) => {
  const currentUser = res.locals.currentUser;
  const myJobsRaw = db.findMany('jobs', {
    where: { posterId: currentUser.id },
    orderBy: { field: 'createdAt', direction: 'desc' },
    limit: 20,
  });
  const myJobIds = myJobsRaw.map((job) => job.id);
  const quoteCounts = db.groupCount('quotes', 'jobId', myJobIds);
  const myJobs = myJobsRaw.map((job) => ({
    ...job,
    quoteCount: quoteCounts.get(job.id) || 0,
    isFeatured: isActiveUntil(job.featuredUntil),
    lifecycle: lifecycleForJob(job),
  }));

  const myQuotesRaw = db.findMany('quotes', {
    where: { workerId: currentUser.id },
    orderBy: { field: 'createdAt', direction: 'desc' },
    limit: 20,
  });
  const quoteJobIds = [...new Set(myQuotesRaw.map((quote) => quote.jobId).filter(Boolean))];
  const quotedJobsById = mapBy(db.findMany('jobs', { where: { id: { $in: quoteJobIds } } }));
  const myQuotes = myQuotesRaw.map((quote) => ({ ...quote, job: quotedJobsById.get(quote.jobId) || null }));

  const quotesForMyJobsRaw = myJobIds.length
    ? db.findMany('quotes', {
      where: { jobId: { $in: myJobIds } },
      orderBy: { field: 'createdAt', direction: 'desc' },
    })
    : [];
  const quoteWorkerIds = [...new Set(quotesForMyJobsRaw.map((quote) => quote.workerId).filter(Boolean))];
  const quoteWorkersById = mapBy(db.findMany('users', { where: { id: { $in: quoteWorkerIds } } }));
  const quoteProfilesByUserId = mapBy(
    db.findMany('workerProfiles', { where: { userId: { $in: quoteWorkerIds } } }),
    'userId',
  );
  const myJobsById = mapBy(myJobsRaw);
  const quotesForMyJobs = quotesForMyJobsRaw.map((quote) => ({
    ...quote,
    job: myJobsById.get(quote.jobId) || null,
    worker: accountUser(quoteWorkersById.get(quote.workerId)),
    profile: quoteProfilesByUserId.get(quote.workerId) || null,
  }));

  const workerProfile = db.findOne('workerProfiles', { where: { userId: currentUser.id } });
  const businessAccount = db.findOne('businessAccounts', { where: { userId: currentUser.id } });

  const savedWorkersRaw = db.findMany('savedWorkers', {
    where: { posterId: currentUser.id },
    orderBy: { field: 'createdAt', direction: 'desc' },
  });
  const savedWorkerIds = [...new Set(savedWorkersRaw.map((saved) => saved.workerId).filter(Boolean))];
  const savedProfileIds = [...new Set(savedWorkersRaw.map((saved) => saved.profileId).filter(Boolean))];
  const savedUsersById = mapBy(db.findMany('users', { where: { id: { $in: savedWorkerIds } } }));
  const savedProfilesById = mapBy(db.findMany('workerProfiles', { where: { id: { $in: savedProfileIds } } }));
  const savedWorkers = savedWorkersRaw.map((saved) => ({
    ...saved,
    profile: savedProfilesById.get(saved.profileId) || null,
    worker: accountUser(savedUsersById.get(saved.workerId)),
  })).filter((saved) => saved.profile && saved.worker);

  const recentMessagesRaw = db.findMany('messages', {
    or: [{ senderId: currentUser.id }, { recipientId: currentUser.id }],
    orderBy: { field: 'createdAt', direction: 'desc' },
    limit: 5,
  });
  const messageUserIds = [...new Set(recentMessagesRaw.flatMap((message) => [message.senderId, message.recipientId]).filter(Boolean))];
  const messageJobIds = [...new Set(recentMessagesRaw.map((message) => message.jobId).filter(Boolean))];
  const messageUsersById = mapBy(db.findMany('users', { where: { id: { $in: messageUserIds } } }));
  const messageJobsById = mapBy(db.findMany('jobs', { where: { id: { $in: messageJobIds } } }));
  const recentMessages = recentMessagesRaw.map((message) => ({
    ...message,
    sender: accountUser(messageUsersById.get(message.senderId)),
    recipient: accountUser(messageUsersById.get(message.recipientId)),
    job: messageJobsById.get(message.jobId) || null,
  }));

  const myPromotions = db.findMany('promotions', {
    where: { userId: currentUser.id },
    orderBy: { field: 'createdAt', direction: 'desc' },
    limit: 5,
  });
  const myPayments = db.findMany('paymentRequests', {
    or: [{ posterId: currentUser.id }, { workerId: currentUser.id }],
    orderBy: { field: 'createdAt', direction: 'desc' },
    limit: 5,
  });
  const myDisputes = db.findMany('disputes', {
    or: [{ openedById: currentUser.id }, { respondentId: currentUser.id }],
    orderBy: { field: 'createdAt', direction: 'desc' },
    limit: 5,
  });
  const myAlerts = db.findMany('jobAlerts', {
    where: { userId: currentUser.id },
    orderBy: { field: 'createdAt', direction: 'desc' },
    limit: 5,
  });

  const documents = db.findMany('documents', { where: { workerId: currentUser.id } });
  const payoutAccount = db.findOne('payoutAccounts', { where: { userId: currentUser.id } });
  const myPosterJobs = db.findMany('jobs', { where: { posterId: currentUser.id } });

  res.render('pages/dashboard', {
    title: 'Dashboard',
    myJobs,
    myQuotes,
    quotesForMyJobs,
    workerProfile,
    businessAccount,
    savedWorkers,
    recentMessages,
    myPromotions,
    myPayments,
    myDisputes,
    myAlerts,
    onboardingChecklist: currentUser.role === 'worker' || currentUser.role === 'both'
      ? workerChecklist(currentUser, workerProfile, documents, payoutAccount)
      : posterChecklist(currentUser, null, myPosterJobs),
    formatDate,
    formatDateTime,
  });
});

module.exports = router;

// ===== src/routes/disputeRoutes.js =====
const express = require('express');
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');
const db = require('../repositories/store');
const privateUpload = require('../middleware/privateUpload');
const { handleMulterError } = require('../middleware/upload');
const { validateMultipartCsrf } = require('../middleware/csrf');
const { requireAuth } = require('../middleware/auth');
const { compact, formatDateTime } = require('../utils/format');
const { canTransition } = require('../services/stateMachine');
const { accountUser } = require('../services/viewModels');
const { registerPrivateFile } = require('../services/privateFiles');
const { discardUploadedFiles } = require('../utils/uploads');
const { dispute: validateDispute, disputeEvidence: validateDisputeEvidence } = require('../services/inputSchemas');
const { recordsByIds, pageRequest, paginationLinks } = require('../repositories/queryHelpers');

const router = express.Router();
router.use(requireAuth);

function userCanAccessJob(user, job) {
  return user.isAdmin || job.posterId === user.id || job.hiredWorkerId === user.id;
}

router.get('/', (req, res) => {
  const currentUser = res.locals.currentUser;
  const paging = pageRequest(req, { perPage: 25 });
  const { items: disputes, pagination } = db.paginate('disputes', {
    ...paging,
    or: [{ openedById: currentUser.id }, { respondentId: currentUser.id }],
    orderBy: { field: 'createdAt', direction: 'desc' },
  });

  const jobIds = [...new Set(disputes.map((d) => d.jobId).filter(Boolean))];
  const paymentIds = [...new Set(disputes.map((d) => d.paymentRequestId).filter(Boolean))];
  const userIds = [...new Set(disputes.flatMap((d) => [d.openedById, d.respondentId]).filter(Boolean))];
  const jobsById = recordsByIds('jobs', jobIds);
  const paymentsById = recordsByIds('paymentRequests', paymentIds);
  const usersById = recordsByIds('users', userIds);

  const enrichedDisputes = disputes.map((dispute) => ({
    ...dispute,
    job: jobsById.get(dispute.jobId) || null,
    payment: paymentsById.get(dispute.paymentRequestId) || null,
    openedBy: accountUser(usersById.get(dispute.openedById)),
    respondent: accountUser(usersById.get(dispute.respondentId)),
  }));

  res.render('disputes/index', { title: 'Disputes', disputes: enrichedDisputes, pagination: paginationLinks(req, pagination), formatDateTime });
});

router.post('/', (req, res) => {
  const currentUser = res.locals.currentUser;
  const parsed = validateDispute(req.body);
  if (!parsed.success) {
    req.flash('error', parsed.errors.join(' '));
    return res.redirect('/disputes');
  }
  const job = db.findById('jobs', parsed.data.jobId);
  const payment = parsed.data.paymentRequestId
    ? db.findById('paymentRequests', parsed.data.paymentRequestId)
    : null;

  if (!job || !userCanAccessJob(currentUser, job)) {
    req.flash('error', 'You can only open disputes for jobs you are involved in.');
    return res.redirect('/disputes');
  }

  const respondentId = currentUser.id === job.posterId ? job.hiredWorkerId : job.posterId;
  if (!respondentId) {
    req.flash('error', 'A dispute needs both a poster and a hired worker.');
    return res.redirect('/disputes');
  }

  db.insert('disputes', {
    id: uuidv4(),
    jobId: job.id,
    paymentRequestId: payment && payment.jobId === job.id ? payment.id : null,
    openedById: currentUser.id,
    respondentId,
    reason: parsed.data.reason,
    requestedOutcome: parsed.data.requestedOutcome,
    description: parsed.data.description,
    status: 'open',
    adminNotes: '',
    resolution: '',
    createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
  });

  req.flash('success', 'Dispute opened for admin review.');
  return res.redirect('/disputes');
});

router.post('/:id/evidence', privateUpload.single('evidence'), handleMulterError('/disputes'), validateMultipartCsrf, (req, res) => {
  const currentUser = res.locals.currentUser;
  const dispute = db.findById('disputes', req.params.id);
  if (!dispute || (dispute.openedById !== currentUser.id && dispute.respondentId !== currentUser.id && !currentUser.isAdmin)) {
    discardUploadedFiles(req);
    req.flash('error', 'Dispute not found.');
    return res.redirect('/disputes');
  }
  const parsed = validateDisputeEvidence(req.body);
  if (!parsed.success) {
    discardUploadedFiles(req);
    req.flash('error', parsed.errors.join(' '));
    return res.redirect('/disputes');
  }
  const evidence = {
    id: uuidv4(),
    disputeId: dispute.id,
    uploadedById: currentUser.id,
    type: parsed.data.type,
    description: parsed.data.description,
    fileUrl: null,
    fileId: null,
    originalName: req.file ? req.file.originalname : '',
    status: 'submitted',
    adminNotes: '',
    createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
  };
  db.transaction((tx) => {
    if (req.file) {
      const privateFile = registerPrivateFile(tx, req.file, { ownerId: currentUser.id, contextType: 'disputeEvidence', contextId: evidence.id });
      evidence.fileId = privateFile.id;
      evidence.fileUrl = `/files/${privateFile.id}`;
    }
    tx.disputeEvidence.insert(evidence);
    if (canTransition('dispute', dispute.status, 'reviewing')) {
      tx.disputes.update(dispute.id, { status: 'reviewing', updatedAt: new Date().toISOString() });
    }
  });
  req.flash('success', 'Dispute evidence saved.');
  return res.redirect('/disputes');
});

module.exports = router;

const express = require('express');
const db = require('../repositories/store');
const { requireAuth } = require('../middleware/auth');
const { formatDateTime } = require('../utils/format');
const { pageRequest, paginationLinks } = require('../repositories/queryHelpers');

const router = express.Router();
router.use(requireAuth);

router.get('/', (req, res) => {
  const currentUser = res.locals.currentUser;
  const paging = pageRequest(req, { perPage: 30 });
  const { items: notifications, pagination } = db.paginate('notifications', {
    ...paging,
    where: { userId: currentUser.id },
    orderBy: { field: 'createdAt', direction: 'desc' },
  });
  res.render('notifications/index', { title: 'Notifications', notifications, pagination: paginationLinks(req, pagination), formatDateTime });
});

router.post('/:id/read', (req, res) => {
  const notification = db.findById('notifications', req.params.id);
  if (notification && notification.userId === res.locals.currentUser.id && !notification.readAt) {
    db.update('notifications', notification.id, { readAt: new Date().toISOString() });
  }
  req.flash('success', 'Notification marked as read.');
  return res.redirect('/notifications');
});

// ===== src/routes/pageRoutes.js =====
const express = require('express');
const db = require('../repositories/store');
const { formatDate } = require('../utils/format');
const { publicSeoLinks, buildSeoPage } = require('../services/seo');
const { publicBaseUrl } = require('../utils/security');

const seoData = () => ({ seoLocations: db.seoLocations, categoryGuides: db.categoryGuides, categories: db.categories });

const router = express.Router();

router.get('/', (req, res) => {
  const openJobs = db.findMany('jobs', {
    where: { status: 'open' },
    orderBy: { field: 'createdAt', direction: 'desc' },
    limit: 6,
  });
  const workerProfiles = db.findMany('workerProfiles', {
    where: { status: 'active' },
    limit: 6,
  });
  res.render('pages/home', {
    title: 'NeighbourTask Canada',
    metaDescription: 'Post local odd jobs, compare quotes from independent workers, and hire directly in Toronto and the GTA.',
    jobs: openJobs,
    workerProfiles,
    seoLinks: publicSeoLinks(seoData()).slice(0, 18),
    formatDate,
  });
});

router.get('/how-it-works', (req, res) => res.render('pages/howItWorks', { title: 'How it works' }));
router.get('/safety', (req, res) => res.render('pages/safety', { title: 'Safety and hiring guide' }));
router.get('/terms', (req, res) => res.render('pages/terms', { title: 'Terms of use' }));
router.get('/privacy', (req, res) => res.render('pages/privacy', { title: 'Privacy policy' }));
router.get('/legal', (req, res) => res.render('pages/legal', { title: 'Legal notes' }));
router.get('/mobile', (req, res) => res.render('pages/mobile', { title: 'Mobile app / PWA' }));
router.get('/mobile/post', (req, res) => res.render('pages/mobilePost', { title: 'Camera-first task post' }));
router.get('/sitemap.xml', (req, res) => {
  const baseUrl = publicBaseUrl(req);
  const staticUrls = ['/', '/jobs', '/workers', '/how-it-works', '/safety', '/mobile'];
  const seoUrls = publicSeoLinks(seoData()).map((link) => link.url);
  const urls = [...staticUrls, ...seoUrls].map((url) => `  <url><loc>${baseUrl}${url}</loc></url>`).join('\n');
  res.header('Content-Type', 'application/xml');
  res.send(`<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>\n<urlset xmlns="http://www.sitemaps.org/schemas/sitemap/0.9">\n${urls}\n</urlset>`);
});

router.get('/robots.txt', (req, res) => {
  res.type('text/plain');
  res.send(`User-agent: *\nAllow: /\nSitemap: ${publicBaseUrl(req)}/sitemap.xml\n`);
});

router.get('/:city(toronto|north-york|scarborough|etobicoke|mississauga|brampton|vaughan|markham|richmond-hill|oakville|burlington|hamilton)/:category', (req, res, next) => {
  const data = seoData();
  const seoPage = buildSeoPage(data, req.params.city, req.params.category);
  if (!seoPage) return next();
  return res.render('pages/seoLanding', {
    title: seoPage.title,
    metaDescription: seoPage.description,
    structuredData: seoPage.structuredData,
    ...seoPage,
    allSeoLinks: publicSeoLinks(data).filter((link) => link.location.id === seoPage.location.id).slice(0, 12),
  });
});

// ===== src/routes/posterRoutes.js =====
const express = require('express');
const db = require('../repositories/store');
const upload = require('../middleware/upload');
const { handleMulterError } = require('../middleware/upload');
const { validateMultipartCsrf } = require('../middleware/csrf');
const { requireAuth } = require('../middleware/auth');
const { compact, formatDateTime } = require('../utils/format');
const { publicUser, publicPosterProfile } = require('../services/viewModels');
const { posterProfile: validatePosterProfile } = require('../services/inputSchemas');
const { discardUploadedFiles } = require('../utils/uploads');
const { posterChecklist } = require('../services/onboarding');
const posterRepository = require('../repositories/posterRepository');
const { createDefaultProfile, saveProfile } = require('../domains/posters/posterService');

const router = express.Router();

router.get('/profile', requireAuth, (req, res) => {
  const currentUser = db.findById('users', res.locals.currentUser.id);
  const profile = posterRepository.findByUserId(currentUser.id) || createDefaultProfile(currentUser);
  const myJobs = posterRepository.jobsForPoster(currentUser.id, { limit: 100 });
  const onboardingChecklist = posterChecklist(currentUser, profile, myJobs);
  return res.render('posters/profile', {
    title: 'Employer profile',
    profile,
    formatDateTime,
    onboardingChecklist,
    autosave: { key: 'poster-profile', enabled: true },
  });
});

router.post('/profile', requireAuth, upload.single('logo'), handleMulterError('/posters/profile'), validateMultipartCsrf, (req, res, next) => {
  const currentUser = db.findById('users', res.locals.currentUser.id);
  const parsed = validatePosterProfile({
    ...req.body,
    displayName: compact(req.body.displayName) || currentUser.name,
  });
  if (parsed.errors.length) {
    discardUploadedFiles(req);
    req.flash('error', parsed.errors.join(' '));
    return res.redirect('/posters/profile');
  }

  try {
    const profile = saveProfile({
      userId: currentUser.id,
      values: parsed.data,
      logoUrl: req.file ? `/uploads/${req.file.filename}` : null,
    });
    if (!profile) {
      discardUploadedFiles(req);
      req.flash('error', 'Account not found.');
      return res.redirect('/auth/login');
    }
    req.flash('success', 'Employer profile saved.');
    return res.redirect('/posters/profile');
  } catch (error) {
    discardUploadedFiles(req);
    return next(error);
  }
});

router.get('/:id', (req, res) => {
  const profile = posterRepository.findById(req.params.id);
  if (!profile) return res.status(404).render('pages/404', { title: 'Employer not found' });
  const user = db.findById('users', profile.userId);
  const activeJobs = db.count('jobs', { posterId: profile.userId, status: 'open' });
  const reviews = db.findMany('reviews', { where: { revieweeId: profile.userId } });
  const avgRating = reviews.length ? Math.round((reviews.reduce((s, r) => s + Number(r.rating || 0), 0) / reviews.length) * 10) / 10 : null;

  return res.render('posters/show', {
    title: profile.displayName,
    profile: publicPosterProfile(profile),
    user: publicUser(user),
    activeJobs,
    reviews,
    avgRating,
  });
});

module.exports = router;

// ===== src/routes/privateFileRoutes.js =====
const fs = require('fs');
const express = require('express');
const db = require('../repositories/store');
const { requireAuth } = require('../middleware/auth');
const { canAccessPrivateFileTx, absolutePrivatePath } = require('../services/privateFiles');

const router = express.Router();
router.use(requireAuth);

router.get('/:id', (req, res) => {
  const file = db.transaction((tx) => {
    const record = tx.privateFiles.findById(req.params.id);
    return record && canAccessPrivateFileTx(tx, res.locals.currentUser, record) ? record : null;
  }, 'deferred');
  if (!file) return res.status(404).render('pages/404', { title: 'File not found' });

  const absolutePath = absolutePrivatePath(file);
  if (!absolutePath || !fs.existsSync(absolutePath)) {
    return res.status(404).render('pages/404', { title: 'File not found' });
  }
  return res.sendFile(absolutePath);
});

module.exports = router;

// ===== src/routes/promotionRoutes.js =====
const express = require('express');
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');
const db = require('../repositories/store');
const { requireAuth } = require('../middleware/auth');
const { compact } = require('../utils/format');
const { recordsByIds, pageRequest, paginationLinks } = require('../repositories/queryHelpers');

const router = express.Router();
router.use(requireAuth);

const promotionPrices = {
  'job-feature-7': 19,
  'job-feature-30': 49,
  'profile-boost-7': 15,
  'profile-boost-30': 39,
};

router.get('/', (req, res) => {
  const currentUser = res.locals.currentUser;
  const paging = pageRequest(req, { perPage: 25 });
  const myJobs = db.findMany('jobs', { where: { posterId: currentUser.id } });
  const myProfile = db.findOne('workerProfiles', { where: { userId: currentUser.id } });
  const { items: myPromotions, pagination } = db.paginate('promotions', {
    ...paging,
    where: { userId: currentUser.id },
    orderBy: { field: 'createdAt', direction: 'desc' },
  });

  const jobIds = myPromotions.filter((p) => p.targetId).map((p) => p.targetId);
  const profileIds = myPromotions.filter((p) => p.type === 'profile-boost').map((p) => p.targetId);
  const jobsById = recordsByIds('jobs', jobIds);
  const profilesById = recordsByIds('workerProfiles', profileIds);

  const enrichedPromotions = myPromotions.map((promotion) => ({
    ...promotion,
    job: jobsById.get(promotion.targetId) || null,
    profile: profilesById.get(promotion.targetId) || null,
  }));

  res.render('promotions/index', {
    title: 'Promotions',
    myJobs,
    myProfile,
    myPromotions: enrichedPromotions,
    promotionPrices,
    pagination: paginationLinks(req, pagination),
  });
});

router.post('/', (req, res) => {
  const currentUser = res.locals.currentUser;
  const type = compact(req.body.type);
  const targetId = compact(req.body.targetId);
  const durationDays = Number(req.body.durationDays || 7);
  const priceKey = `${type}-${durationDays}`;

  if (!['job-feature', 'profile-boost'].includes(type) || !promotionPrices[priceKey]) {
    req.flash('error', 'Invalid promotion type.');
    return res.redirect('/promotions');
  }

  if (type === 'job-feature') {
    const job = db.findOne('jobs', { where: { id: targetId, posterId: currentUser.id } });
    if (!job) {
      req.flash('error', 'You can only feature your own jobs.');
      return res.redirect('/promotions');
    }
  }

  if (type === 'profile-boost') {
    const profile = db.findOne('workerProfiles', { where: { id: targetId, userId: currentUser.id } });
    if (!profile) {
      req.flash('error', 'You can only boost your own worker profile.');
      return res.redirect('/promotions');
    }
  }

  db.insert('promotions', {
    id: uuidv4(),
    userId: currentUser.id,
    type,
    targetId,
    durationDays,
    price: promotionPrices[priceKey],
    status: 'pending',
    paymentStatus: 'demo-unpaid',
    adminNotes: '',
    createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
  });

  req.flash('success', 'Promotion request created. In this demo, an admin activates it after review/payment confirmation.');
  return res.redirect('/promotions');
});

module.exports = router;

// ===== src/routes/reportRoutes.js =====
const express = require('express');
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const db = require('../repositories/store');
const { requireAuth } = require('../middleware/auth');
const { compact } = require('../utils/format');
const { safeRedirectTarget } = require('../utils/security');
const { report: validateReport } = require('../services/inputSchemas');

const router = express.Router();
const reportLimiter = rateLimit({ windowMs: 60 * 60 * 1000, max: 10, standardHeaders: true, legacyHeaders: false });

router.post('/', requireAuth, reportLimiter, (req, res) => {
  const currentUser = res.locals.currentUser;
  const back = safeRedirectTarget(req, req.get('Referrer'), '/');
  const parsed = validateReport(req.body);
  if (!parsed.success) {
    req.flash('error', parsed.errors.join(' '));
    return res.redirect(back);
  }
  const reportedUser = parsed.data.reportedUserId
    ? db.findById('users', parsed.data.reportedUserId)
    : null;
  const job = parsed.data.jobId ? db.findById('jobs', parsed.data.jobId) : null;

  if (!reportedUser && !job) {
    req.flash('error', 'Choose a valid user or job to report.');
    return res.redirect(back);
  }
  if (reportedUser && reportedUser.id === currentUser.id) {
    req.flash('error', 'You cannot report your own account.');
    return res.redirect(back);
  }

  if (job) {
    const relatedUserIds = new Set([job.posterId, job.hiredWorkerId].filter(Boolean));
    const jobQuotes = db.findMany('quotes', { where: { jobId: job.id } });
    jobQuotes.filter((quote) => quote.workerId).forEach((quote) => relatedUserIds.add(quote.workerId));
    if (!currentUser.isAdmin && !relatedUserIds.has(currentUser.id)) {
      req.flash('error', 'You can only report jobs you are involved with.');
      return res.redirect(back);
    }
    if (reportedUser && !relatedUserIds.has(reportedUser.id)) {
      req.flash('error', 'That user is not connected to this job.');
      return res.redirect(back);
    }
  }

  db.insert('reports', {
    id: uuidv4(),
    reporterId: currentUser.id,
    reportedUserId: reportedUser ? reportedUser.id : null,
    jobId: job ? job.id : null,
    reason: parsed.data.reason,
    description: parsed.data.description,
    status: 'open',
    adminNotes: '',
    createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
  });
  req.flash('success', 'Report submitted. Thank you for helping keep the marketplace safe.');
  return res.redirect(back);
});

module.exports = router;

// ===== src/routes/reviewRoutes.js =====
const express = require('express');
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');
const db = require('../repositories/store');
const { requireAuth } = require('../middleware/auth');
const { safeRedirectTarget } = require('../utils/security');
const { review: validateReview } = require('../services/inputSchemas');

const router = express.Router();
router.use(requireAuth);

function recalculateWorkerRating(userId) {
  const reviews = db.findMany('reviews', { where: { revieweeId: userId } });
  const relevantReviews = reviews.filter((review) => {
    const job = db.findById('jobs', review.jobId);
    return job && job.hiredWorkerId === userId;
  });
  const profile = db.findOne('workerProfiles', { where: { userId } });
  if (!profile) return;
  if (!relevantReviews.length) {
    const completedJobs = db.count('jobs', { hiredWorkerId: userId, status: 'completed' });
    db.update('workerProfiles', profile.id, { averageRating: null, completedJobs });
    return;
  }
  const total = relevantReviews.reduce((sum, review) => sum + Number(review.rating || 0), 0);
  const averageRating = Math.round((total / relevantReviews.length) * 10) / 10;
  const completedJobs = db.count('jobs', { hiredWorkerId: userId, status: 'completed' });
  db.update('workerProfiles', profile.id, { averageRating, completedJobs });
}

router.post('/', (req, res) => {
  const currentUser = res.locals.currentUser;
  const back = safeRedirectTarget(req, req.get('Referrer'), '/dashboard');
  const parsed = validateReview(req.body);
  if (!parsed.success) {
    req.flash('error', parsed.errors.join(' '));
    return res.redirect(back);
  }
  const job = db.findById('jobs', parsed.data.jobId);
  const rating = parsed.data.rating;

  if (!job || job.status !== 'completed' || !job.hiredWorkerId) {
    req.flash('error', 'Reviews are only available for completed jobs.');
    return res.redirect(back);
  }

  const canReview = currentUser.id === job.posterId || currentUser.id === job.hiredWorkerId;
  if (!canReview || !rating) {
    req.flash('error', 'Unable to submit that review.');
    return res.redirect(back);
  }

  const revieweeId = currentUser.id === job.posterId ? job.hiredWorkerId : job.posterId;
  const existing = db.findOne('reviews', { where: { jobId: job.id, reviewerId: currentUser.id, revieweeId } });
  if (existing) {
    req.flash('error', 'You already reviewed this person for this job.');
    return res.redirect(safeRedirectTarget(req, req.get('Referrer'), `/jobs/${job.id}`));
  }

  db.insert('reviews', {
    id: uuidv4(),
    jobId: job.id,
    reviewerId: currentUser.id,
    revieweeId,
    rating,
    communicationRating: parsed.data.communicationRating,
    qualityRating: parsed.data.qualityRating,
    reliabilityRating: parsed.data.reliabilityRating,
    comment: parsed.data.comment,
    createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
  });

  recalculateWorkerRating(revieweeId);
  recalculateWorkerRating(currentUser.id);
  req.flash('success', 'Review submitted.');
  return res.redirect(safeRedirectTarget(req, req.get('Referrer'), `/jobs/${job.id}`));
});

module.exports = router;

// ===== src/routes/workerRoutes.js =====
module.exports = require('../domains/workers/workerRoutes');

// ===== src/services/accessPolicy.js =====
function isAdmin(user) {
  return Boolean(user && user.isAdmin);
}

function isJobParticipant(user, job) {
  return Boolean(user && job && [job.posterId, job.hiredWorkerId].filter(Boolean).includes(user.id));
}

function canViewJob(user, job) {
  if (!job) return false;
  if (job.status === 'open') return true;
  return isAdmin(user) || isJobParticipant(user, job);
}

function canManageJob(user, job) {
  return Boolean(user && job && (isAdmin(user) || user.id === job.posterId));
}

function canViewQuote(user, job, quote) {
  return Boolean(user && job && quote && quote.jobId === job.id && (
    isAdmin(user) || user.id === job.posterId || user.id === quote.workerId
  ));
}

function canAccessPayment(user, payment) {
  return Boolean(user && payment && (isAdmin(user) || payment.posterId === user.id || payment.workerId === user.id));
}

function canAccessDispute(user, dispute) {
  return Boolean(user && dispute && (isAdmin(user) || dispute.openedById === user.id || dispute.respondentId === user.id));
}

function relationshipExists(data, firstUserId, secondUserId) {
  if (!firstUserId || !secondUserId || firstUserId === secondUserId) return false;
  if (data.messages.some((message) => (
    (message.senderId === firstUserId && message.recipientId === secondUserId)
    || (message.senderId === secondUserId && message.recipientId === firstUserId)
  ))) return true;

  return data.quotes.some((quote) => {
    if (!quote.workerId) return false;
    const job = data.jobs.find((candidate) => candidate.id === quote.jobId);
    return Boolean(job && (
      (job.posterId === firstUserId && quote.workerId === secondUserId)
      || (job.posterId === secondUserId && quote.workerId === firstUserId)
    ));
  });
}

function canMessageUsers(data, sender, recipient, job = null, quote = null) {
  if (!sender || !recipient || sender.id === recipient.id) return false;
  if (isAdmin(sender)) return true;
  if (job || quote) return canViewQuote(sender, job, quote)
    && [job.posterId, quote.workerId].includes(recipient.id);
  return relationshipExists(data, sender.id, recipient.id);
}

module.exports = {
  isAdmin,
  isJobParticipant,
  canViewJob,
  canManageJob,
  canViewQuote,
  canAccessPayment,
  canAccessDispute,
  relationshipExists,
  canMessageUsers,
};

// ===== src/services/audit.js =====
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');

function auditRecord(actorId, action, targetType, targetId, details = {}, severity = 'info') {
  return {
    id: uuidv4(),
    actorId: actorId || null,
    action,
    targetType,
    targetId: targetId || null,
    severity,
    meta: details,
    createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
  };
}

function addAudit(data, actorId, action, targetType, targetId, details = {}, severity = 'info') {
  if (!Array.isArray(data.auditLog)) data.auditLog = [];
  data.auditLog.push(auditRecord(actorId, action, targetType, targetId, details, severity));
}

function addAuditTx(tx, actorId, action, targetType, targetId, details = {}, severity = 'info') {
  tx.auditLog.insert(auditRecord(actorId, action, targetType, targetId, details, severity));
}

function moderationCaseRecord(attrs) {
  return {
    id: uuidv4(),
    targetType: attrs.targetType,
    targetId: attrs.targetId,
    reason: attrs.reason || 'Manual review',
    priority: attrs.priority || 'normal',
    status: 'open',
    assignedToId: attrs.assignedToId || null,
    adminNotes: attrs.adminNotes || '',
    createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
  };
}

function openModerationCase(data, attrs) {
  if (!Array.isArray(data.moderationCases)) data.moderationCases = [];
  const existing = data.moderationCases.find((item) => item.targetType === attrs.targetType && item.targetId === attrs.targetId && item.status !== 'closed');
  if (existing) return existing;
  const item = moderationCaseRecord(attrs);
  data.moderationCases.push(item);
  return item;
}

function openModerationCaseTx(tx, attrs) {
  const existing = tx.moderationCases.findOne({ where: { targetType: attrs.targetType, targetId: attrs.targetId, status: { $ne: 'closed' } } });
  if (existing) return existing;
  const item = moderationCaseRecord(attrs);
  tx.moderationCases.insert(item);
  return item;
}

function legalAcceptanceRecord(userId, documentType, version, source = 'web') {
  return {
    id: uuidv4(),
    userId,
    documentType,
    version,
    source,
    status: 'accepted',
    acceptedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
  };
}

function acceptLegal(data, userId, documentType, version, source = 'web') {
  if (!Array.isArray(data.legalAcceptances)) data.legalAcceptances = [];
  const acceptance = legalAcceptanceRecord(userId, documentType, version, source);
  data.legalAcceptances.push(acceptance);
  return acceptance;
}

function acceptLegalTx(tx, userId, documentType, version, source = 'web') {
  const acceptance = legalAcceptanceRecord(userId, documentType, version, source);
  tx.legalAcceptances.insert(acceptance);
  return acceptance;
}

module.exports = { auditRecord, addAudit, addAuditTx, moderationCaseRecord, openModerationCase, openModerationCaseTx, legalAcceptanceRecord, acceptLegal, acceptLegalTx };

// ===== src/services/businessTools.js =====
function businessMetrics(data, business, userId) {
  const jobs = data.jobs.filter((job) => job.posterId === userId);
  const quotes = data.quotes.filter((quote) => jobs.some((job) => job.id === quote.jobId));
  const payments = data.paymentRequests.filter((payment) => payment.posterId === userId || jobs.some((job) => job.id === payment.jobId));
  const totalSpend = payments
    .filter((payment) => ['external-paid', 'released'].includes(payment.status))
    .reduce((sum, payment) => sum + Number(payment.posterTotal || payment.amount || 0), 0);
  return {
    jobsPosted: jobs.length,
    openJobs: jobs.filter((job) => job.status === 'open').length,
    quotesReceived: quotes.length,
    totalSpend,
    preferredWorkers: data.preferredWorkers.filter((item) => item.businessId === business.id).length,
    recurringTemplates: data.recurringTaskTemplates.filter((item) => item.businessId === business.id && item.status !== 'archived').length,
  };
}

function toCsv(rows, headers) {
  const escape = (value) => {
    const text = String(value === undefined || value === null ? '' : value);
    if (/[",\n]/.test(text)) return `"${text.replace(/"/g, '""')}"`;
    return text;
  };
  return [headers.map((header) => escape(header.label)).join(','), ...rows.map((row) => headers.map((header) => escape(row[header.key])).join(','))].join('\n');
}

module.exports = { businessMetrics, toCsv };

// ===== src/services/inputSchema.js =====
const { compact, parseNumber } = require('../utils/format');
const { normalizeEmail } = require('../utils/security');

function labelFor(field, rule) {
  return rule.label || field.replace(/([A-Z])/g, ' $1').replace(/^./, (letter) => letter.toUpperCase());
}

function booleanValue(value) {
  return value === true || value === 1 || ['on', 'true', '1', 'yes'].includes(String(value || '').toLowerCase());
}

function stringValue(value, rule) {
  let result = rule.trim === false ? String(value ?? '') : compact(value);
  if (rule.lowercase) result = result.toLowerCase();
  if (rule.uppercase) result = result.toUpperCase();
  return result;
}

function parseField(field, rawValue, rule, errors) {
  const label = labelFor(field, rule);
  if (rule.type === 'boolean') return booleanValue(rawValue);

  if (rule.type === 'array') {
    const rawItems = rawValue === undefined || rawValue === null || rawValue === ''
      ? []
      : (Array.isArray(rawValue) ? rawValue : [rawValue]);
    const itemRule = rule.items || {};
    const values = rawItems.map((value) => {
      const item = stringValue(value, itemRule);
      if (itemRule.maxLength && item.length > itemRule.maxLength) {
        errors.push(`${label} items must be no more than ${itemRule.maxLength} characters.`);
        return item.slice(0, itemRule.maxLength);
      }
      return item;
    }).filter(Boolean);
    if (rule.maxItems && values.length > rule.maxItems) errors.push(`${label} may contain at most ${rule.maxItems} items.`);
    return [...new Set(values)].slice(0, rule.maxItems || values.length);
  }

  if (rule.type === 'number' || rule.type === 'integer') {
    const value = parseNumber(rawValue);
    if (value === null) {
      if (rule.required) errors.push(`${label} is required.`);
      return rule.default ?? null;
    }
    if (!Number.isFinite(value) || (rule.type === 'integer' && !Number.isInteger(value))) {
      errors.push(`${label} must be a valid ${rule.type}.`);
      return rule.default ?? null;
    }
    if (rule.min !== undefined && value < rule.min) errors.push(`${label} must be at least ${rule.min}.`);
    if (rule.max !== undefined && value > rule.max) errors.push(`${label} must be no more than ${rule.max}.`);
    return value;
  }

  const value = rule.type === 'email' ? normalizeEmail(rawValue) : stringValue(rawValue, rule);
  if (!value) {
    if (rule.required) errors.push(`${label} is required.`);
    return rule.default ?? '';
  }

  if (rule.minLength && value.length < rule.minLength) errors.push(`${label} must be at least ${rule.minLength} characters.`);
  if (rule.maxLength && value.length > rule.maxLength) errors.push(`${label} must be no more than ${rule.maxLength} characters.`);
  if (rule.pattern && !rule.pattern.test(value)) errors.push(rule.patternMessage || `${label} has an invalid format.`);

  if (rule.type === 'email' && !/^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/.test(value)) {
    errors.push(`${label} must be a valid email address.`);
  }
  if (rule.type === 'enum' && !(rule.values || []).includes(value)) {
    if (rule.default !== undefined) return rule.default;
    errors.push(`${label} is not valid.`);
  }
  if (rule.type === 'date') {
    const timestamp = new Date(value).getTime();
    if (Number.isNaN(timestamp)) errors.push(`${label} must be a valid date.`);
  }
  if (rule.type === 'url') {
    try {
      const parsed = new URL(value);
      if (!['http:', 'https:'].includes(parsed.protocol)) throw new Error('Unsupported protocol');
    } catch (_error) {
      errors.push(`${label} must be a valid HTTP or HTTPS URL.`);
    }
  }
  return value;
}

function parseInput(input, schema, { crossValidate } = {}) {
  const errors = [];
  const data = {};
  for (const [field, rule] of Object.entries(schema)) {
    data[field] = parseField(field, input ? input[field] : undefined, rule, errors);
  }
  if (typeof crossValidate === 'function') crossValidate(data, errors);
  return { success: errors.length === 0, data, errors };
}

module.exports = { parseInput, booleanValue };

// ===== src/services/inputSchemas.js =====
const { parseInput } = require('./inputSchema');
const { isStrongPassword } = require('../utils/security');

const text = (maxLength, options = {}) => ({ type: 'string', maxLength, ...options });
const optionalDate = (label) => ({ type: 'date', label, default: '' });

function registration(input) {
  const result = parseInput(input, {
    name: text(120, { required: true, minLength: 2 }),
    email: { type: 'email', required: true, maxLength: 254 },
    phone: text(40),
    password: { type: 'string', required: true, trim: false, maxLength: 200 },
    role: { type: 'enum', values: ['poster', 'worker', 'both'], default: 'poster' },
    city: text(120),
    postalCode: text(20, { uppercase: true }),
    terms: { type: 'boolean' },
  });
  if (result.data.password && !isStrongPassword(result.data.password)) {
    result.errors.push('Password must use 10+ characters with upper-case, lower-case, and a number.');
  }
  if (!result.data.terms) result.errors.push('You must accept the terms.');
  result.success = result.errors.length === 0;
  return result;
}

function message(input) {
  return parseInput(input, {
    recipientId: text(100, { required: true }),
    jobId: text(100),
    quoteId: text(100),
    body: text(5000),
  });
}

function report(input) {
  return parseInput(input, {
    reportedUserId: text(100),
    jobId: text(100),
    reason: text(120, { default: 'Other' }),
    description: text(5000, { required: true, minLength: 10 }),
  });
}

function review(input) {
  return parseInput(input, {
    jobId: text(100, { required: true }),
    rating: { type: 'integer', required: true, min: 1, max: 5 },
    communicationRating: { type: 'integer', min: 1, max: 5 },
    qualityRating: { type: 'integer', min: 1, max: 5 },
    reliabilityRating: { type: 'integer', min: 1, max: 5 },
    comment: text(3000),
  });
}

function dispute(input) {
  return parseInput(input, {
    jobId: text(100, { required: true }),
    paymentRequestId: text(100),
    reason: text(120, { default: 'Other' }),
    requestedOutcome: text(1000),
    description: text(5000, { required: true, minLength: 20 }),
  });
}

function alert(input) {
  return parseInput(input, {
    name: text(120, { default: 'My job alert' }),
    categoryId: text(100),
    city: text(120),
    keyword: text(120),
    maxDistanceKm: { type: 'number', min: 1, max: 500 },
    minBudget: { type: 'number', min: 0, max: 1_000_000 },
    frequency: { type: 'enum', values: ['instant', 'daily', 'weekly'], default: 'daily' },
    channel: { type: 'enum', values: ['email', 'sms', 'push-placeholder'], default: 'email' },
    enabled: { type: 'boolean' },
  });
}

function businessAccount(input, fallbackEmail = '') {
  return parseInput(input, {
    businessName: text(160, { required: true, minLength: 2 }),
    businessType: text(100, { default: 'small-business' }),
    website: { type: 'url', maxLength: 500, default: '' },
    phone: text(40),
    billingEmail: { type: 'email', maxLength: 254, default: fallbackEmail },
    locations: text(2000),
    plan: { type: 'enum', values: ['free', 'starter', 'pro'], default: 'free' },
    insuranceRequirements: text(2000),
    paymentTerms: text(2000),
    preferredWorkerNotes: text(3000),
  });
}

  return parseInput(input, {
    name: text(160, { required: true, minLength: 2 }),
    address: text(300, { required: true }),

  });
}

function recurringTemplate(input) {
  return parseInput(input, {
    title: text(160, { required: true, minLength: 5 }),
    categoryId: text(100, { default: 'general-labour' }),
    description: text(5000, { required: true, minLength: 20 }),
    defaultBudgetMin: { type: 'number', min: 0, max: 1_000_000 },
    defaultBudgetMax: { type: 'number', min: 0, max: 1_000_000 },
    estimatedHours: { type: 'number', min: 0.25, max: 10_000 },
    recurringPattern: text(500, { required: true }),
    toolsRequired: { type: 'boolean' },
    insuranceRequired: { type: 'boolean' },
    safetyWarningsAccepted: { type: 'boolean' },
  }, {
    crossValidate(data, errors) {
      if (data.defaultBudgetMin !== null && data.defaultBudgetMax !== null && data.defaultBudgetMin > data.defaultBudgetMax) {
        errors.push('Minimum budget cannot exceed maximum budget.');
      }
      if (!data.safetyWarningsAccepted) errors.push('You must accept the recurring-work safety warning.');
    },
  });
}
