// ===== src/services/jobLifecycle.js =====
const STEPS = [
  ['posted', 'Posted'],
  ['review', 'Safety review'],
  ['open', 'Open for quotes'],
  ['hired', 'Worker selected'],
  ['completed', 'Completed'],
];

function lifecycleForJob(job) {
  const state = job?.status || 'draft';
  const activeIndex = state === 'draft' ? -1 : state === 'review' ? 1 : state === 'open' ? 2 : state === 'hired' ? 3 : state === 'completed' ? 4 : 2;
  return STEPS.map(([key, label], index) => ({
    key, label, complete: index < activeIndex || (state === key), current: state === key,
  }));
}

module.exports = { lifecycleForJob };

// ===== src/services/jobService.js =====
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');
const { validateJobInput } = require('./validation');
const { scanJob } = require('./riskScanner');
const { notifyMatchingAlertsTx } = require('./marketplace');

class JobInputError extends Error {
  constructor(errors) {
    super(errors.join(' '));
    this.name = 'JobInputError';
    this.code = 'INVALID_JOB_INPUT';
    this.errors = errors;
  }
}

function buildJob({
  posterId,
  input,
  photos = [],
  adminNotes = '',
} = {}) {
  if (!posterId) throw new JobInputError(['A poster is required.']);
  const validation = validateJobInput(global.categories || [], input || {});
  if (validation.errors.length) throw new JobInputError(validation.errors);

  const values = validation.values;
  const riskScan = scanJob({
    title: values.title,
    description: values.description,
    categoryId: values.categoryId,
    riskFlags: values.riskFlags,
  });
  const now = new Date().toISOString();
  return {
    id: uuidv4(),
    posterId,
    title: values.title,
    categoryId: values.categoryId,
    description: values.description,
    city: values.city,
    postalCode: values.postalCode,
    locationVisibility: values.locationVisibility,
    payType: values.payType,
    budgetMin: values.budgetMin,
    budgetMax: values.budgetMax,
    estimatedHours: values.estimatedHours,
    desiredDate: values.desiredDate,
    urgency: values.urgency,
    requiresTools: values.requiresTools,
    requiresInsurance: values.requiresInsurance,
    requiresWsib: values.requiresWsib,
    requiresCertification: values.requiresCertification,
    riskFlags: values.riskFlags,
    riskLevel: riskScan.riskLevel,
    riskScan,
    photos: Array.isArray(photos) ? photos.slice(0, 12) : [],
    featuredUntil: null,
    hiredWorkerId: null,
    status: riskScan.riskLevel === 'high' ? 'review' : 'open',
    adminNotes: String(adminNotes || '').slice(0, 10_000),
    createdAt: now,
    updatedAt: now,
  };
}

function createJob(data, {
  posterId,
  input,
  photos = [],
  adminNotes = '',
  notifyAlerts = true,
} = {}) {
  const job = buildJob({ posterId, input, photos, adminNotes });
  data.jobs.push(job);
  if (notifyAlerts && job.status === 'open') notifyMatchingAlerts(data, job);
  return job;
}

function createJobTx(tx, {
  posterId,
  input,
  photos = [],
  adminNotes = '',
  notifyAlerts = true,
} = {}) {
  const job = buildJob({ posterId, input, photos, adminNotes });
  tx.jobs.insert(job);
  if (notifyAlerts && job.status === 'open') notifyMatchingAlertsTx(tx, job);
  return job;
}

module.exports = { JobInputError, buildJob, createJob, createJobTx };

// ===== src/services/jobWorkflow.js =====
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');
const db = require('../db');
const { assertTransition, canTransition } = require('./stateMachine');
const { createNotificationTx } = require('./marketplace');

class WorkflowError extends Error {
  constructor(message, code = 'WORKFLOW_ERROR') {
    super(message);
    this.name = 'WorkflowError';
    this.code = code;
  }
}

function acceptQuote({ jobId, quoteId, actor }) {
  if (!actor) throw new WorkflowError('Authentication is required.', 'AUTH_REQUIRED');
  return db.transaction((tx) => {
    const job = tx.jobs.findById(jobId);
    const quote = tx.quotes.findById(quoteId);
    if (!job || !quote || quote.jobId !== jobId) throw new WorkflowError('Quote not found.', 'NOT_FOUND');
    if (job.posterId !== actor.id && !actor.isAdmin) {
      throw new WorkflowError('Only the poster can accept a quote.', 'FORBIDDEN');
    }
    if (!quote.workerId) {
      throw new WorkflowError('Guest quotes must be linked to a verified worker account before acceptance.', 'GUEST_QUOTE');
    }
    if (quote.status === 'accepted' && job.status === 'hired' && job.hiredWorkerId === quote.workerId) {
      return { job, quote, changed: false };
    }

    assertTransition('quote', quote.status, 'accepted');
    assertTransition('job', job.status, 'hired');

    const now = new Date().toISOString();
    tx.quotes.update(quote.id, { status: 'accepted', updatedAt: now });
    tx.jobs.update(job.id, { status: 'hired', hiredWorkerId: quote.workerId, updatedAt: now });

    const otherQuotes = tx.quotes.findMany({ where: { jobId: job.id, id: { $ne: quote.id } } });
    for (const candidate of otherQuotes) {
      if (canTransition('quote', candidate.status, 'declined')) {
        tx.quotes.update(candidate.id, { status: 'declined', updatedAt: now });
      }
    }

    const existingAppointment = tx.appointments.findOne({ where: { jobId: job.id, quoteId: quote.id } });
    if (!existingAppointment) {
      tx.appointments.insert({
        id: uuidv4(),
        jobId: job.id,
        quoteId: quote.id,
        posterId: job.posterId,
        workerId: quote.workerId,
        proposedById: actor.id,
        startsAt: job.desiredDate || null,
        locationNote: '',
        scopeNote: job.title,
        status: 'proposed',
        posterConfirmedAt: actor.id === job.posterId ? now : null,
        workerConfirmedAt: null,
        createdAt: now,
        updatedAt: now,
      });
    }

    createNotificationTx(
      tx,
      quote.workerId,
      'quote-accepted',
      `Quote accepted: ${job.title}`,
      'Confirm appointment, safety checklist, and payment expectations before starting.',
      `/jobs/${job.id}`,
      { quoteId: quote.id },
    );
    return { job: tx.jobs.findById(job.id), quote: tx.quotes.findById(quote.id), changed: true };
  });
}

function completeJob({ jobId, actor }) {
  if (!actor) throw new WorkflowError('Authentication is required.', 'AUTH_REQUIRED');
  return db.transaction((tx) => {
    const job = tx.jobs.findById(jobId);
    if (!job) throw new WorkflowError('Job not found.', 'NOT_FOUND');
    if (job.posterId !== actor.id && !actor.isAdmin) {
      throw new WorkflowError('Only the poster can mark this job complete.', 'FORBIDDEN');
    }
    if (job.status === 'completed') return { job, changed: false };
    assertTransition('job', job.status, 'completed');

    const now = new Date().toISOString();
    tx.jobs.update(job.id, { status: 'completed', completedAt: now, updatedAt: now });

    const profile = tx.workerProfiles.findOne({ where: { userId: job.hiredWorkerId } });
    if (profile) {
      const completedCount = tx.jobs.findMany({ where: { hiredWorkerId: job.hiredWorkerId, status: 'completed' } }).length;
      tx.workerProfiles.update(profile.id, { completedJobs: completedCount, updatedAt: now });
    }
    return { job: tx.jobs.findById(job.id), changed: true };
  });
}

function confirmCompletion({ jobId, actor, notes = '' }) {
  if (!actor) throw new WorkflowError('Authentication is required.', 'AUTH_REQUIRED');
  return db.transaction((tx) => {
    const job = tx.jobs.findById(jobId);
    if (!job || ![job.posterId, job.hiredWorkerId].includes(actor.id)) {
      throw new WorkflowError('Only the poster or hired worker can confirm completion.', 'FORBIDDEN');
    }
    if (!['hired', 'completed'].includes(job.status)) {
      throw new WorkflowError('Completion can only be confirmed for a hired job.', 'INVALID_STATE_TRANSITION');
    }

    const role = actor.id === job.posterId ? 'poster' : 'worker';
    const now = new Date().toISOString();
    let confirmation = tx.completionConfirmations.findOne({ where: { jobId: job.id, userId: actor.id } });
    if (!confirmation) {
      confirmation = {
        id: uuidv4(),
        jobId: job.id,
        userId: actor.id,
        role,
        notes: String(notes || '').trim().slice(0, 2000),
        createdAt: now,
      };
      tx.completionConfirmations.insert(confirmation);
    }

    const confirmations = tx.completionConfirmations.findMany({ where: { jobId: job.id } });
    const bothConfirmed = confirmations.some((candidate) => candidate.role === 'poster')
      && confirmations.some((candidate) => candidate.role === 'worker');
    if (bothConfirmed && job.status !== 'completed') {
      assertTransition('job', job.status, 'completed');
      tx.jobs.update(job.id, { status: 'completed', completedAt: now, updatedAt: now });
    } else {
      tx.jobs.update(job.id, { updatedAt: now });
    }

    const recipientId = role === 'poster' ? job.hiredWorkerId : job.posterId;
    if (recipientId) {
      createNotificationTx(
        tx,
        recipientId,
        'completion-confirmed',
        `Completion update: ${job.title}`,
        `${actor.name || 'The other party'} confirmed completion.`,
        `/jobs/${job.id}`,
        {},
      );
    }
    return { job: tx.jobs.findById(job.id), confirmation, bothConfirmed };
  });
}

module.exports = {
  WorkflowError,
  acceptQuote,
  completeJob,
  confirmCompletion,
};

// ===== src/services/marketplace.js =====
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');
const { workerMatchScore, quoteValue } = require('./matchScorer');

function normalize(value) { return String(value || '').toLowerCase(); }

function alertMatchesJob(alert = {}, job = {}) {
  if (!alert.enabled || job.status !== 'open') return false;
  if (alert.categoryId && alert.categoryId !== job.categoryId) return false;
  if (alert.city && !normalize(job.city).includes(normalize(alert.city))) return false;
  if (alert.keyword && !normalize(`${job.title} ${job.description}`).includes(normalize(alert.keyword))) return false;
  const minBudget = Number(alert.minBudget || 0);
  const jobBudget = Number(job.budgetMax || job.budgetMin || 0);
  if (minBudget && jobBudget && jobBudget < minBudget) return false;
  return true;
}

function notificationRecord(userId, type, title, body, url, meta = {}) {
  return { id: uuidv4(), userId, type, title, body, url, meta, channel: 'in-app', readAt: null, createdAt: new Date().toISOString() };
}

function createNotification(data, userId, type, title, body, url, meta = {}) {
  const item = notificationRecord(userId, type, title, body, url, meta);
  data.notifications.push(item);
  return item;
}

function createNotificationTx(tx, userId, type, title, body, url, meta = {}) {
  const item = notificationRecord(userId, type, title, body, url, meta);
  tx.notifications.insert(item);
  return item;
}

function notifyMatchingAlerts(data, job) {
  data.jobAlerts.filter((alert) => alertMatchesJob(alert, job)).forEach((alert) => {
    alert.lastMatchedAt = new Date().toISOString();
    alert.updatedAt = new Date().toISOString();
    createNotification(data, alert.userId, 'job-alert-match', `New matching job: ${job.title}`, `${job.city || 'Local'} · ${job.payType || 'quote'}`, `/jobs/${job.id}`, { alertId: alert.id, jobId: job.id });
  });
}

function notifyMatchingAlertsTx(tx, job) {
  const alerts = tx.jobAlerts.findMany({ where: { enabled: true } });
  alerts.filter((alert) => alertMatchesJob(alert, job)).forEach((alert) => {
    tx.jobAlerts.update(alert.id, { lastMatchedAt: new Date().toISOString(), updatedAt: new Date().toISOString() });
    createNotificationTx(tx, alert.userId, 'job-alert-match', `New matching job: ${job.title}`, `${job.city || 'Local'} · ${job.payType || 'quote'}`, `/jobs/${job.id}`, { alertId: alert.id, jobId: job.id });
  });
}

function responseStatsForWorker(data, workerId) {
  const quotes = data.quotes.filter((q) => q.workerId === workerId);
  const accepted = quotes.filter((q) => q.status === 'accepted').length;
  return { submitted: quotes.length, accepted, acceptanceRate: quotes.length ? Math.round((accepted / quotes.length) * 100) : null, messageCount: data.messages.filter((m) => m.senderId === workerId).length };
}

function recommendedWorkersForJob(data, job, limit = 6) {
  return data.workerProfiles.filter((p) => p.status === 'active').map((profile) => {
    const user = data.users.find((u) => u.id === profile.userId) || {};
    const match = workerMatchScore(profile, user, job);
    const stats = responseStatsForWorker(data, profile.userId);
    const score = Math.min(100, match.score + (stats.acceptanceRate ? Math.min(8, stats.acceptanceRate / 15) : 0));
    return { profile, user, match, responseStats: stats, recommendationScore: Math.round(score) };
  }).sort((a, b) => b.recommendationScore - a.recommendationScore).slice(0, limit);
}

function recommendedJobsForWorker(data, profile, user, limit = 8) {
  return data.jobs.filter((job) => job.status === 'open' && job.posterId !== user.id).map((job) => ({
    job,
    match: workerMatchScore(profile, user, job),
    quoteCount: data.quotes.filter((q) => q.jobId === job.id).length,
  })).sort((a, b) => b.match.score - a.match.score).slice(0, limit);
}

function quoteQualityScore(data, quote, job) {
  const worker = data.users.find((u) => u.id === quote.workerId) || {};
  const profile = data.workerProfiles.find((p) => p.userId === quote.workerId) || {};
  const match = workerMatchScore(profile, worker, job);
  const total = quoteValue(quote);
  let score = Math.round(match.score * 0.55);
  const reasons = [...match.reasons];
  if ((quote.message || '').length >= 60) { score += 10; reasons.push('detailed quote'); }
  if (quote.availability) { score += 6; reasons.push('availability provided'); }
  if (quote.toolsIncluded) { score += 6; reasons.push('tools included'); }
  if (job.budgetMax && total <= Number(job.budgetMax)) { score += 8; reasons.push('within budget'); }
  return { score: Math.min(100, Math.round(score)), reasons: reasons.slice(0, 5) };
}

function paymentFeeEstimate(amount, feeModel = 'none') {
  const subtotal = Number(amount || 0);
  let posterServiceFee = 0;
  let workerPlatformFee = 0;
  if (feeModel === 'poster-5') posterServiceFee = Math.round(subtotal * 0.05 * 100) / 100;
  if (feeModel === 'worker-10') workerPlatformFee = Math.round(subtotal * 0.10 * 100) / 100;
  if (feeModel === 'split-3-7') { posterServiceFee = Math.round(subtotal * 0.03 * 100) / 100; workerPlatformFee = Math.round(subtotal * 0.07 * 100) / 100; }
  return { subtotal, posterServiceFee, workerPlatformFee, platformFee: posterServiceFee + workerPlatformFee, posterTotal: subtotal + posterServiceFee, workerNetAmount: subtotal - workerPlatformFee };
}

module.exports = { alertMatchesJob, notificationRecord, createNotification, createNotificationTx, notifyMatchingAlerts, notifyMatchingAlertsTx, responseStatsForWorker, recommendedWorkersForJob, recommendedJobsForWorker, quoteQualityScore, paymentFeeEstimate };

// ===== src/services/matchScorer.js =====
function normalize(value) {
  return String(value || '').toLowerCase();
}

function tokenize(value) {
  return normalize(value)
    .replace(/[^a-z0-9\s-]/g, ' ')
    .split(/\s+/)
    .filter((token) => token.length >= 3);
}

function isActiveUntil(value) {
  if (!value) return false;
  const date = new Date(value);
  return !Number.isNaN(date.getTime()) && date > new Date();
}

function verificationBadges(profile = {}, user = {}) {
  const badges = [];
  if (user.phoneVerified) badges.push({ label: 'phone verified', tone: 'info' });
  if (profile.insuranceStatus === 'verified') badges.push({ label: 'insurance verified', tone: 'success' });
  if (profile.wsibStatus === 'verified') badges.push({ label: 'WSIB verified', tone: 'success' });
  if (profile.tradeCertificationStatus === 'verified') badges.push({ label: 'trade verified', tone: 'success' });
  if (profile.hasVehicle) badges.push({ label: 'vehicle', tone: 'secondary' });
  if (isActiveUntil(profile.boostedUntil)) badges.push({ label: 'boosted', tone: 'warning' });
  return badges;
}

function workerMatchScore(profile = {}, user = {}, job = {}) {
  let score = 0;
  const reasons = [];
  const skillTokens = new Set((profile.skills || []).flatMap(tokenize));
  const jobTokens = new Set(tokenize(`${job.title || ''} ${job.description || ''} ${job.categoryId || ''}`));
  let skillMatches = 0;

  skillTokens.forEach((token) => {
    if (jobTokens.has(token)) skillMatches += 1;
  });

  if (skillMatches) {
    score += Math.min(35, skillMatches * 10);
    reasons.push(`${skillMatches} skill match${skillMatches === 1 ? '' : 'es'}`);
  }

  if (profile.tools && (job.requiresTools || normalize(job.description).includes('tool'))) {
    score += 12;
    reasons.push('tools listed');
  }

  if (profile.hasVehicle && normalize(job.description).match(/move|haul|junk|delivery|pickup|transport/)) {
    score += 10;
    reasons.push('vehicle helpful');
  }

  if (job.requiresInsurance && profile.insuranceStatus === 'verified') {
    score += 15;
    reasons.push('insurance verified');
  }

  if (job.requiresWsib && profile.wsibStatus === 'verified') {
    score += 15;
    reasons.push('WSIB verified');
  }

  if (job.requiresCertification && profile.tradeCertificationStatus === 'verified') {
    score += 20;
    reasons.push('trade credential verified');
  }

  if (user.phoneVerified) {
    score += 5;
    reasons.push('phone verified');
  }

  if (profile.averageRating) {
    score += Math.min(10, Number(profile.averageRating) * 2);
    reasons.push(`${Number(profile.averageRating).toFixed(1)} rating`);
  }

  if (isActiveUntil(profile.boostedUntil)) {
    score += 7;
    reasons.push('boosted profile');
  }

  return {
    score: Math.min(100, Math.round(score)),
    reasons: reasons.slice(0, 4),
  };
}

function quoteValue(quote = {}) {
  if (quote.quoteType === 'fixed') return Number(quote.amount || 0);
  return Number(quote.amount || 0) * Number(quote.estimatedHours || 1);
}

module.exports = {
  isActiveUntil,
  verificationBadges,
  workerMatchScore,
  quoteValue,
};

// ===== src/services/messageSafety.js =====
const rules = [
  { key: 'tax-risk', regex: /under\s+the\s+table|no\s+tax|cash\s+only|avoid\s+h.?s.?t/i, notice: 'possible tax/cash-risk wording' },
  { key: 'unsafe', regex: /no\s+license\s+needed|ignore\s+safety|without\s+permit/i, notice: 'possible unsafe or unlicensed work request' },
  { key: 'harassment', regex: /\b(threat|kill|hurt\s+you|idiot|stupid)\b/i, notice: 'possible harassment or threat' },
  { key: 'discrimination', regex: /young\s+guy|men\s+only|women\s+only|canadian\s+only|no\s+disabled/i, notice: 'possible discriminatory wording' },
];
function scanMessage(body = '') { const matches = rules.filter((r) => r.regex.test(body)); return { flagged: matches.length > 0, flags: matches.map((m) => m.key), notices: matches.map((m) => m.notice) }; }
function usersAreBlocked(data, a, b) { return data.userBlocks.some((x) => x.status === 'active' && ((x.blockerId === a && x.blockedId === b) || (x.blockerId === b && x.blockedId === a))); }
module.exports = { scanMessage, usersAreBlocked };

// ===== src/services/onboarding.js =====
function checklistItem(key, label, complete, href, description) {
  return { key, label, complete: Boolean(complete), href, description };
}

function workerChecklist(user, profile, documents = [], payoutAccount = null) {
  const verifiedTypes = new Set(documents.filter((item) => item.status === 'verified').map((item) => item.type));
  const items = [
    checklistItem('profile', 'Complete your worker profile', profile && profile.displayName && profile.bio, '/workers/profile', 'Add a useful bio and public display name.'),
    checklistItem('skills', 'Add skills and tools', profile && Array.isArray(profile.skills) && profile.skills.length > 0, '/workers/profile', 'Help posters understand what work you can take.'),
    checklistItem('availability', 'Set availability and service area', profile && profile.availability && profile.serviceRadiusKm !== null, '/workers/profile', 'Make job matching more accurate.'),
    checklistItem('portfolio', 'Add portfolio photos', profile && Array.isArray(profile.portfolioPhotos) && profile.portfolioPhotos.length > 0, '/workers/profile', 'Show examples of completed work.'),
    checklistItem('identity', 'Submit identity verification', verifiedTypes.has('id'), '/workers/profile#documents', 'Private documents are visible only to authorized reviewers.'),
    checklistItem('insurance', 'Add insurance or WSIB details', verifiedTypes.has('insurance') || verifiedTypes.has('wsib'), '/workers/profile#documents', 'Required for some higher-risk tasks.'),
    checklistItem('payout', 'Prepare payout information', Boolean(payoutAccount), '/dashboard', 'Payment collection remains disabled until a regulated processor is connected.'),
  ];
  return summarize(items);
}

function posterChecklist(user, profile, jobs = []) {
  const items = [
    checklistItem('profile', 'Complete your employer profile', profile && profile.displayName, '/posters/profile', 'A complete profile helps workers evaluate your task.'),
    checklistItem('contact', 'Confirm your account contact details', user && (user.email || user.phone), '/posters/profile', 'Keep a reliable way to receive quote and scheduling updates.'),
    checklistItem('first-job', 'Post your first task', jobs.length > 0, '/jobs/new', 'Describe the scope, budget, timing, and safety requirements.'),
    checklistItem('review-quotes', 'Review incoming quotes', jobs.some((job) => Number(job.quoteCount || 0) > 0), '/dashboard', 'Compare scope, availability, verification, and total price.'),
  ];
  return summarize(items);
}

function summarize(items) {
  const completed = items.filter((item) => item.complete).length;
  return {
    items,
    completed,
    total: items.length,
    percent: items.length ? Math.round((completed / items.length) * 100) : 100,
    next: items.find((item) => !item.complete) || null,
  };
}

module.exports = { workerChecklist, posterChecklist };

// ===== src/services/postAssistant.js =====
function clean(value) { return String(value || '').trim(); }
function improveJobPost(input = {}) {
  const title = clean(input.title) || clean(input.rawText).split(/[.!?]/)[0].slice(0, 80) || 'Odd job task';
  const details = [clean(input.description), clean(input.rawText), input.riskFlags ? `Risk notes: ${[].concat(input.riskFlags).join(', ')}` : ''].filter(Boolean).join('\n');
  return {
    title: title.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + title.slice(1),
    description: details || 'Describe the work, tools, timing, access, hazards, and payment expectations.',
    suggestedChecklist: ['Add photos', 'Confirm tools/materials', 'Disclose hazards', 'Ask for insurance/WSIB when risk is higher', 'Use licensed trades for regulated work'],
  };
}
module.exports = { improveJobPost };

// ===== src/services/privateFiles.js =====
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');
const { canAccessPayment, canAccessDispute } = require('./accessPolicy');

const privateRoot = path.join(__dirname, '..', '..', 'data', 'private-uploads');

function ensurePrivateRoot() {
  fs.mkdirSync(privateRoot, { recursive: true, mode: 0o700 });
}

function privateFileRecord(file, { ownerId, contextType, contextId }) {
  return {
    id: uuidv4(),
    ownerId,
    contextType,
    contextId,
    storageName: file.filename,
    originalName: file.originalname,
    mimeType: file.mimetype,
    size: file.size,
    createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
  };
}

function registerPrivateFile(data, file, { ownerId, contextType, contextId }) {
  if (!file) return null;
  if (file.path) {
    try { fs.chmodSync(file.path, 0o600); } catch (_error) { /* best effort */ }
  }
  const record = privateFileRecord(file, { ownerId, contextType, contextId });
  if (Array.isArray(data.privateFiles)) {
    data.privateFiles.push(record);
  } else if (typeof data.privateFiles?.insert === 'function') {
    data.privateFiles.insert(record);
  } else {
    if (!Array.isArray(data.privateFiles)) data.privateFiles = [];
    data.privateFiles.push(record);
  }
  return record;
}

function canAccessPrivateFile(data, user, file) {
  if (!user || !file) return false;
  if (user.isAdmin || file.ownerId === user.id) return true;

  if (file.contextType === 'message') {
    const message = data.messages.find((item) => item.id === file.contextId);
    return Boolean(message && [message.senderId, message.recipientId].includes(user.id));
  }
  if (file.contextType === 'workerDocument') {
    const document = data.documents.find((item) => item.id === file.contextId);
    return Boolean(document && document.workerId === user.id);
  }
  if (file.contextType === 'paymentEvidence') {
    const evidence = data.paymentEvidence.find((item) => item.id === file.contextId);
    const payment = evidence && data.paymentRequests.find((item) => item.id === evidence.paymentRequestId);
    return canAccessPayment(user, payment);
  }
  if (file.contextType === 'disputeEvidence') {
    const evidence = data.disputeEvidence.find((item) => item.id === file.contextId);
    const dispute = evidence && data.disputes.find((item) => item.id === evidence.disputeId);
    return canAccessDispute(user, dispute);
  }
  return false;
}

function canAccessPrivateFileTx(tx, user, file) {
  if (!user || !file) return false;
  if (user.isAdmin || file.ownerId === user.id) return true;

  if (file.contextType === 'message') {
    const message = tx.messages.findById(file.contextId);
    return Boolean(message && [message.senderId, message.recipientId].includes(user.id));
  }
  if (file.contextType === 'workerDocument') {
    const document = tx.documents.findById(file.contextId);
    return Boolean(document && document.workerId === user.id);
  }
  if (file.contextType === 'paymentEvidence') {
    const evidence = tx.paymentEvidence.findById(file.contextId);
    const payment = evidence && tx.paymentRequests.findById(evidence.paymentRequestId);
    return canAccessPayment(user, payment);
  }
  if (file.contextType === 'disputeEvidence') {
    const evidence = tx.disputeEvidence.findById(file.contextId);
    const dispute = evidence && tx.disputes.findById(evidence.disputeId);
    return canAccessDispute(user, dispute);
  }
  return false;
}

function absolutePrivatePath(file) {
  ensurePrivateRoot();
  const candidate = path.resolve(privateRoot, file.storageName);
  if (!candidate.startsWith(path.resolve(privateRoot) + path.sep)) return null;
  return candidate;
}

module.exports = {
  privateRoot,
  ensurePrivateRoot,
  privateFileRecord,
  registerPrivateFile,
  canAccessPrivateFile,
  canAccessPrivateFileTx,
  absolutePrivatePath,
};

// ===== src/services/riskScanner.js =====
const restrictedTerms = [
  'electrical', 'panel', 'breaker', 'wiring', 'outlet', 'gas', 'gas line', 'hvac', 'refrigerant',
  'air conditioner', 'air conditioning', 'plumbing', 'pipe', 'roof', 'roofing', 'structural',
  'load bearing', 'asbestos', 'mould', 'mold', 'demolition', 'permit', 'pest poison', 'extermination',
];

const safetyTerms = [
  'ladder', 'height', 'heights', 'roof', 'heavy lifting', 'concrete drilling', 'hammer drill',
  'drill into concrete', '140 lbs', '150 lbs', 'stairs', 'staircase', 'glass', 'sharp', 'confined space',
];

const employmentTerms = [
  'every week', 'weekly shift', 'ongoing shift', 'report to manager', 'use our tools', 'set hours',
  'staff coverage', 'employee', 'payroll', 'part time', 'full time', 'schedule every', 'recurring',
];

const discriminationTerms = [
  'male only', 'men only', 'young guy', 'young man', 'canadian only', 'no disability', 'no disabled',
  'girls only', 'boys only', 'student only',
];

const taxRiskTerms = [
  'under the table', 'cash only no receipt', 'no tax', 'avoid tax', 'off the books',
];

function findMatches(text, terms) {
  const lowerText = text.toLowerCase();
  return terms.filter((term) => lowerText.includes(term));
}

function scanJob({ title = '', description = '', categoryId = '', riskFlags = [] }) {
  const text = `${title} ${description} ${Array.isArray(riskFlags) ? riskFlags.join(' ') : riskFlags}`;
  const restrictedMatches = findMatches(text, restrictedTerms);
  const safetyMatches = findMatches(text, safetyTerms);
  const employmentMatches = findMatches(text, employmentTerms);
  const discriminationMatches = findMatches(text, discriminationTerms);
  const taxMatches = findMatches(text, taxRiskTerms);

  let riskLevel = 'low';
  if (safetyMatches.length || employmentMatches.length) riskLevel = 'medium';
  if (restrictedMatches.length || categoryId === 'restricted-trade' || discriminationMatches.length || taxMatches.length) riskLevel = 'high';

  const notices = [];

  if (restrictedMatches.length || categoryId === 'restricted-trade') {
    notices.push('This task may involve regulated or licensed work. Ask for proof of certification, insurance, and WSIB where applicable.');
  }

  if (safetyMatches.length) {
    notices.push('This task has safety-sensitive details. Confirm tools, lifting plan, ladder/work-at-heights safety, and liability coverage before hiring.');
  }

  if (employmentMatches.length) {
    notices.push('This post may look like recurring supervised employment rather than an independent contractor task. Consider payroll/employment compliance.');
  }

  if (discriminationMatches.length) {
    notices.push('This post may contain discriminatory language. Use job-relevant requirements instead, such as lifting ability or legal authorization to work.');
  }

  if (taxMatches.length) {
    notices.push('Avoid cash/no-tax language. Workers and businesses are responsible for tax compliance.');
  }

  return {
    riskLevel,
    flags: {
      restricted: restrictedMatches,
      safety: safetyMatches,
      employment: employmentMatches,
      discrimination: discriminationMatches,
      tax: taxMatches,
    },
    notices,
  };
}

module.exports = { scanJob };

// ===== src/services/seo.js =====
function titleCase(value) {
  return String(value || '')
    .split('-')
    .filter(Boolean)
    .map((part) => part.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + part.slice(1))
    .join(' ');
}

function getSeoCategory(data, slugOrId) {
  return (data.categoryGuides || []).find((guide) => guide.slug === slugOrId || guide.categoryId === slugOrId)
    || (data.categories || []).map((category) => ({ categoryId: category.id, slug: category.id, headline: category.name, keywords: [] })).find((guide) => guide.slug === slugOrId || guide.categoryId === slugOrId)
    || null;
}

function getSeoLocation(data, slug) {
  return (data.seoLocations || []).find((location) => location.id === slug) || null;
}

function buildSeoPage(data, locationSlug, categorySlug) {
  const location = getSeoLocation(data, locationSlug);
  const guide = getSeoCategory(data, categorySlug);
  if (!location || !guide) return null;

  const jobs = data.jobs
    .filter((job) => job.status === 'open')
    .filter((job) => (job.city || '').toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, '-') === location.id || (job.city || '').toLowerCase().includes(location.name.toLowerCase()))
    .filter((job) => job.categoryId === guide.categoryId)
    .slice(0, 12);

  const workers = data.workerProfiles
    .filter((profile) => profile.status === 'active')
    .map((profile) => ({ ...profile, user: data.users.find((user) => user.id === profile.userId) }))
    .filter((profile) => profile.user && (profile.user.city || '').toLowerCase().includes(location.name.toLowerCase()))
    .filter((profile) => {
      const text = `${profile.skills || []} ${profile.bio || ''} ${profile.tools || ''}`.toLowerCase();
      return [guide.categoryId, guide.slug, ...(guide.keywords || [])].some((keyword) => text.includes(String(keyword).toLowerCase()));
    })
    .slice(0, 12);

  const title = `${guide.headline} in ${location.name}`;
  const description = `Post ${guide.headline.toLowerCase()} jobs in ${location.name}, compare local quotes, review worker profiles, and hire directly.`;
  const structuredData = {
    '@context': 'https://schema.org',
    '@type': 'WebPage',
    name: title,
    description,
    about: guide.headline,
    areaServed: `${location.name}, ${location.province}`,
    potentialAction: {
      '@type': 'SearchAction',
      target: `/jobs?city=${encodeURIComponent(location.name)}&category=${encodeURIComponent(guide.categoryId)}`,
      query: 'odd jobs marketplace',
    },
  };

  return { location, guide, jobs, workers, title, description, structuredData };
}

function publicSeoLinks(data) {
  const locations = data.seoLocations || [];
  const guides = data.categoryGuides || [];
  return locations.flatMap((location) => guides.map((guide) => ({
    location,
    guide,
    url: `/${location.id}/${guide.slug}`,
    label: `${guide.headline} in ${location.name}`,
  })));
}

module.exports = { titleCase, getSeoCategory, getSeoLocation, buildSeoPage, publicSeoLinks };

// ===== src/services/sessionSecurity.js =====
const db = require('../db');

function invalidateUserSessions(userId, exceptSid = null) {
  const sqlite = db.getDb();
  const rows = sqlite.prepare('SELECT sid, data FROM sessions').all();
  const remove = sqlite.prepare('DELETE FROM sessions WHERE sid = ?');
  const transaction = sqlite.transaction(() => {
    for (const row of rows) {
      if (exceptSid && row.sid === exceptSid) continue;
      try {
        const session = JSON.parse(row.data);
        if (session.userId === userId) remove.run(row.sid);
      } catch (_error) {
        remove.run(row.sid);
      }
    }
  });
  transaction();
}

module.exports = { invalidateUserSessions };

// ===== src/services/stateMachine.js =====
const transitions = {
  job: {
    review: new Set(['open', 'removed', 'closed']),
    open: new Set(['hired', 'closed', 'removed']),
    hired: new Set(['completed', 'closed']),
    completed: new Set(['closed']),
    closed: new Set([]),
    removed: new Set([]),
  },
  quote: {
    submitted: new Set(['shortlisted', 'accepted', 'declined']),
    shortlisted: new Set(['submitted', 'accepted', 'declined']),
    accepted: new Set([]),
    declined: new Set([]),
  },
  dispute: {
    open: new Set(['reviewing', 'closed']),
    reviewing: new Set(['waiting-on-poster', 'waiting-on-worker', 'resolved', 'closed']),
    'waiting-on-poster': new Set(['reviewing', 'resolved', 'closed']),
    'waiting-on-worker': new Set(['reviewing', 'resolved', 'closed']),
    resolved: new Set(['closed']),
    closed: new Set([]),
  },
  payment: {
    requested: new Set(['invoice-sent', 'authorized-demo', 'external-paid', 'cancelled']),
    'invoice-sent': new Set(['external-paid', 'cancelled']),
    'authorized-demo': new Set(['released', 'cancelled', 'refunded-demo']),
    'external-paid': new Set(['released', 'refunded-demo']),
    released: new Set(['refunded-demo']),
    cancelled: new Set([]),
    'refunded-demo': new Set([]),
  },
  report: {
    open: new Set(['reviewing', 'closed']),
    reviewing: new Set(['open', 'closed']),
    closed: new Set([]),
  },
  document: {
    pending: new Set(['verified', 'rejected', 'expired']),
    verified: new Set(['expired']),
    rejected: new Set(['pending']),
    expired: new Set(['pending']),
  },
  promotion: {
    pending: new Set(['active', 'rejected']),
    active: new Set(['expired']),
    rejected: new Set(['pending']),
    expired: new Set(['pending']),
  },
  moderation: {
    open: new Set(['reviewing', 'needs-edits', 'escalated', 'closed']),
    reviewing: new Set(['open', 'needs-edits', 'escalated', 'closed']),
    'needs-edits': new Set(['reviewing', 'escalated', 'closed']),
    escalated: new Set(['reviewing', 'closed']),
    closed: new Set([]),
  },
  appointment: {
    proposed: new Set(['confirmed', 'cancelled']),
    confirmed: new Set(['completed', 'cancelled']),
    completed: new Set([]),
    cancelled: new Set([]),
  },
  account: {
    guest: new Set(['active', 'deleted']),
    active: new Set(['suspended', 'deleted']),
    suspended: new Set(['active', 'deleted']),
    service: new Set(['suspended', 'deleted']),
    deleted: new Set([]),
  },
};

function canTransition(type, current, next) {
  if (current === next) return true;
  return Boolean(transitions[type] && transitions[type][current] && transitions[type][current].has(next));
}

function assertTransition(type, current, next) {
  if (!canTransition(type, current, next)) {
    const error = new Error(`Invalid ${type} transition: ${current} -> ${next}`);
    error.code = 'INVALID_STATE_TRANSITION';
    throw error;
  }
}

function allowedNext(type, current) {
  return transitions[type] && transitions[type][current]
    ? [...transitions[type][current]]
    : [];
}

module.exports = { canTransition, assertTransition, allowedNext, transitions };

// ===== src/services/tokenService.js =====
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');
const { randomToken, hashToken, safeEqual } = require('../utils/security');

function tokenRecord(userId, purpose, ttlMinutes = 60, meta = {}) {
  const rawToken = randomToken();
  const now = new Date();
  return {
    rawToken,
    token: {
      id: uuidv4(),
      userId,
      purpose,
      tokenHash: hashToken(rawToken),
      meta,
      expiresAt: new Date(now.getTime() + ttlMinutes * 60 * 1000).toISOString(),
      consumedAt: null,
      createdAt: now.toISOString(),
    },
  };
}

function issueToken(data, { userId, purpose, ttlMinutes = 60, meta = {} }) {
  const { rawToken, token } = tokenRecord(userId, purpose, ttlMinutes, meta);
  data.authTokens.push(token);
  return { rawToken, token };
}

function issueTokenTx(tx, { userId, purpose, ttlMinutes = 60, meta = {} }) {
  const { rawToken, token } = tokenRecord(userId, purpose, ttlMinutes, meta);
  tx.authTokens.insert(token);
  return { rawToken, token };
}

function findValidToken(data, rawToken, purpose) {
  const digest = hashToken(rawToken);
  const now = Date.now();
  return data.authTokens.find((token) => (
    token.purpose === purpose
    && !token.consumedAt
    && new Date(token.expiresAt).getTime() > now
    && safeEqual(token.tokenHash, digest)
  )) || null;
}

function findValidTokenTx(tx, rawToken, purpose) {
  const digest = hashToken(rawToken);
  const now = Date.now();
  return tx.authTokens.findOne({ where: { purpose, consumedAt: null, expiresAt: { $gt: new Date(now).toISOString() } }, extra: { tokenHash: digest, safeEqual: true } }) || null;
}

function consumeToken(data, rawToken, purpose) {
  const token = findValidToken(data, rawToken, purpose);
  if (!token) return null;
  token.consumedAt = new Date().toISOString();
  return token;
}

function consumeTokenTx(tx, rawToken, purpose) {
  const token = findValidTokenTx(tx, rawToken, purpose);
  if (!token) return null;
  tx.authTokens.update(token.id, { consumedAt: new Date().toISOString() });
  return token;
}

function revokeUserTokens(data, userId, purpose) {
  const now = new Date().toISOString();
  for (const token of data.authTokens) {
    if (token.userId === userId && (!purpose || token.purpose === purpose) && !token.consumedAt) {
      token.consumedAt = now;
    }
  }
}

function revokeUserTokensTx(tx, userId, purpose) {
  const now = new Date().toISOString();
  const tokens = tx.authTokens.findMany({ where: { userId, purpose, consumedAt: null } });
  for (const token of tokens) {
    tx.authTokens.update(token.id, { consumedAt: now });
  }
}

function pruneTokens(data) {
  const cutoff = Date.now() - 7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
  data.authTokens = data.authTokens.filter((token) => (
    !token.consumedAt || new Date(token.consumedAt).getTime() > cutoff
  ));
}

function pruneTokensTx(tx) {
  const cutoff = new Date(Date.now() - 7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000).toISOString();
  const expired = tx.authTokens.findMany({ where: { consumedAt: { $lt: cutoff } } });
  for (const token of expired) {
    tx.authTokens.delete(token.id);
  }
}

module.exports = { tokenRecord, issueToken, issueTokenTx, findValidToken, findValidTokenTx, consumeToken, consumeTokenTx, revokeUserTokens, revokeUserTokensTx, pruneTokens, pruneTokensTx };

// ===== src/services/ux.js =====
const STATUS_LABELS = Object.freeze({
  review: 'Safety review', open: 'Open for quotes', hired: 'Worker selected', completed: 'Completed',
  closed: 'Closed', removed: 'Removed', submitted: 'Submitted', shortlisted: 'Shortlisted',
  accepted: 'Accepted', declined: 'Declined', pending: 'Pending review', verified: 'Verified',
  rejected: 'Rejected', active: 'Active', suspended: 'Suspended', resolved: 'Resolved',
  reviewing: 'Under review', requested: 'Requested', released: 'Released', cancelled: 'Cancelled',
});

function statusLabel(value) {
  const key = String(value || '').trim();
  if (!key) return 'Unknown';
  return STATUS_LABELS[key] || key.replace(/[-_]+/g, ' ').replace(/\b\w/g, (letter) => letter.toUpperCase());
}

function statusTone(value) {
  const key = String(value || '').toLowerCase();
  if (['completed', 'accepted', 'verified', 'active', 'released', 'resolved', 'external-paid'].includes(key)) return 'success';
  if (['review', 'reviewing', 'pending', 'requested', 'shortlisted', 'invoice-sent'].includes(key)) return 'warning';
  if (['removed', 'rejected', 'suspended', 'cancelled', 'declined', 'expired'].includes(key)) return 'danger';
  if (['open', 'submitted', 'hired'].includes(key)) return 'info';
  return 'neutral';
}

module.exports = { STATUS_LABELS, statusLabel, statusTone };

// ===== src/services/validation.js =====
const { compact, parseNumber } = require('../utils/format');
const { normalizeEmail } = require('../utils/security');

function validEmail(value) {
  const email = normalizeEmail(value);
  return !email || (email.length <= 254 && /^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/.test(email));
}

function finiteNonNegative(value, max = Number.POSITIVE_INFINITY) {
  const parsed = parseNumber(value);
  return parsed === null || (Number.isFinite(parsed) && parsed >= 0 && parsed <= max);
}

function normalizeStringArray(value, { maxItems = 20, maxLength = 120 } = {}) {
  const input = value === undefined || value === null || value === ''
    ? []
    : (Array.isArray(value) ? value : [value]);
  return [...new Set(input.map(compact).filter(Boolean).map((item) => item.slice(0, maxLength)))].slice(0, maxItems);
}

function validateJobInput(categories, body) {
  const errors = [];
  const title = compact(body.title);
  const description = compact(body.description);
  const categoryId = compact(body.categoryId);
  const city = compact(body.city);
  const postalCode = compact(body.postalCode).toUpperCase();
  const budgetMin = parseNumber(body.budgetMin);
  const budgetMax = parseNumber(body.budgetMax);
  const estimatedHours = parseNumber(body.estimatedHours);
  const desiredDate = compact(body.desiredDate) || null;
  const riskFlags = normalizeStringArray(body.riskFlags);
  const locationVisibility = ['neighbourhood', 'city', 'private-after-hire'].includes(body.locationVisibility)
    ? body.locationVisibility
    : 'neighbourhood';
  const payType = ['quote', 'hourly', 'fixed'].includes(body.payType) ? body.payType : 'quote';
  const urgency = ['urgent', 'this-week', 'flexible'].includes(body.urgency) ? body.urgency : 'flexible';

  if (title.length < 5 || title.length > 120) errors.push('Title must be between 5 and 120 characters.');
  if (description.length < 20 || description.length > 5000) errors.push('Description must be between 20 and 5,000 characters.');
  if (!categories.some((category) => category.id === categoryId)) errors.push('Choose a valid category.');
  if (city.length > 120) errors.push('City must be no more than 120 characters.');
  if (postalCode.length > 20) errors.push('Postal code must be no more than 20 characters.');
  if (!finiteNonNegative(body.budgetMin, 1_000_000) || !finiteNonNegative(body.budgetMax, 1_000_000)) {
    errors.push('Budgets must be between $0 and $1,000,000.');
  }
  if (budgetMin !== null && budgetMax !== null && budgetMin > budgetMax) errors.push('Minimum budget cannot exceed maximum budget.');
  if (estimatedHours !== null && (estimatedHours <= 0 || estimatedHours > 10_000)) {
    errors.push('Estimated hours must be between 0 and 10,000.');
  }
  if (desiredDate && Number.isNaN(new Date(desiredDate).getTime())) errors.push('Choose a valid desired date.');

  return {
    errors,
    values: {
      title,
      description,
      categoryId,
      city,
      postalCode,
      budgetMin,
      budgetMax,
      estimatedHours,
      desiredDate,
      riskFlags,
      locationVisibility,
      payType,
      urgency,
      requiresTools: body.requiresTools === 'on' || body.requiresTools === true,
      requiresInsurance: body.requiresInsurance === 'on' || body.requiresInsurance === true,
      requiresWsib: body.requiresWsib === 'on' || body.requiresWsib === true,
      requiresCertification: body.requiresCertification === 'on' || body.requiresCertification === true,
    },
  };
}

function validateQuoteInput(body) {
  const errors = [];
  const quoteType = ['hourly', 'fixed'].includes(body.quoteType) ? body.quoteType : 'fixed';
  const amount = parseNumber(body.amount);
  const estimatedHours = parseNumber(body.estimatedHours);
  const email = normalizeEmail(body.email);
  const phone = compact(body.phone);
  const message = compact(body.message);
  const availability = compact(body.availability);

  if (!amount || amount <= 0 || amount > 1_000_000) errors.push('Enter a positive quote amount below $1,000,000.');
  if (quoteType === 'hourly' && (!estimatedHours || estimatedHours <= 0 || estimatedHours > 10_000)) {
    errors.push('Enter valid estimated hours for an hourly quote.');
  }
  if (!validEmail(email)) errors.push('Enter a valid email address.');
  if (phone.length > 40) errors.push('Phone number must be no more than 40 characters.');
  if (message.length > 5000) errors.push('Quote message must be no more than 5,000 characters.');
  if (availability.length > 1000) errors.push('Availability must be no more than 1,000 characters.');

  return {
    errors,
    values: {
      quoteType,
      amount,
      estimatedHours,
      email,
      phone,
      message,
      availability,
      toolsIncluded: body.toolsIncluded === 'on' || body.toolsIncluded === true,
    },
  };
}

module.exports = {
  validEmail,
  finiteNonNegative,
  normalizeStringArray,
  validateJobInput,
  validateQuoteInput,
};

function accountUser(user) {

  return {
    id: user.id,
    name: user.name,
    email: user.email || '',
    phone: user.phone || '',

    postalCode: user.postalCode || '',

    phoneVerified: Boolean(user.phoneVerified),
    accountStatus: user.accountStatus,
    createdAt: user.createdAt,
    updatedAt: user.updatedAt,
  };
}

  if (!user) return null;
  return {
    id: user.id,
    name: user.name,
    city: user.city || '',
    role: user.role,
  };
}
