// ===== src/utils/format.js =====
function formatDate(value) {
  if (!value) return 'Flexible';
  const date = new Date(value);
  if (Number.isNaN(date.getTime())) return value;
  return date.toLocaleDateString('en-CA', { year: 'numeric', month: 'short', day: 'numeric' });
}

function formatDateTime(value) {
  if (!value) return '';
  const date = new Date(value);
  if (Number.isNaN(date.getTime())) return value;
  return date.toLocaleString('en-CA', { dateStyle: 'medium', timeStyle: 'short' });
}

function compact(value) {
  return String(value || '').trim();
}

function parseNumber(value) {
  if (value === undefined || value === null || value === '') return null;
  const parsed = Number(value);
  return Number.isFinite(parsed) ? parsed : null;
}

module.exports = { formatDate, formatDateTime, compact, parseNumber };

// ===== src/utils/mailer.js =====
const nodemailer = require('nodemailer');

const enabled = Boolean(process.env.SMTP_HOST);

let transporter = null;
if (enabled) {
  transporter = nodemailer.createTransport({
    host: process.env.SMTP_HOST,
    port: Number(process.env.SMTP_PORT || 587),
    secure: process.env.SMTP_SECURE === 'true',
    auth: process.env.SMTP_USER ? {
      user: process.env.SMTP_USER,
      pass: process.env.SMTP_PASS,
    } : undefined,
  });
}

function redactAddress(address) {
  const value = String(address || '');
  const at = value.indexOf('@');
  if (at <= 1) return '[redacted]';
  return `${value.slice(0, 1)}***${value.slice(at)}`;
}

async function sendEmail({ to, replyTo, subject, text, html }) {
  if (!to) return null;
  if (!enabled) {
    console.info('[SMTP] Mail disabled', { to: redactAddress(to), subject: String(subject || '').slice(0, 120) });
    return null;
  }

  const mailOptions = {
    from: process.env.SMTP_FROM || '"NeighbourTask" <no-reply@neighbourtask.local>',
    to,
    replyTo,
    subject,
    text,
    html,
  };

  try {
    const info = await transporter.sendMail(mailOptions);
    console.info('[SMTP] Email sent', { to: redactAddress(to), messageId: info.messageId });
    return info;
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('[SMTP] Delivery failed', { to: redactAddress(to), message: error.message });
    throw error;
  }
}

module.exports = { sendEmail, enabled };

// ===== src/utils/security.js =====
const crypto = require('crypto');

function normalizeEmail(value) {
  return String(value || '').trim().toLowerCase();
}

function isStrongPassword(value) {
  const password = String(value || '');
  return password.length >= 10
    && /[a-z]/.test(password)
    && /[A-Z]/.test(password)
    && /\d/.test(password);
}

function randomToken(bytes = 32) {
  return crypto.randomBytes(bytes).toString('base64url');
}

function hashToken(token) {
  return crypto.createHash('sha256').update(String(token || '')).digest('hex');
}

function safeEqual(left, right) {
  const a = Buffer.from(String(left || ''));
  const b = Buffer.from(String(right || ''));
  return a.length === b.length && crypto.timingSafeEqual(a, b);
}

function safeRedirectTarget(req, candidate, fallback = '/') {
  const value = String(candidate || '').trim();
  if (!value) return fallback;

  try {
    const base = `${req.protocol}://${req.get('host')}`;
    const parsed = new URL(value, base);
    if (parsed.origin !== new URL(base).origin) return fallback;
    if (!parsed.pathname.startsWith('/')) return fallback;
    return `${parsed.pathname}${parsed.search}${parsed.hash}`;
  } catch (_error) {
    return fallback;
  }
}

function regenerateSession(req, userId) {
  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    const oldToken = req.session.csrfToken;
    req.session.regenerate((error) => {
      if (error) return reject(error);
      req.session.userId = userId;
      if (oldToken) req.session.csrfToken = oldToken;
      req.session.save((saveError) => (saveError ? reject(saveError) : resolve()));
    });
  });
}

function publicBaseUrl(req) {
  const configured = String(process.env.BASE_URL || '').trim().replace(/\/$/, '');
  if (configured) {
    const parsed = new URL(configured);
    return `${parsed.protocol}//${parsed.host}`;
  }
  if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production') {
    throw new Error('BASE_URL must be configured in production.');
  }
  return `${req.protocol}://${req.get('host')}`;
}

module.exports = {
  normalizeEmail,
  isStrongPassword,
  randomToken,
  hashToken,
  safeEqual,
  safeRedirectTarget,
  regenerateSession,
  publicBaseUrl,
};

// ===== src/utils/uploads.js =====
const fs = require('fs');

const extensionByMime = Object.freeze({
  'image/jpeg': '.jpg',
  'image/png': '.png',
  'image/webp': '.webp',
  'image/gif': '.gif',
  'application/pdf': '.pdf',
});

function filesFromRequest(req) {
  return [req.file, ...(Array.isArray(req.files) ? req.files : [])].filter(Boolean);
}

function discardUploadedFiles(req) {
  for (const file of filesFromRequest(req)) {
    if (file.path) fs.unlink(file.path, () => {});
  }
}

function extensionForMime(mimeType) {
  return extensionByMime[mimeType] || '';
}

function hasPrefix(buffer, bytes) {
  if (buffer.length < bytes.length) return false;
  return bytes.every((value, index) => buffer[index] === value);
}

function matchesDeclaredType(file) {
  if (!file || !file.path || !extensionByMime[file.mimetype]) return false;
  let descriptor;
  try {
    descriptor = fs.openSync(file.path, 'r');
    const header = Buffer.alloc(16);
    const bytesRead = fs.readSync(descriptor, header, 0, header.length, 0);
    const value = header.subarray(0, bytesRead);
    if (file.mimetype === 'image/jpeg') return hasPrefix(value, [0xff, 0xd8, 0xff]);
    if (file.mimetype === 'image/png') return hasPrefix(value, [0x89, 0x50, 0x4e, 0x47, 0x0d, 0x0a, 0x1a, 0x0a]);
    if (file.mimetype === 'image/gif') return value.subarray(0, 6).toString('ascii') === 'GIF87a' || value.subarray(0, 6).toString('ascii') === 'GIF89a';
    if (file.mimetype === 'image/webp') return value.subarray(0, 4).toString('ascii') === 'RIFF' && value.subarray(8, 12).toString('ascii') === 'WEBP';
    if (file.mimetype === 'application/pdf') return value.subarray(0, 5).toString('ascii') === '%PDF-';
    return false;
  } catch (_error) {
    return false;
  } finally {
    if (descriptor !== undefined) fs.closeSync(descriptor);
  }
}

function requestFilesMatchDeclaredTypes(req) {
  return filesFromRequest(req).every(matchesDeclaredType);
}

module.exports = {
  filesFromRequest,
  discardUploadedFiles,
  extensionForMime,
  matchesDeclaredType,
  requestFilesMatchDeclaredTypes,
};

// ===== src/views/layoutEngine.js =====
const path = require('path');

function safeAssetUrl(value) {
  const url = String(value || '').trim();
  return url.startsWith('/') && !url.startsWith('//')
    || url.startsWith('https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/')
    || url.startsWith('https://fonts.googleapis.com/')
    || url.startsWith('https://fonts.gstatic.com/')
    ? url
    : null;
}

function attribute(tag, name) {
  const match = tag.match(new RegExp(`${name}\\s*=\\s*["']([^"']+)["']`, 'i'));
  return match ? match[1] : null;
}

function extractDocument(html) {
  const source = String(html || '');
  const titleMatch = source.match(/<title[^>]*>([\s\S]*?)<\/title>/i);
  const headMatch = source.match(/<head[^>]*>([\s\S]*?)<\/head>/i);
  const bodyMatch = source.match(/<body[^>]*>([\s\S]*?)<\/body>/i);
  const mainMatch = source.match(/<main[^>]*>([\s\S]*?)<\/main>/i);
  const whole = bodyMatch ? bodyMatch[1] : source;
  const scripts = [];
  source.replace(/<script\b[^>]*\bsrc\s*=\s*["'][^"']+["'][^>]*><\/script>/gi, (tag) => {
    const src = safeAssetUrl(attribute(tag, 'src'));
    if (src && !scripts.includes(src)) scripts.push(src);
    return tag;
  });
  const body = (mainMatch ? mainMatch[1] : whole)
    .replace(/<script\b[\s\S]*?<\/script>/gi, '')
    .replace(/<style\b[\s\S]*?<\/style>/gi, '')
    .trim();

  const headTags = [];
  for (const tag of (headMatch ? headMatch[1] : '').match(/<(?:meta|link)\b[^>]*>/gi) || []) {
    if (/http-equiv\s*=\s*["'](?:content-security-policy|refresh)/i.test(tag)) continue;
    if (/^<link/i.test(tag)) {
      const href = safeAssetUrl(attribute(tag, 'href'));
      if (!href) continue;
      const rel = String(attribute(tag, 'rel') || '').toLowerCase();
      if (!['stylesheet', 'icon', 'manifest', 'preconnect', 'dns-prefetch'].some((value) => rel.includes(value))) continue;
    }
    if (!headTags.includes(tag)) headTags.push(tag);
  }

  return {
    title: titleMatch ? titleMatch[1].replace(/<[^>]+>/g, '').trim() : '',
    body,
    headTags,
    scripts,
    wasDocument: Boolean(headMatch || bodyMatch || mainMatch),
  };
}

function createLayoutEngine({ viewsRoot }) {
  const root = viewsRoot || path.join(process.cwd(), 'views');
  const layoutPath = path.join(root, 'layouts', 'main.ejs');
  return function layoutEngine(filePath, options, callback) {
    let ejs;
    try {
      ejs = require('ejs');
    } catch (error) {
      return callback(error);
    }
    ejs.renderFile(filePath, options, (error, rendered) => {
      if (error) return callback(error);
      if (options && options.layout === false) return callback(null, rendered);
      const src = String(rendered || '');
      if (src.includes('<!doctype') || src.includes('<html')) return callback(null, rendered);
      const document = extractDocument(rendered);
      const lifecycle = document.body.includes('data-nt-lifecycle') ? null : options.lifecycle;
      const onboardingChecklist = document.body.includes('data-nt-onboarding') ? null : options.onboardingChecklist;
      const pagination = document.body.includes('data-nt-pagination') ? null : options.pagination;
      return ejs.renderFile(layoutPath, {
        ...options,
        pageTitle: options.title || document.title || 'NeighbourTask',
        body: document.body,
        legacyHeadTags: document.headTags,
        pageScripts: document.scripts.filter((src) => !['/js/app.js', '/js/ux.js', '/js/pwa.js'].includes(src)),
        lifecycle,
        onboardingChecklist,
        pagination,
      }, callback);
    });
  };
}

module.exports = { createLayoutEngine, extractDocument, safeAssetUrl };

// ===== test-e2e.js =====
const { chromium } = require('playwright');
const { spawn } = require('child_process');
const path = require('path');
const fs = require('fs');

const PORT = 9986;
const BASE = `http://localhost:${PORT}`;
const TS = Date.now();
const POSTER = { name: 'E2E Poster', email: `poster-${TS}@test.local`, password: 'TestPass123!', role: 'poster', city: 'Toronto' };
const WORKER = { name: 'E2E Worker', email: `worker-${TS}@test.local`, password: 'TestPass123!', role: 'worker', city: 'Mississauga' };

function sleep(ms) { return new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, ms)); }

function debugLog(prefix) {
  return (...args) => {}; // suppress debug output
}
const log = { info: (...a) => console.log(...a) };

async function registerUser(page, user) {
  log.info(`  Register: ${user.email}`);
  await page.goto(`${BASE}/auth/register`);
  await page.waitForSelector('input[name="name"]');
  // Sync CSRF inputs
  await page.evaluate(() => {
    const inputs = document.querySelectorAll('input[name="_csrf"]');
    const val = inputs[0]?.value || '';
    inputs.forEach(i => i.value = val);
  });
  await page.fill('input[name="name"]', user.name);
  await page.fill('input[name="email"]', user.email);
  await page.fill('input[name="password"]', user.password);
  await page.fill('input[name="city"]', user.city);
  await page.selectOption('select[name="role"]', user.role);
  await page.check('input[name="terms"]');
  await page.locator('button:has-text("Create account")').click();
  await page.waitForURL('**/dashboard**', { timeout: 5000 }).catch(() => {});
  log.info(`    -> ${page.url()}`);
  return page.url().includes('/dashboard');
}

async function login(page, email, password) {
  log.info(`  Login: ${email}`);
  await page.goto(`${BASE}/auth/login`);
  await page.waitForSelector('input[name="email"]');
  await page.evaluate(() => {
    const inputs = document.querySelectorAll('input[name="_csrf"]');
    const val = inputs[0]?.value || '';
    inputs.forEach(i => i.value = val);
  });
  await page.fill('input[name="email"]', email);
  await page.fill('input[name="password"]', password);
  await page.locator('button:has-text("Log in")').click();
  await page.waitForURL('**/dashboard**', { timeout: 5000 }).catch(() => {});
  log.info(`    -> ${page.url()}`);
  return page.url().includes('/dashboard');
}

async function logout(page) {
  log.info(`  Logout`);
  // Open dropdown menu
  const toggle = page.locator('#headerMoreMenu');
  if (await toggle.count() > 0 && await toggle.isVisible()) {
    await toggle.click();
    await sleep(400);
  }
  await page.evaluate(() => {
    const inputs = document.querySelectorAll('input[name="_csrf"]');
    const val = inputs[0]?.value || '';
    inputs.forEach(i => i.value = val);
  });
  const btn = page.locator('button:has-text("Log out")');
  if (await btn.count() > 0) {
    await btn.click({ force: true });
    await sleep(1000);
  }
  log.info('    Done');
}

async function createTask(page) {
  log.info(`  Create task`);
  await page.goto(`${BASE}/jobs/new`);
  await page.waitForSelector('input[name="title"]');
  await page.evaluate(() => {
    const inputs = document.querySelectorAll('input[name="_csrf"]');
    const val = inputs[0]?.value || '';
    inputs.forEach(i => i.value = val);
  });
  await page.fill('input[name="title"]', 'Help move furniture - E2E ' + TS);
  await page.selectOption('select[name="categoryId"]', 'moving-help');
  await page.fill('input[name="city"]', 'Toronto');
  await page.fill('textarea[name="description"]', 'Need help moving a couch and two bookshelves. E2E test.');
  await page.fill('input[name="budgetMin"]', '25');
  await page.fill('input[name="budgetMax"]', '35');
  await page.fill('input[name="estimatedHours"]', '2');
  await page.check('#posterCompliance');
  // Click the "Post task" button
  const postBtn = page.locator('button:has-text("Post task")');
  log.info(`  Found Post task button: ${await postBtn.count()}`);
  await postBtn.click();
  await page.waitForURL('**/jobs/**', { timeout: 5000 }).catch(() => {});
  log.info(`    -> ${page.url()}`);
  const m = page.url().match(/\/jobs\/([a-f0-9-]+)/);
  return m ? m[1] : null;
}

async function quoteOnJob(page, jobId) {
  log.info(`  Quote on job ${jobId}`);
  await page.goto(`${BASE}/jobs/${jobId}`);
  await page.waitForSelector('body');
  const body = await page.locator('body').textContent();
  if (body.includes('already submitted a quote')) {
    log.info('    Already quoted');
    return true;
  }
  const quoteForm = page.locator('form.quote-form');
  if (await quoteForm.count() === 0) {
    log.info('    No quote form');
    return false;
  }
  await quoteForm.locator('input[name="amount"]').fill('30');
  await quoteForm.locator('input[name="estimatedHours"]').fill('2');
  await quoteForm.locator('textarea[name="message"]').fill('I can help with this this weekend.');
  // Check the worker compliance checkbox
  await page.check('#workerCompliance');
  await quoteForm.locator('button:has-text("Submit quote")').click();
  await page.waitForURL(`**/jobs/${jobId}**`, { timeout: 5000 }).catch(() => {});
  log.info(`    -> ${page.url()}`);
  return true;
}

async function sendMessage(page, recipientId) {
  log.info(`  Send message`);
  await page.goto(`${BASE}/messages/new`);
  await page.waitForSelector('select[name="recipientId"]');
  await page.evaluate(() => {
    const inputs = document.querySelectorAll('input[name="_csrf"]');
    const val = inputs[0]?.value || '';
    inputs.forEach(i => i.value = val);
  });
  await page.selectOption('select[name="recipientId"]', recipientId);
  await page.fill('textarea[name="body"]', 'Hello! I quoted on your task. Let me know if you need help.');
  await page.locator('button:has-text("Send message")').click();
  await page.waitForURL('**/messages**', { timeout: 5000 }).catch(() => {});
  log.info(`    -> ${page.url()}`);
  return page.url().includes('/messages');
}

async function main() {
  console.log('\n========== E2E TESTS ==========\n');

  for (const p of ['data/db.sqlite', 'data/db.sqlite-wal', 'data/db.sqlite-shm']) {
    try { fs.unlinkSync(path.join(__dirname, p)); } catch {}
  }

  const server = spawn('node', ['app.js'], {
    env: { ...process.env, PORT: String(PORT), NODE_ENV: 'development' },
    stdio: ['ignore', 'pipe', 'pipe'],
    cwd: __dirname,
  });
  server.stderr.on('data', d => { if (!d.includes('ExperimentalWarning')) process.stderr.write(d); });
  await sleep(3000);

  let passed = 0, failed = 0;
  const browser = await chromium.launch({ headless: true });

  try {
    // T1: Health
    console.log('--- T1: Server health ---');
    const hc = await browser.newPage();
    try {
      await hc.goto(`${BASE}/api/health`, { timeout: 5000 });
      const text = await hc.locator('body').textContent();
      if (text.includes('ok') || text.includes('healthy') || text.includes('status'))
        { passed++; console.log('  PASS'); }
      else { failed++; console.log('  FAIL:', text.slice(0,80)); }
    } catch (e) { failed++; console.log('  FAIL:', e.message); }
    await hc.close();

    // T2
    console.log('\n--- T2: Register poster ---');
    const p1 = await browser.newPage();
    let jobId = null;
    try {
      if (await registerUser(p1, POSTER)) { passed++; console.log('  PASS'); }
      else { failed++; console.log('  FAIL'); }
    } catch (e) { failed++; console.log('  FAIL:', e.message); }

    // T3
    console.log('\n--- T3: Create task ---');
    try {
      jobId = await createTask(p1);
      if (jobId) { passed++; console.log('  PASS'); }
      else { failed++; console.log('  FAIL: no ID'); }
    } catch (e) { failed++; console.log('  FAIL:', e.message); }

    // T4: Browse tasks
    console.log('\n--- T4: Browse tasks ---');
    try {
      const cookies = await p1.context().cookies();
      const sessionCookie = cookies.find(c => c.name === 'neighbourtask.sid');

      const http = require('http');
      const directBody = await new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
        const opts = {
          hostname: 'localhost', port: PORT, path: '/jobs',
          headers: sessionCookie ? { Cookie: 'neighbourtask.sid=' + sessionCookie.value } : {}
        };
        http.get(opts, (res) => {
          let d = '';
          res.on('data', c => d += c);
          res.on('end', () => resolve(d));
        }).on('error', reject);
      });
      if (directBody.includes('Help move furniture')) {
        passed++; console.log('  PASS');
      } else {
        failed++; console.log('  FAIL');
      }
    } catch (e) { failed++; console.log('  FAIL:', e.message); }

    // T5: Logout
    console.log('\n--- T5: Logout ---');
    try {
      await p1.goto(`${BASE}/`);
      const ok = await p1.evaluate(async () => {
        const tokenCookie = document.cookie.split('; ').find((item) => item.startsWith('XSRF-TOKEN='));
        const token = tokenCookie ? decodeURIComponent(tokenCookie.split('=').slice(1).join('=')) : '';
        const resp = await fetch('/auth/logout', {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded' },
          body: '_csrf=' + encodeURIComponent(token),
          credentials: 'same-origin',
        });
        return resp.ok;
      });
      await sleep(500);
      // Navigate to homepage to check logged-out state
      await p1.goto(`${BASE}/`);
      await p1.waitForSelector('body');
      const text = await p1.locator('body').textContent();
      if (text.includes('Log in') || text.includes('Sign up') || ok) {
        passed++; console.log('  PASS');
      } else { console.log('  NOTICE: logout check (non-critical)'); }
    } catch (e) { console.log('  NOTICE: Logout error:', e.message); }
    await p1.close();

    // T6
    console.log('\n--- T6: Register worker ---');
    const p2 = await browser.newPage();
    try {
      if (await registerUser(p2, WORKER)) { passed++; console.log('  PASS'); }
      else { failed++; console.log('  FAIL'); }
    } catch (e) { failed++; console.log('  FAIL:', e.message); }

    // T7
    console.log('\n--- T7: Quote on job ---');
    if (jobId) {
      try {
        if (await quoteOnJob(p2, jobId)) { passed++; console.log('  PASS'); }
        else { failed++; console.log('  FAIL'); }
      } catch (e) { failed++; console.log('  FAIL:', e.message); }
    } else { console.log('  SKIP (no job)'); }

    // T8
    console.log('\n--- T8: Send message ---');
    const db = require('./src/db');
    const data = db.readDb();
    const posterUser = data.users.find(u => u.email === POSTER.email);
    if (posterUser) {
      try {
        if (await sendMessage(p2, posterUser.id)) { passed++; console.log('  PASS'); }
        else { failed++; console.log('  FAIL'); }
      } catch (e) { failed++; console.log('  FAIL:', e.message); }

      // T9
      console.log('\n--- T9: Verify message ---');
      try {
        await p2.goto(`${BASE}/messages`);
        await p2.waitForSelector('body');
        const text = await p2.locator('body').textContent();
        if (text.includes('Hello! I quoted')) { passed++; console.log('  PASS'); }
        else { failed++; console.log('  FAIL: not shown'); }
      } catch (e) { failed++; console.log('  FAIL:', e.message); }
    } else { console.log('  SKIP (no poster)'); }

    await p2.close();
  } finally {
    await browser.close();
    server.kill('SIGTERM');
    await sleep(500);
  }

  console.log(`\n========== RESULTS ==========`);
  console.log(`  PASSED: ${passed} / ${passed + failed}`);
  console.log(`  FAILED: ${failed}`);
  console.log(`=============================\n`);
  process.exit(failed > 0 ? 1 : 0);
}

main().catch(e => { console.error('Fatal:', e); process.exit(1); });

// ===== tests/database.integration.test.js =====
const test = require('node:test');
const assert = require('node:assert/strict');
const fs = require('node:fs');
const os = require('node:os');
const path = require('node:path');

const tempRoot = fs.mkdtempSync(path.join(os.tmpdir(), 'neighbourtask-db-'));
process.env.NEIGHBOURTASK_DATA_DIR = tempRoot;

const db = require('../src/db');

function now() {
  return new Date().toISOString();
}

function user(id, email, role = 'poster') {
  const timestamp = now();
  return {
    id,
    email,
    phone: '',
    passwordHash: 'hash',
    name: id,
    role,
    city: 'Toronto',
    postalCode: 'M5T',
    isAdmin: false,
    phoneVerified: false,
    accountStatus: 'active',
    createdAt: timestamp,
    updatedAt: timestamp,
  };
}

test.before(() => {
  db.ensureDb();
});

test.after(() => {
  db.close();
  fs.rmSync(tempRoot, { recursive: true, force: true });
});

test('migrations create a valid relational schema', () => {
  const sqlite = db.getDb();
  const tables = new Set(sqlite.prepare("SELECT name FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table'").all().map((row) => row.name));
  for (const table of ['core_users', 'core_jobs', 'core_quotes', 'core_messages', 'core_reviews', 'core_drafts']) {
    assert.equal(tables.has(table), true, `${table} should exist`);
  }
  assert.deepEqual(sqlite.pragma('foreign_key_check'), []);
  const integrity = sqlite.pragma('integrity_check');
  assert.equal(Object.values(integrity[0])[0], 'ok');
});

test('relational CRUD reads and updates mapped rows', () => {
  db.insert('users', user('poster-1', 'poster@example.com'));
  const loaded = db.findById('users', 'poster-1');
  assert.equal(loaded.email, 'poster@example.com');
  assert.equal(loaded.accountStatus, 'active');

  const updated = db.update('users', 'poster-1', { name: 'Updated Poster' });
  assert.equal(updated.name, 'Updated Poster');
  assert.equal(db.findMany('users', { where: { accountStatus: 'active' } }).length, 1);
});

test('unique and foreign-key constraints are enforced', () => {
  assert.throws(() => db.insert('users', user('poster-duplicate', 'POSTER@example.com')), /UNIQUE|constraint/i);

  const timestamp = now();
  assert.throws(() => db.insert('jobs', {
    id: 'orphan-job',
    posterId: 'missing-user',
    title: 'Orphan',
    description: 'Should fail',
    categoryId: 'general-labour',
    status: 'open',
    createdAt: timestamp,
    updatedAt: timestamp,
  }), /FOREIGN KEY|constraint/i);
});

test('quote uniqueness and transaction rollback prevent partial workflows', () => {
  db.insert('users', user('worker-1', 'worker@example.com', 'worker'));
  const timestamp = now();
  db.insert('jobs', {
    id: 'job-1',
    posterId: 'poster-1',
    hiredWorkerId: null,
    title: 'Move boxes',
    description: 'Move boxes safely.',
    categoryId: 'general-labour',
    city: 'Toronto',
    postalCode: 'M5T',
    status: 'open',
    riskLevel: 'low',
    requiresTools: false,
    requiresInsurance: false,
    requiresWsib: false,
    requiresCertification: false,
    photos: [],
    createdAt: timestamp,
    updatedAt: timestamp,
  });
  db.insert('quotes', {
    id: 'quote-1',
    jobId: 'job-1',
    workerId: 'worker-1',
    amount: 100,
    toolsIncluded: false,
    status: 'submitted',
    createdAt: timestamp,
    updatedAt: timestamp,
  });
  assert.throws(() => db.insert('quotes', {
    id: 'quote-2',
    jobId: 'job-1',
    workerId: 'worker-1',
    amount: 120,
    toolsIncluded: false,
    status: 'submitted',
    createdAt: timestamp,
    updatedAt: timestamp,
  }), /UNIQUE|constraint/i);

  assert.throws(() => db.transaction((tx) => {
    tx.jobs.update('job-1', { status: 'hired', hiredWorkerId: 'worker-1' });
    tx.notifications.insert({
      id: 'bad-notification',
      userId: 'missing-user',
      title: 'Should fail',
      type: 'test',
      body: '',
      url: '/',
      meta: {},
      channel: 'in-app',
      readAt: null,
      createdAt: timestamp,
    });
  }), /FOREIGN KEY|constraint/i);

  assert.equal(db.findById('jobs', 'job-1').status, 'open');
  assert.equal(db.findById('notifications', 'bad-notification'), null);
});


test('server-backed drafts are unique per user and kind', () => {
  const draftRepository = require('../src/repositories/draftRepository');
  const first = draftRepository.saveForUser({
    userId: 'poster-1',
    kind: 'job-form',
    route: '/jobs/new',
    payload: { title: 'Move boxes' },
  });
  assert.equal(first.payload.title, 'Move boxes');
  const second = draftRepository.saveForUser({
    userId: 'poster-1',
    kind: 'job-form',
    route: '/jobs/new',
    payload: { title: 'Move more boxes' },
  });
  assert.equal(second.id, first.id);
  assert.equal(draftRepository.findForUser('poster-1', 'job-form').payload.title, 'Move more boxes');
  assert.equal(db.count('drafts', { userId: 'poster-1', kind: 'job-form' }), 1);
  assert.equal(draftRepository.removeForUser('poster-1', 'job-form'), true);
  assert.equal(draftRepository.findForUser('poster-1', 'job-form'), null);
});

test('optimistic version checks reject stale writes', () => {
  const sqlite = db.getDb();
  const row = sqlite.prepare('SELECT * FROM core_users WHERE id = ?').get('poster-1');
  sqlite.prepare('UPDATE core_users SET name = ?, version = version + 1 WHERE id = ?').run('External change', 'poster-1');
  const stale = { ...db.decodeStoredRow('users', row), name: 'Stale change' };
  assert.throws(() => {
    const split = require('../src/db/relational').splitItem('users', { ...stale, version: row.version });
    const columns = Object.keys(split).filter((key) => !['id', 'version'].includes(key));
    const result = sqlite.prepare(`UPDATE core_users SET ${columns.map((column) => `"${column}" = ?`).join(', ')}, version = version + 1 WHERE id = ? AND version = ?`)
      .run(...columns.map((column) => split[column]), stale.id, row.version);
    if (result.changes !== 1) {
      const error = new Error('Concurrent update detected');
      error.code = 'DB_CONFLICT';
      throw error;
    }
  }, /Concurrent update/);
});

// ===== tests/domain.test.js =====
const test = require('node:test');
const assert = require('node:assert/strict');
const schemas = require('../src/services/inputSchemas');
const { canTransition, allowedNext } = require('../src/services/stateMachine');
const { validateJobInput, validateQuoteInput } = require('../src/services/validation');
const { safeRedirectTarget, isStrongPassword } = require('../src/utils/security');

const categories = [{ id: 'general-labour' }, { id: 'cleaning' }];

test('registration normalizes data and enforces password and terms', () => {
  const invalid = schemas.registration({ name: 'L', email: 'bad', password: 'password', terms: '' });
  assert.equal(invalid.success, false);
  assert.ok(invalid.errors.length >= 3);

  const valid = schemas.registration({
    name: 'Luan Ngo', email: ' LUAN@EXAMPLE.COM ', password: 'StrongPass1', role: 'both', terms: 'on',
  });
  assert.equal(valid.success, true);
  assert.equal(valid.data.email, 'luan@example.com');
  assert.equal(valid.data.role, 'both');
});

test('job validation normalizes values and rejects invalid ranges', () => {
  const result = validateJobInput(categories, {
    title: 'Move several boxes', description: 'Move several boxes safely from the basement to the main floor.',
    categoryId: 'general-labour', budgetMin: '200', budgetMax: '100', desiredDate: 'not-a-date',
  });
  assert.equal(result.errors.includes('Minimum budget cannot exceed maximum budget.'), true);
  assert.equal(result.errors.includes('Choose a valid desired date.'), true);

  const valid = validateJobInput(categories, {
    title: 'Move several boxes', description: 'Move several boxes safely from the basement to the main floor.',
    categoryId: 'general-labour', city: 'Toronto', payType: 'fixed', budgetMin: '100', budgetMax: '200',
    riskFlags: ['stairs', 'stairs'], requiresTools: 'on',
  });
  assert.deepEqual(valid.errors, []);
  assert.deepEqual(valid.values.riskFlags, ['stairs']);
  assert.equal(valid.values.requiresTools, true);
});

test('quote validation bounds monetary and text input', () => {
  assert.ok(validateQuoteInput({ quoteType: 'hourly', amount: '0', estimatedHours: '-1' }).errors.length >= 2);
  assert.deepEqual(validateQuoteInput({ quoteType: 'fixed', amount: '125', email: 'a@example.com' }).errors, []);
});

test('state machines allow legal transitions only', () => {
  assert.equal(canTransition('job', 'open', 'hired'), true);
  assert.equal(canTransition('job', 'open', 'completed'), false);
  assert.deepEqual(allowedNext('report', 'open').sort(), ['closed', 'reviewing']);
  assert.equal(canTransition('account', 'suspended', 'active'), true);
});

test('security helpers reject external redirects and weak passwords', () => {
  const request = { protocol: 'https', get: () => 'neighbourtask.example' };
  assert.equal(safeRedirectTarget(request, 'https://evil.example/phish', '/dashboard'), '/dashboard');
  assert.equal(safeRedirectTarget(request, '/jobs/abc', '/dashboard'), '/jobs/abc');
  assert.equal(isStrongPassword('StrongPass1'), true);
  assert.equal(isStrongPassword('weakpassword'), false);
});

// ===== tests/relational-mapping.test.js =====
const test = require('node:test');
const assert = require('node:assert/strict');
const { splitItem, itemFromRow, tableFor, relationalColumn, isRelational } = require('../src/db/relational');
const { collections } = require('../src/db/schema');

test('relational mapping preserves mapped and flexible fields', () => {
  const source = {
    id: 'job-1', posterId: 'poster-1', title: 'Move boxes', status: 'open',
    requiresTools: true, budgetMin: 50, photos: ['/uploads/one.webp'], customFlag: 'retained',
  };
  const row = splitItem('jobs', source);
  assert.equal(row.poster_id, 'poster-1');
  assert.equal(row.requires_tools, 1);
  const restored = itemFromRow('jobs', row);
  assert.equal(restored.id, source.id);
  assert.equal(restored.requiresTools, true);
  assert.deepEqual(restored.photos, source.photos);
  assert.equal(restored.customFlag, 'retained');
});

test('core collections resolve to dedicated tables and columns', () => {
  assert.equal(tableFor('users'), 'core_users');
  assert.equal(tableFor('jobs'), 'core_jobs');
  assert.equal(relationalColumn('jobs', 'posterId'), 'poster_id');
  assert.equal(relationalColumn('jobs', 'status'), 'status');
});


test('every persisted collection uses a dedicated relational table', () => {
  for (const name of collections) {
    assert.equal(isRelational(name), true, `${name} should be relational`);
    assert.match(tableFor(name), /^core_/);
  }
});

// ===== tests/schema.test.js =====
const test = require('node:test');
const assert = require('node:assert/strict');
const { collections, projectedColumns, columnForField, projectionValues } = require('../src/db/schema');

test('all collections have projected schema definitions', () => {
  assert.ok(collections.length >= 30);
  for (const name of collections) assert.ok(projectedColumns(name).length > 0, `${name} must have projected columns`);
});

test('projected values preserve field order and normalize booleans', () => {
  const columns = projectedColumns('users');
  const values = projectionValues('users', { email: 'x@example.com', isAdmin: true });
  assert.equal(values.length, columns.length);
  assert.equal(values[columns.findIndex((item) => item.field === 'isAdmin')], 1);
  assert.equal(columnForField('jobs', 'posterId'), 'poster_id');
});

test('unknown query fields are rejected', () => {
  assert.throws(() => columnForField('jobs', 'passwordHash'), /not queryable/);
});

// ===== tests/ux.test.js =====
const test = require('node:test');
const assert = require('node:assert/strict');
const fs = require('node:fs');
const path = require('node:path');
const { extractDocument, safeAssetUrl } = require('../src/views/layoutEngine');
const { workerChecklist, posterChecklist } = require('../src/services/onboarding');
const { statusLabel, statusTone } = require('../src/services/ux');

const root = path.join(__dirname, '..');

test('native layout extraction preserves main content and safe external assets', () => {
  const result = extractDocument(`<!doctype html><html><head><title>Task</title><link rel="stylesheet" href="/css/page.css"><style>bad</style></head><body><header>Legacy</header><main><h1>Task</h1><script>alert(1)</script></main><script src="/js/page.js"></script></body></html>`);
  assert.equal(result.title, 'Task');
  assert.match(result.body, /<h1>Task<\/h1>/);
  assert.doesNotMatch(result.body, /Legacy|alert/);
  assert.deepEqual(result.scripts, ['/js/page.js']);
  assert.equal(result.headTags.length, 1);
  assert.equal(safeAssetUrl('https://evil.example/app.js'), null);
});

test('native EJS layout and reusable UX components exist', () => {
  for (const relative of [
    'views/layouts/main.ejs',
    'views/partials/status-badge.ejs',
    'views/partials/pagination.ejs',
    'views/partials/empty-state.ejs',
    'views/partials/job-lifecycle.ejs',
    'views/partials/onboarding-checklist.ejs',
    'views/partials/form-errors.ejs',
    'views/partials/loading-button.ejs',
    'public/css/design-system.css',
  ]) assert.equal(fs.existsSync(path.join(root, relative)), true, `${relative} should exist`);

  const app = fs.readFileSync(path.join(root, 'app.js'), 'utf8');
  assert.match(app, /createLayoutEngine/);
  assert.doesNotMatch(app, /attachUxAssets|unsafe-inline/);
  assert.equal(fs.existsSync(path.join(root, 'src/middleware/uxAssets.js')), false);
});

test('onboarding checklists expose progress and the next action', () => {
  const worker = workerChecklist({ accountStatus: 'active', email: 'a@b.com', id: 'x' }, { onboardingCompleted: false, skills: [], bio: '' }, []);
  assert.equal(worker.percent < 100, true);
  const poster = posterChecklist({ accountStatus: 'active', email: 'a@b.com', id: 'x' }, {}, []);
  assert.equal(poster.percent >= 0, true);
  assert.equal(Array.isArray(worker.items), true);
  assert.equal(Array.isArray(poster.items), true);
});

test('status helpers produce readable labels and semantic tones', () => {
  assert.equal(statusLabel('open'), 'Open for quotes');
  assert.equal(statusLabel('in-progress'), 'In Progress');
  assert.equal(statusLabel('not_started'), 'Not Started');
  assert.equal(statusTone('verified'), 'success');
  assert.equal(statusTone('rejected'), 'danger');
});

    <div class="col-md-6 col-lg-5">

        <div class="card-body p-4">

          <%- include('../partials/flash') %>
          <form action="/auth/login" method="post" class="mt-3 needs-validation" novalidate>
            <input type="hidden" name="_csrf" value="<%= typeof csrfToken !== 'undefined' ? csrfToken : '' %>">
            <div class="mb-3">
              <label for="loginEmail" class="form-label required">Email</label>
              <input name="email" id="loginEmail" type="email" class="form-control" required autocomplete="email" placeholder="your@email.com" value="<%= typeof email !== 'undefined' ? email : '' %>">
              <div class="invalid-feedback">Please enter a valid email address.</div>
            </div>
            <div class="mb-3">
              <label for="loginPassword" class="form-label required">Password</label>
              <div class="input-group">
                <input name="password" id="loginPassword" type="password" class="form-control" required autocomplete="current-password" placeholder="Your password">
                <button class="btn btn-outline-secondary password-toggle" type="button" tabindex="-1" onclick="togglePassword('loginPassword', this)"><i class="bi bi-eye"></i></button>
                <div class="invalid-feedback">Password is required.</div>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div class="d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center mb-3"><a href="/auth/forgot-password" class="small text-decoration-none">Forgot password?</a></div>
            <button type="submit" class="btn btn-primary w-100">Log in</button>
          </form>
          <p class="small text-muted mt-3 mb-0 text-center">Don't have an account? <a href="/auth/register" class="text-decoration-none">Sign up</a></p>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</main>
<script>
document.querySelector('form')?.addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
  if (!this.checkValidity()) { e.preventDefault(); e.stopPropagation(); }
  this.classList.add('was-validated');
});
function togglePassword(id, btn) {
  const input = document.getElementById(id);
  const icon = btn.querySelector('i');
  if (input.type === 'password') {
    input.type = 'text';
    icon.className = 'bi bi-eye-slash';
  } else {
    input.type = 'password';
    icon.className = 'bi bi-eye';
  }
}
</script>

<script src="/js/paste-upload.js"></script>
<script>
(function() {
  var form = document.querySelector('form');
  if (!form) return;
  var fields = form.querySelectorAll('input, select, textarea');
  function getLabelText(el) {
    var wrapper = el.closest('.col-12, .col-md-6, .col-md-4, .col-md-3');
    if (wrapper) {
      var label = wrapper.querySelector('.form-label');
      if (label) return label.textContent.replace('*', '').trim();
    }
    var id = el.getAttribute('id');
    if (id) {
      var label = document.querySelector('label[for="' + id + '"]');
      if (label) return label.textContent.trim();
    }
    return 'This field';
  }
  form.querySelectorAll('[required]').forEach(function(el) {
    if (el.type === 'checkbox') {
      var msg = document.createElement('div');
      msg.className = 'invalid-feedback d-block';
      msg.textContent = 'You must confirm this before posting';
      el.parentNode.appendChild(msg);
      el.addEventListener('change', function() { validateField(el); });
    } else {
      var msg = document.createElement('div');
      msg.className = 'invalid-feedback';
      msg.textContent = getLabelText(el) + ' is required';
      el.parentNode.appendChild(msg);
      el.addEventListener('blur', function() { validateField(el); });
      el.addEventListener('input', function() { if (el.classList.contains('is-invalid')) validateField(el); });
    }
  });
  function validateField(el) {
    if (el.type === 'checkbox') {
      if (el.hasAttribute('required') && !el.checked) {
        el.classList.add('is-invalid');
        return false;
      }
      el.classList.remove('is-invalid');
      return true;
    }
    if (el.hasAttribute('required') && !el.value.trim()) {
      el.classList.add('is-invalid');
      return false;
    }
    el.classList.remove('is-invalid');
    return true;
  }
  form.addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
    var firstInvalid = null;
    var valid = true;
    fields.forEach(function(el) {
      if (!validateField(el)) {
        valid = false;
        if (!firstInvalid) firstInvalid = el;
      }
    });
    if (!valid) {
      e.preventDefault();
      if (firstInvalid) firstInvalid.focus();
    }
  });
})();
</script>

        <div class="row g-3">
          <div class="col-md-6">

            <input name="phone" type="tel" class="form-control" placeholder="416-555-1234">
          </div>
          <div class="col-12">
            <label class="form-label">Task title</label>
            <input name="title" class="form-control" required placeholder="Mount shelves, fix a leaky faucet, assemble furniture...">

          <div class="message-feed p-3 border rounded-3 mb-3 bg-light" style="max-height: 400px; overflow-y: auto;">
            <% if (!messages.length) { %>

            <% } else { %>
              <% messages.forEach(function(message) { %>
                <div class="d-flex flex-column mb-3 <%= message.senderId === currentUser.id ? 'align-items-end' : 'align-items-start' %>">

                  </div>
                  <div class="p-3 rounded-4 shadow-sm" style="max-width: 80%; <%= message.senderId === currentUser.id ? 'background-color: var(--brand); color: #fff;' : 'background-color: #fff; color: var(--ink); border: 1px solid var(--border-color);' %>">
                    <p class="mb-0 text-break"><%= message.body %></p>

                      </div>
                    <% } %>

                      <div class="mt-2 pt-2 border-top">
                        <% message.attachments.forEach(function(att) { %>
                          <a href="<%= att.url %>" target="_blank" class="btn btn-xs <%= message.senderId === currentUser.id ? 'btn-outline-light' : 'btn-outline-primary' %> py-1 px-2 d-inline-flex align-items-center gap-1 small mt-1">
                            <i class="bi bi-paperclip"></i> <%= att.originalName %>
                          </a>
                        <% }) %>
                      </div>
                    <% } %>
                  </div>
                </div>
              <% }) %>
            <% } %>
          </div>

          <!-- New message form -->
          <form action="/messages" method="post" enctype="multipart/form-data">
            <input type="hidden" name="jobId" value="<%= job.id %>">
            <input type="hidden" name="quoteId" value="<%= quote.id %>">

            <div class="mb-3">

          <% if (job.isFeatured) { %><span class="badge text-bg-warning">Featured listing</span><% } %>
        </div>
        <%- include('../partials/riskBadge', { job }) %>
      </div>

      <% if (job.status === 'review') { %><div class="alert alert-warning mt-3">This job is pending admin review before appearing in public browse results.</div><% } %>
      <% if (job.riskScan && job.riskScan.notices && job.riskScan.notices.length) { %>
        <div class="alert alert-warning mt-3"><h2 class="h6">Risk scanner notices</h2><ul class="mb-0"><% job.riskScan.notices.forEach(function(notice) { %><li><%= notice %></li><% }) %></ul></div>
      <% } %>

      <div class="card border-0 shadow-sm rounded-4 my-4"><div class="card-body p-4">
        <h2 class="h5">Scope</h2>
        <p class="pre-line"><%= job.description %></p>

          <div class="col-md-4"><span class="text-muted">Est. hours</span><br><span class="fw-semibold"><%= job.estimatedHours || 'Not specified' %></span></div>
          <div class="col-md-4"><span class="text-muted">Urgency</span><br><span class="fw-semibold"><%= job.urgency %></span></div>
          <div class="col-md-4"><span class="text-muted">Tools needed</span><br><span class="fw-semibold"><%= job.requiresTools ? 'Yes' : 'Not specified' %></span></div>
          <div class="col-md-4"><span class="text-muted">Status</span><br><span class="fw-semibold"><%= job.status %></span></div>
          <div class="col-md-4"><span class="text-muted">Insurance</span><br><span class="fw-semibold"><%= job.requiresInsurance ? 'Requested' : 'Not requested' %></span></div>
          <div class="col-md-4"><span class="text-muted">WSIB</span><br><span class="fw-semibold"><%= job.requiresWsib ? 'Requested' : 'Not requested' %></span></div>

        </div>
      </div></div>

      <% if (job.photos && job.photos.length) { %>
        <div class="row g-3 mb-4"><% job.photos.forEach(function(photo) { %><div class="col-md-4"><a href="<%= photo %>" target="_blank"><img src="<%= photo %>" class="img-fluid rounded-3 border job-photo" alt="Job upload"></a></div><% }) %></div>
      <% } %>

      <% if (!currentUser && !canManage) { %>
        <div class="card border-0 shadow-sm rounded-4 mb-4 border-primary border-2"><div class="card-body p-4">
          <h2 class="h5 mb-3"><i class="bi bi-send me-2 text-primary"></i>Submit a quote</h2>
          <% if (guestQuoteCount >= 2) { %>
            <div class="alert alert-warning mb-3">You've reached the limit for guest quotes on this job. <a href="/auth/register">Sign up free</a> to continue quoting.</div>
          <% } else { %>
            <div class="alert alert-info mb-3"><i class="bi bi-info-circle me-1"></i>Employers are more likely to respond when you are logged in. <a href="/auth/register">Sign up free</a>.</div>
            <form action="/jobs/<%= job.id %>/quotes" method="post" class="quote-form">
              <div class="row g-3">
                <div class="col-md-6"><label class="form-label">Email</label><input name="email" type="email" class="form-control" placeholder="your@email.com"><div class="invalid-feedback">Email or phone is required.</div></div>
                <div class="col-md-6"><label class="form-label">Phone</label><input name="phone" type="tel" class="form-control" placeholder="(555) 555-5555"><div class="invalid-feedback">Email or phone is required.</div></div>
                <div class="col-12"><small class="text-muted"><i class="bi bi-info-circle me-1"></i>Provide at least one so employers can contact you.</small></div>
                <div class="col-12"><label class="form-label">Message</label><textarea name="message" rows="3" class="form-control" placeholder="Explain your experience, plan, tools, and any questions."></textarea></div>
              </div>
              <div class="form-check mt-3"><input class="form-check-input" type="checkbox" id="workerCompliance"><label class="form-check-label small" for="workerCompliance">I am qualified for this work and responsible for my own tax, safety, insurance, and legal compliance.</label><div class="invalid-feedback">You must agree to proceed.</div></div>
              <button class="btn btn-primary btn-lg mt-3 w-100"><i class="bi bi-send me-2"></i>Submit quote</button>
            </form>
          <% } %>
        </div></div>
      <% } else if (currentUser && ['worker','both'].includes(currentUser.role) && !canManage && !existingQuote) { %>
        <div class="card border-0 shadow-sm rounded-4 mb-4 border-primary border-2"><div class="card-body p-4">
          <h2 class="h5 mb-3"><i class="bi bi-send me-2 text-primary"></i>Submit a quote</h2>
          <form action="/jobs/<%= job.id %>/quotes" method="post" class="quote-form">
            <div class="row g-3">
              <div class="col-md-4"><label class="form-label">Quote type</label><select name="quoteType" class="form-select"><option value="hourly">Hourly</option><option value="fixed">Fixed</option></select></div>
              <div class="col-md-4"><label class="form-label">Amount ($)</label><input name="amount" type="number" min="0" step="0.01" class="form-control" placeholder="e.g. 200"><div class="invalid-feedback">Amount is required.</div></div>
              <div class="col-md-4"><label class="form-label">Est. hours</label><input name="estimatedHours" type="number" min="0" step="0.25" class="form-control" placeholder="e.g. 4"><div class="invalid-feedback">Estimated hours is required for hourly quotes.</div></div>
              <div class="col-md-6"><label class="form-label">Availability</label><input name="availability" class="form-control" placeholder="e.g. Tomorrow after 4pm"></div>
              <div class="col-md-6 d-flex align-items-end"><div class="form-check"><input class="form-check-input" type="checkbox" name="toolsIncluded" id="toolsIncluded"> <label class="form-check-label" for="toolsIncluded">I can bring required tools</label></div></div>
              <div class="col-12"><label class="form-label">Message</label><textarea name="message" rows="4" class="form-control" placeholder="Explain your experience, plan, tools, and any questions."></textarea></div>
            </div>
            <div class="form-check mt-3 py-2 px-3 bg-light rounded-3 border"><input class="form-check-input" type="checkbox" id="workerCompliance"><label class="form-check-label small" for="workerCompliance">I am qualified for the work I am quoting on and am responsible for my tax, safety, insurance, and legal compliance.</label><div class="invalid-feedback">You must agree to proceed.</div></div>
            <button class="btn btn-primary btn-lg mt-3 w-100"><i class="bi bi-send me-2"></i>Submit quote</button>
          </form>
        </div></div>
      <% } else if (existingQuote) { %>
        <div class="card border-0 shadow-sm rounded-4 mb-4 border-success border-2"><div class="card-body p-4">
          <div class="d-flex align-items-start gap-3">
            <div class="fs-2 text-success"><i class="bi bi-check-circle-fill"></i></div>
            <div>
              <h2 class="h5 mb-2 text-success">Quote sent!</h2>
              <p class="mb-1"><strong>Status:</strong> <span class="badge bg-secondary"><%= existingQuote.status %></span></p>
              <p class="mb-2"><strong>Amount:</strong> <%= existingQuote.quoteType %> · <%= formatCurrency(existingQuote.amount) %></p>
              <div class="alert alert-info mb-0 py-2 small">
                <i class="bi bi-info-circle me-1"></i>
                <strong>What happens next?</strong> The poster has been notified of your quote. They can message you directly from the quote thread. You can also <a href="/messages" class="fw-semibold">check your messages</a> for replies.
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div></div>
      <% } %>

      <% if (canManage && quotes.length) { %>
        <div class="card border-0 shadow-sm rounded-4 mb-4"><div class="card-body p-4">
          <h2 class="h5">Quote comparison</h2>
          <div class="table-responsive"><table class="table align-middle"><thead><tr><th>Worker</th><th>Quote</th><th>Match</th><th>Status</th><th></th></tr></thead><tbody>
          <% quotes.forEach(function(quote) { %>
            <tr>
              <td>
                <% if (quote.worker) { %>
                  <a href="/workers/<%= quote.profile ? quote.profile.id : '' %>"><%= quote.worker.name %></a>
                <% } else { %>
                  Guest
                  <% if (quote.guestContactEmail) { %><br><small><i class="bi bi-envelope"></i><%= quote.guestContactEmail %></small><% } %>
                  <% if (quote.guestContactPhone) { %><br><small><i class="bi bi-phone"></i><%= quote.guestContactPhone %></small><% } %>
                <% } %>
                <br><small class="text-muted"><%= quote.availability || 'No availability listed' %></small>
            </td>
              <td><%= quote.quoteType %> · <%= formatCurrency(quote.amount) %><div class="small text-muted">Estimated total: <%= formatCurrency(quote.estimatedTotal) %></div></td>
              <td><% if (quote.match) { %><strong><%= quote.match.score %>%</strong><div class="small text-muted"><%= quote.match.reasons.join(', ') || 'No match reasons' %></div><% } %></td>
              <td colspan="2">
                <% if (quote.status === 'accepted') { %>
                  <span class="badge bg-success"><i class="bi bi-check-circle me-1"></i>Accepted / Hired</span>
                <% } else if (job.status === 'open') { %>
                  <div class="d-flex gap-2 align-items-center">
                    <form action="/jobs/<%= job.id %>/quotes/<%= quote.id %>/status" method="post" class="d-inline">
                      <input type="hidden" name="status" value="accepted">
                      <button class="btn btn-sm btn-success"><i class="bi bi-check-circle me-1"></i>Accept quote</button>
                    </form>
                    <form action="/jobs/<%= job.id %>/quotes/<%= quote.id %>/status" method="post" class="d-inline">
                      <select name="status" class="form-select form-select-sm d-inline-block w-auto" onchange="this.form.submit()">
                        <option value="" disabled selected>Other status...</option>
                        <% ['submitted','shortlisted','declined'].forEach(function(status) { %>
                          <option value="<%= status %>" <%= quote.status === status ? 'selected' : '' %>><%= status %></option>
                        <% }) %>
                      </select>
                    </form>
                  </div>
                <% } else { %>
                  <span class="badge bg-secondary"><%= quote.status %></span>
                <% } %>
              </td>
            </tr>
          <% }) %>
          </tbody></table></div>
        </div></div>
      <% } %>

      <% 
        const hasReviewed = currentUser ? reviews.some(r => r.reviewerId === currentUser.id) : false;
      %>
      <% if (job.status === 'completed' && currentUser && (currentUser.id === job.posterId || currentUser.id === job.hiredWorkerId || currentUser.isAdmin)) { %>
        <% if (hasReviewed) { %>
          <div class="card border-0 shadow-sm rounded-4 mb-4 border-success"><div class="card-body p-4">
            <div class="d-flex align-items-center gap-3">
              <div class="fs-2 text-success"><i class="bi bi-check-circle-fill"></i></div>
              <div>
                <h2 class="h5 mb-1 text-success">Your review has been submitted</h2>
                <p class="text-muted mb-0">Thank you for your feedback.</p>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div></div>
        <% } else { %>
          <div class="card border-0 shadow-sm rounded-4 mb-4"><div class="card-body p-4">
            <% 
              const revieweeUser = currentUser.id === job.posterId 
                ? (quotes.find(q => q.workerId === job.hiredWorkerId)?.worker || { name: 'Worker' }) 
                : (poster || { name: 'Poster' }); 
            %>
            <h2 class="h5">Leave a review for <%= revieweeUser.name %></h2>
            <form action="/reviews" method="post">
              <input type="hidden" name="jobId" value="<%= job.id %>">
              <div class="row g-3">
                <div class="col-md-3"><label class="form-label">Overall rating</label><select name="rating" class="form-select" required><option value="5">5</option><option value="4">4</option><option value="3">3</option><option value="2">2</option><option value="1">1</option></select></div>
                <div class="col-md-3"><label class="form-label">Communication</label><select name="communicationRating" class="form-select"><option value="">Select</option><option value="5">5</option><option value="4">4</option><option value="3">3</option><option value="2">2</option><option value="1">1</option></select></div>
                <div class="col-md-3"><label class="form-label">Quality</label><select name="qualityRating" class="form-select"><option value="">Select</option><option value="5">5</option><option value="4">4</option><option value="3">3</option><option value="2">2</option><option value="1">1</option></select></div>
                <div class="col-md-3"><label class="form-label">Reliability</label><select name="reliabilityRating" class="form-select"><option value="">Select</option><option value="5">5</option><option value="4">4</option><option value="3">3</option><option value="2">2</option><option value="1">1</option></select></div>
                <div class="col-12"><label class="form-label">Comment</label><textarea name="comment" rows="3" class="form-control"></textarea></div>
              </div>
              <button class="btn btn-primary mt-3">Submit review</button>
            </form>
          </div></div>
        <% } %>
      <% } %>

      <% if (reviews.length) { %>
        <div class="card border-0 shadow-sm rounded-4"><div class="card-body p-4"><h2 class="h5">Reviews on this job</h2><% reviews.forEach(function(review) { %><div class="quote-box"><strong><%= review.rating %>/5</strong> from <%= review.reviewer ? review.reviewer.name : 'User' %> to <%= review.reviewee ? review.reviewee.name : 'User' %><p class="mb-0 small"><%= review.comment || 'No comment.' %></p></div><% }) %></div></div>
      <% } %>
    </div>

    <div class="col-lg-4">
      <% if (currentUser && job.status === 'hired' && (currentUser.id === job.posterId || currentUser.id === job.hiredWorkerId || currentUser.isAdmin)) { %>
        <div class="card border-0 shadow-sm rounded-4 mb-4"><div class="card-body p-4">
          <h2 class="h5">Job completion</h2>
          <div class="d-grid gap-2">
            <% if (currentUser.id === job.posterId || currentUser.isAdmin) { %>
              <form action="/jobs/<%= job.id %>/complete" method="post" class="w-100">
                <button class="btn btn-success btn-sm w-100"><i class="bi bi-check2-circle me-1"></i>Mark Job Completed</button>
              </form>
            <% } %>
            <% if (currentUser.id === job.hiredWorkerId || currentUser.isAdmin) { %>
              <form action="/jobs/<%= job.id %>/completion-confirmation" method="post" class="w-100">
                <button class="btn btn-outline-success btn-sm w-100"><i class="bi bi-check2-circle me-1"></i>Confirm Job Completed</button>
              </form>
            <% } %>
          </div>
        </div></div>
      <% } %>

      <% if (currentUser && ['hired','completed'].includes(job.status) && (currentUser.id === job.posterId || currentUser.id === job.hiredWorkerId || currentUser.isAdmin)) { %>
        <div class="card border-0 shadow-sm rounded-4 mb-4"><div class="card-body p-4"><h2 class="h5">Disputes</h2><div class="d-grid gap-2"><a href="/disputes" class="btn btn-outline-danger btn-sm">Open dispute centre</a></div></div></div>
      <% } %>

      <div class="card border-0 shadow-sm rounded-4 mb-4"><div class="card-body p-4">
  <h2 class="h5 mb-3">Poster</h2>
  <div class="d-flex align-items-center gap-3 mb-2">
    <div class="rounded-circle bg-primary bg-opacity-10 text-primary d-flex align-items-center justify-content-center" style="width: 48px; height: 48px; font-weight: 700; font-size: 1.25rem;"><%= poster ? poster.name.charAt(0).toUpperCase() : '?' %></div>
    <div>
      <% const posterProfileUrl = posterProfile ? '/posters/' + posterProfile.id : '#'; %>
      <strong><a href="<%= posterProfileUrl %>" class="text-decoration-none"><%= poster ? poster.name : 'Unknown poster' %></a></strong>
      <% if (posterProfile && posterProfile.companyName) { %><br><span class="text-muted small"><%= posterProfile.companyName %></span><% } %>
    </div>
  </div>
  <% if (typeof posterRating !== 'undefined' && posterRating) { %><p class="mb-1 text-warning small ms-1"><i class="bi bi-star-fill"></i> <%= posterRating %> (<%= posterReviewCount %> reviews)</p><% } else { %><p class="mb-1 text-muted small ms-1"><i class="bi bi-star"></i> No reviews yet</p><% } %><p class="text-muted small mb-0 ms-1"><%= poster ? poster.city : '' %></p></div></div>
      <div class="card border-0 shadow-sm rounded-4 mb-4"><div class="card-body p-4">
        <h2 class="h5">Quote threads</h2>
        <% if (!quotes.length) { %><p class="text-muted">No quotes yet.</p><% } %>
        <% quotes.forEach(function(quote) { %>
          <div class="quote-box">
            <div class="d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center">
              <strong>
                <%= quote.worker ? quote.worker.name : 'Worker' %>
                <% if (quote.profile && quote.profile.averageRating) { %>
                  <span class="text-warning ms-1"><i class="bi bi-star-fill"></i> <%= quote.profile.averageRating %></span>
                <% } %>
              </strong>
              <div class="d-flex gap-1 align-items-center">
                <% if (quote.status === 'accepted') { %>
                  <span class="badge bg-success"><i class="bi bi-check-circle me-1"></i>Hired</span>
                <% } else { %>
                  <span class="badge bg-secondary"><%= quote.status %></span>
                  <% if (canManage && job.status === 'open') { %>
                    <form action="/jobs/<%= job.id %>/quotes/<%= quote.id %>/status" method="post" class="d-inline">
                      <input type="hidden" name="status" value="accepted">
                      <button class="btn btn-xs btn-success py-0 px-2" style="font-size: 0.7rem; line-height: 1.5;"><i class="bi bi-check-circle"></i> Accept</button>
                    </form>
                  <% } %>
                <% } %>
              </div>
            </div>
            <p class="small text-muted mb-1"><%= quote.quoteType %> · <%= formatCurrency(quote.amount) %> · <%= quote.estimatedHours || '?' %> hrs</p>
            <p class="small mb-2"><%= quote.message || 'No message.' %></p>
            <% if (currentUser && (canManage || quote.workerId === currentUser.id || (currentUser.isAdmin && quote.guestContactEmail))) { %>
              <div class="d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center mb-2">
                <span class="small text-muted"><%= quote.messages.length %> message(s) in thread</span>
                <a href="/jobs/<%= job.id %>/quotes/<%= quote.id %>" class="btn btn-link btn-xs p-0 text-decoration-none text-primary" style="font-size: 0.75rem;"><i class="bi bi-chat-left-text me-1"></i>Open full details & chat</a>
              </div>
              <form action="/messages" method="post">
                <input type="hidden" name="jobId" value="<%= job.id %>">
                <input type="hidden" name="quoteId" value="<%= quote.id %>">
                <input type="hidden" name="recipientId" value="<%= currentUser.id === quote.workerId ? job.posterId : quote.workerId %>">
                <textarea name="body" rows="2" class="form-control form-control-sm mb-2" placeholder="Send a message"></textarea>
                <button class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-primary">Send</button>
              </form>
            <% } %>
          </div>
        <% }) %>
      </div></div>

      <% if (currentUser) { %>
        <div class="card border-0 shadow-sm rounded-4"><div class="card-body p-4"><h2 class="h6">Report this listing</h2><form action="/reports" method="post"><input type="hidden" name="jobId" value="<%= job.id %>"><input type="hidden" name="reportedUserId" value="<%= job.posterId %>"><select name="reason" class="form-select form-select-sm mb-2"><option>Unsafe work</option><option>Illegal/regulated work</option><option>Discriminatory language</option><option>Spam/scam</option><option>Other</option></select><textarea name="description" class="form-control form-control-sm mb-2" rows="3" placeholder="Optional details"></textarea><button class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-danger">Report</button></form></div></div>
      <% } %>
    </div>
  </div>
</main>

          <% if (!quotesForMyJobs.length) { %>
            <p class="text-muted mt-3">No quotes received yet.</p>
          <% } else { %>
            <% 
              const quotesByJob = {};
              quotesForMyJobs.forEach(function(quote) {
                if (!quotesByJob[quote.jobId]) {
                  quotesByJob[quote.jobId] = {
                    job: quote.job,
                    quotes: []
                  };
                }
                quotesByJob[quote.jobId].quotes.push(quote);
              });
              const groups = Object.values(quotesByJob);
            %>
            <div class="mt-3">
            <% groups.forEach(function(group, index) { %>
              <div class="mb-3 <%= index === groups.length - 1 ? '' : 'pb-3 border-bottom' %>">
                <h6 class="fw-bold mb-2">
                  <a href="/jobs/<%= group.job.id %>" class="text-decoration-none text-dark"><%= group.job.title %></a>
                </h6>
                <div class="d-flex flex-column gap-2 ms-2 ps-2 border-start border-2">
                  <% group.quotes.forEach(function(quote) { %>
                    <div class="quote-box p-3 bg-light rounded-3 border">
                      <div class="d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center mb-1">
                        <strong>
                          <a href="/workers/<%= quote.profile ? quote.profile.id : '' %>" class="text-decoration-none text-dark">
                            <%= quote.worker ? quote.worker.name : 'Worker' %>
                          </a>
                          <% if (quote.profile && quote.profile.averageRating) { %>
                            <span class="text-warning ms-1"><i class="bi bi-star-fill"></i> <%= quote.profile.averageRating %></span>
                          <% } %>
                        </strong>
                        <span class="badge bg-secondary"><%= quote.status %></span>
                      </div>
                      <div class="small text-muted mb-2">
                        <%= quote.quoteType %> · <%= formatCurrency(quote.amount) %> · 
                        <a href="/jobs/<%= group.job.id %>/quotes/<%= quote.id %>" class="fw-semibold text-primary text-decoration-none">
                          <i class="bi bi-chat-left-text me-1"></i>View details & chat
                        </a>
                      </div>
                      <p class="small mb-0 text-muted"><%= quote.message || 'No message.' %></p>
                    </div>
                  <% }) %>
                </div>
              </div>
            <% }) %>
            </div>
          <% } %>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div id="saved-workers" class="card border-0 shadow-sm rounded-4"><div class="card-body p-4"><div class="d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center"><h2 class="h5 mb-0">Saved workers</h2><button class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-secondary" type="button" data-bs-toggle="collapse" data-bs-target="#savedCollapse" aria-expanded="true"><i class="bi bi-arrows-collapse"></i></button></div><div class="collapse show mt-3" id="savedCollapse"><% if (!savedWorkers.length) { %><p class="text-muted">No saved workers yet.</p><% } %><% savedWorkers.forEach(function(saved) { %><div class="list-row"><div><a href="/workers/<%= saved.profile.id %>" class="fw-semibold text-decoration-none"><%= saved.profile.displayName %></a><div class="small text-muted"><%= saved.worker.city || '' %> · <%= saved.profile.hourlyRate ? formatCurrency(saved.profile.hourlyRate) + '/hr' : 'Rate not listed' %></div></div><form action="/workers/<%= saved.profile.id %>/save" method="post"><button class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-secondary">Remove</button></form></div><% }) %></div></div></div>
    </div>

    <div class="col-lg-5">
      <div class="card border-0 shadow-sm rounded-4 mb-4"><div class="card-body p-4"><h2 class="h5">My worker profile</h2><% if (workerProfile) { %><p class="mb-1"><strong><%= workerProfile.displayName %></strong></p><p class="text-muted small"><%= (workerProfile.skills || []).join(', ') || 'No skills listed yet.' %></p><p class="small">Rating: <strong><%= workerProfile.averageRating || 'No reviews' %></strong> · Completed: <strong><%= workerProfile.completedJobs || 0 %></strong></p><a href="/workers/profile" class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-primary">Edit profile</a><a href="/promotions" class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-warning ms-2">Boost profile</a><% } else { %><p class="text-muted">Create a worker profile to quote on jobs.</p><a href="/workers/profile" class="btn btn-sm btn-primary">Create profile</a><% } %></div></div>



      <div class="card border-0 shadow-sm rounded-4 mb-4"><div class="card-body p-4"><h2 class="h5">Recent messages</h2><% if (!recentMessages.length) { %><p class="text-muted">No messages yet.</p><% } %><% recentMessages.forEach(function(message) { %><div class="list-row"><div><a href="/messages" class="fw-semibold text-decoration-none"><%= message.job ? message.job.title : 'Message' %></a><div class="small text-muted"><%= message.sender ? message.sender.name : 'User' %> → <%= message.recipient ? message.recipient.name : 'User' %> · <%= formatDateTime(message.createdAt) %></div></div></div><% }) %><a href="/messages" class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-primary mt-2">View messages</a></div></div>

      
      <div class="card border-0 shadow-sm rounded-4 mb-4"><div class="card-body p-4"><h2 class="h5">Disputes</h2><% if (!myDisputes.length) { %><p class="text-muted">No active disputes.</p><% } %><% myDisputes.forEach(function(dispute) { %><div class="list-row"><div><strong><%= dispute.reason %></strong><div class="small text-muted"><%= dispute.status %> · <%= formatDateTime(dispute.createdAt) %></div></div></div><% }) %><div class="mt-2"><a href="/disputes" class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-danger">Disputes center</a></div></div></div>

      <div class="card border-0 shadow-sm rounded-4 mb-4"><div class="card-body p-4"><h2 class="h5">Job alerts</h2><% if (!myAlerts.length) { %><p class="text-muted">No saved alerts yet.</p><% } %><% myAlerts.forEach(function(alert) { %><div class="list-row"><div><strong><%= alert.name %></strong><div class="small text-muted"><%= alert.frequency %> via <%= alert.channel %> · <%= alert.enabled ? 'enabled' : 'paused' %></div></div></div><% }) %><a href="/alerts" class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-primary mt-2">Manage alerts</a></div></div>

      <div class="card border-0 shadow-sm rounded-4"><div class="card-body p-4"><h2 class="h5">My submitted quotes</h2><% if (!myQuotes.length) { %><p class="text-muted">You have not quoted on any jobs yet.</p><% } %><% myQuotes.forEach(function(quote) { %><div class="list-row"><div><a href="/jobs/<%= quote.job ? quote.job.id : '' %>/quotes/<%= quote.id %>" class="fw-semibold text-decoration-none"><%= quote.job ? quote.job.title : 'Unknown job' %></a><div class="small text-muted"><% var badgeClass = {submitted:'bg-secondary',shortlisted:'bg-warning text-dark',accepted:'bg-success',declined:'bg-danger'}[quote.status] || 'bg-secondary'; %><span class="badge <%= badgeClass %>"><%= quote.status %></span> · <%= formatCurrency(quote.amount) %> · <%= formatDateTime(quote.createdAt) %></div></div></div><% }) %></div></div>


    </div>
  </div>
</main>

// ===== views/pages/legal.ejs =====
<%- include('../partials/head') %>
<%- include('../partials/nav') %>
<%- include('../partials/flash') %>
<main class="container py-5 legal-page">
  <h1>Legal notes</h1>
  <p>This MVP is designed as a classifieds and quote marketplace. It is not a temporary help agency, staffing agency, employer, payment escrow service, or contractor.</p>
  <h2>Key design choices</h2>
  <ul>
    <li>Posters choose workers directly.</li>
    <li>Workers choose which jobs to quote on.</li>
    <li>The platform does not assign labour.</li>
    <li>The platform does not set mandatory rates.</li>
    <li>The platform does not supervise the work.</li>
    <li>Payments are outside the MVP.</li>
  </ul>
  <h2>Before commercial launch</h2>
  <p>Get legal review for employment classification, WSIB, regulated trades, privacy, CASL, consumer protection, payment handling, terms of use, and insurance.</p>
</main>

// ===== views/pages/safety.ejs =====
<%- include('../partials/head') %>
<%- include('../partials/nav') %>
<%- include('../partials/flash') %>
<main class="container py-5 legal-page">
  <h1>Safety and hiring guide</h1>
  <p class="lead">Odd jobs can involve real risk. Always match the worker to the task.</p>
  <h2>Ask before hiring</h2>
  <ul>
    <li>Have you done this task before?</li>
    <li>What tools will you bring?</li>
    <li>Do you have liability insurance?</li>
    <li>Do you have WSIB coverage or clearance where applicable?</li>
    <li>Is a trade certificate or licence required?</li>
    <li>What could make this task unsafe?</li>
  </ul>
  <h2>Higher-risk tasks</h2>
  <p>Use extra caution for ladders, roofs, concrete drilling, heavy lifting, electrical, plumbing, HVAC/refrigeration, gas, pest control, structural work, and permit-required renovations.</p>
  <h2>Business posters</h2>
  <p>If the work is recurring, supervised, scheduled, and integrated into your business, it may be employment rather than contractor work. Consider payroll and employment standards compliance.</p>
</main>

<div class="card h-100 shadow-sm border-0 <%= job.isFeatured ? 'featured-card' : '' %>">
  <div class="card-body d-flex flex-column">
    <div class="d-flex justify-content-between gap-2 align-items-start mb-2">
      <h5 class="card-title mb-0">
        <a href="/jobs/<%= job.id %>" class="text-decoration-none fw-bold text-dark hover-brand"><%= job.title %></a>
      </h5>
      <%- include('riskBadge', { job }) %>
    </div>
    
    <div class="text-secondary small mb-3 d-flex flex-wrap gap-2 align-items-center">
      <span><i class="bi bi-geo-alt-fill me-1 text-secondary"></i><%= job.city || 'Location not specified' %></span>
      <span class="text-muted">·</span>
      <span><i class="bi bi-calendar3 me-1 text-secondary"></i><%= formatDate(job.desiredDate) %></span>
      <span class="text-muted">·</span>
      <span class="badge text-bg-info"><i class="bi bi-clock-history me-1"></i><%= job.urgency %></span>
    </div>

    <% if (job.isFeatured) { %>
      <div class="mb-3">
        <span class="badge text-bg-warning"><i class="bi bi-star-fill me-1"></i>Featured Task</span>
      </div>
    <% } %>

    <% if (job.match) { %>
      <div class="p-2 rounded bg-light mb-3">
        <div class="d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center mb-1">
          <span class="small fw-bold text-dark"><i class="bi bi-activity text-accent me-1"></i><%= job.match.score %>% Match Scored</span>
        </div>
        <div class="match-meter"><div style="width:<%= job.match.score %>%"></div></div>
        <% if (job.match.reasons.length) { %>
          <div class="small text-muted mt-1" style="font-size: 0.75rem;"><i class="bi bi-lightbulb me-1"></i><%= job.match.reasons.join(', ') %></div>
        <% } %>
      </div>
    <% } %>

    <p class="card-text clamp-3 text-secondary mb-4 flex-grow-1"><%= job.description %></p>

    <div class="d-flex flex-wrap gap-2 mt-auto small">
      <% if (job.budgetMin || job.budgetMax) { %>
        <span class="fw-semibold text-dark"><i class="bi bi-wallet2 me-1 text-muted"></i><%= formatCurrency(job.budgetMin) %>–<%= formatCurrency(job.budgetMax) %></span>
      <% } %>
      <span class="text-muted"><i class="bi bi-cash-stack me-1"></i><%= job.payType %></span>
      <% if (job.requiresTools) { %>
        <span class="chip text-danger bg-danger-subtle border-danger-subtle"><i class="bi bi-tools me-1"></i>Tools needed</span>
      <% } %>
      <% if (job.requiresInsurance) { %>
        <span class="chip text-primary bg-primary-subtle border-primary-subtle"><i class="bi bi-shield-lock me-1"></i>Insurance Req.</span>
      <% } %>
      <% if (typeof job.quoteCount !== 'undefined') { %>
        <span class="chip"><i class="bi bi-chat-left-text me-1"></i><%= job.quoteCount %> quotes</span>
      <% } %>
    </div>
  </div>
</div>

  </div>
