  </div>

  <div class="row g-4">
    <div class="col-lg-5">
      <div class="card border-0 shadow-sm rounded-4">
        <div class="card-body p-4">
          <h2 class="h5">Create payment request</h2>
          <% if (!acceptedQuotes.length) { %>
            <p class="text-muted">You need an accepted quote before creating a payment request.</p>
          <% } else { %>
            <form action="/payments/requests" method="post" class="row g-3">
              <div class="col-12"><label class="form-label">Accepted quote</label><select name="quoteId" class="form-select" required><% acceptedQuotes.forEach(function(quote) { %><option value="<%= quote.id %>"><%= quote.job.title %> — <%= quote.worker ? quote.worker.name : 'Worker' %> — <%= formatCurrency(quote.estimatedTotal) %></option><% }) %></select></div>
              <div class="col-md-6"><label class="form-label">Amount</label><input name="amount" type="number" min="0" step="0.01" class="form-control" placeholder="Optional"></div>
              <div class="col-md-6"><label class="form-label">Mode</label><select name="processorMode" class="form-select"><% Object.keys(processorModes).forEach(function(mode) { %><option value="<%= mode %>"><%= processorModes[mode] %></option><% }) %></select></div>
              <div class="col-12"><label class="form-label">Reference / invoice number</label><input name="paymentReference" class="form-control"></div>
              <div class="col-12"><label class="form-label">Note</label><textarea name="note" rows="3" class="form-control"></textarea></div>
              <div class="col-12"><button class="btn btn-primary">Record request</button></div>
            </form>
          <% } %>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
    <div class="col-lg-7">
      <div class="card border-0 shadow-sm rounded-4">
        <div class="card-body p-4">
          <h2 class="h5">Payment records</h2>
          <% if (!payments.length) { %><p class="text-muted">No payment records yet.</p><% } %>
          <% payments.forEach(function(payment) { %>
            <div class="quote-box">
              <div class="d-flex justify-content-between gap-2"><div><strong><%= payment.job ? payment.job.title : 'Job' %></strong><div class="small text-muted"><%= payment.poster ? payment.poster.name : 'Poster' %> → <%= payment.worker ? payment.worker.name : 'Worker' %> · <%= formatDateTime(payment.createdAt) %></div></div><span class="badge bg-secondary"><%= payment.status %></span></div>
              <div class="small my-2">Amount: <strong><%= formatCurrency(payment.amount) %></strong> · Platform fee: <%= formatCurrency(payment.platformFee) %> · <%= payment.processorMode %></div>
              <p class="small text-muted mb-2"><%= payment.complianceNote %></p>
              <% if (currentUser && (currentUser.id === payment.posterId || currentUser.isAdmin)) { %>
                <form action="/payments/<%= payment.id %>/status" method="post" class="row g-2 align-items-end">
                  <div class="col-md-4"><label class="form-label small">Status</label><select name="status" class="form-select form-select-sm"><% ['requested','invoice-sent','authorized-demo','external-paid','released','cancelled','refunded-demo'].forEach(function(status) { %><option value="<%= status %>" <%= payment.status === status ? 'selected' : '' %>><%= status %></option><% }) %></select></div>
                  <div class="col-md-4"><label class="form-label small">Reference</label><input name="paymentReference" value="<%= payment.paymentReference || '' %>" class="form-control form-control-sm"></div>
                  <div class="col-md-4"><button class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-primary w-100">Update</button></div>
                </form>
              <% } %>
            </div>
          <% }) %>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</main>

        <label class="form-check"><input class="form-check-input" type="checkbox" name="vehicle" <%= filters.vehicle === 'on' ? 'checked' : '' %>> Vehicle</label>
        <label class="form-check"><input class="form-check-input" type="checkbox" name="insurance" value="verified" <%= filters.insurance === 'verified' ? 'checked' : '' %>> Insurance verified</label>
        <label class="form-check"><input class="form-check-input" type="checkbox" name="wsib" value="verified" <%= filters.wsib === 'verified' ? 'checked' : '' %>> WSIB verified</label>
        <label class="form-check"><input class="form-check-input" type="checkbox" name="trade" value="verified" <%= filters.trade === 'verified' ? 'checked' : '' %>> Trade verified</label>
      </div>
      <div class="col-md-4">
        <button class="btn btn-primary w-100"><i class="bi bi-funnel me-1"></i>Apply filters</button>
      </div>
    </div>
  </form>

  <div class="row g-3">
    <% if (!profiles.length) { %>
      <div class="col-12">
        <div class="empty-state">
          <i class="bi bi-people"></i>
          <h3>No workers match your filters</h3>
          <p class="text-muted">Try clearing some options or searching for different keywords.</p>
        </div>
      </div>
    <% } %>
    <% profiles.forEach(function(profile) { %>
      <div class="col-md-6 col-lg-4">
        <div class="card h-100 border-0 shadow-sm rounded-4 <%= profile.isBoosted ? 'featured-card' : '' %>">
          <div class="card-body d-flex flex-column">
            <div class="d-flex justify-content-between gap-2 align-items-start mb-2">
              <h2 class="h5 mb-0">
                <a class="text-decoration-none fw-bold text-dark hover-brand" href="/workers/<%= profile.id %>"><%= profile.displayName %></a>
              </h2>
              <% if (profile.isBoosted) { %>
                <span class="badge text-bg-warning"><i class="bi bi-lightning-fill me-1"></i>Boosted</span>
              <% } %>
            </div>
            
            <div class="text-muted small mb-3">
              <span><i class="bi bi-geo-alt-fill me-1"></i><%= profile.user ? profile.user.city : '' %></span>
              <span class="mx-1">·</span>
              <span class="fw-semibold text-success"><i class="bi bi-cash-stack me-1"></i><%= profile.hourlyRate ? formatCurrency(profile.hourlyRate) + '/hr' : 'Contact for quote' %></span>
              <span class="mx-1">·</span>
              <span><i class="bi bi-check-all me-1"></i><%= profile.completedJobs || 0 %> completed</span>
            </div>

            <% if (profile.averageRating) { %>
              <div class="mb-3 d-flex align-items-center gap-1 text-warning">
                <i class="bi bi-star-fill"></i>
                <span class="text-dark small fw-bold"><%= profile.averageRating %>/5</span>
                <span class="text-muted small">(<%= profile.reviews ? profile.reviews.length : 1 %> reviews)</span>
              </div>
            <% } %>

            <p class="clamp-3 text-secondary mb-4 flex-grow-1"><%= profile.bio || 'No bio yet.' %></p>
            
            <div class="d-flex flex-wrap gap-1 mb-3">
              <% (profile.skills || []).slice(0,5).forEach(function(skill) { %>
                <span class="chip"><i class="bi bi-tag-fill me-1" style="font-size: 0.7rem;"></i><%= skill %></span>
              <% }) %>
            </div>

            <div class="d-flex flex-wrap gap-1 mb-4">
              <% profile.badges.forEach(function(badge) { %>
                <span class="badge text-bg-<%= badge.tone %>"><%= badge.label %></span>
              <% }) %>
            </div>

            <% if (currentUser) { %>
              <div class="mt-auto">
                <form action="/workers/<%= profile.id %>/save" method="post" class="d-grid">
                  <button class="btn btn-sm <%= profile.saved ? 'btn-secondary' : 'btn-outline-primary' %>">
                    <% if (profile.saved) { %>
                      <i class="bi bi-bookmark-fill me-1"></i>Saved
                    <% } else { %>
                      <i class="bi bi-bookmark me-1"></i>Save worker
                    <% } %>
                  </button>
                </form>
              </div>
            <% } %>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    <% }) %>
  </div>
</main>
<%- include('../partials/footer') %>

      <% if (currentUser) { %><form action="/workers/<%= profile.id %>/save" method="post" class="mb-4"><button class="btn <%= saved ? 'btn-secondary' : 'btn-outline-primary' %>"><%= saved ? 'Saved worker' : 'Save worker' %></button></form><% } %>
      <div class="card border-0 shadow-sm rounded-4 mb-4"><div class="card-body p-4"><h2 class="h5">About</h2><p class="pre-line"><%= profile.bio || 'No bio yet.' %></p></div></div>

          <li>Insurance: <strong><%= profile.insuranceStatus %></strong></li>
          <li>WSIB: <strong><%= profile.wsibStatus %></strong></li>
